	Bin5-Sou3-Ki3	(4)
[1]	I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chhut Ai-kip8 toe7 i2-au7, te7-ji7 ni5, ji7-geh8 chhoe-it jit8, Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 Se-nai2 e5 khong3-ia2 ti7 hoe7-bou7-tiong hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  2). Lin2 tioh8 chiong I2-sek-liat8 choan5-hoe7 e5 chong2-sou3, chiau3 in e5 ke-khau2 chong-chok8, chiau3 lang5-mia5 e5 siau3-giah8, sng3 in ta-pou e5 jin5-teng.  3). KiN3-na7 I2-sek-liat8 tiong, tui3 ji7-chap8 he3 i2-chiuN7, oe7 chhut khi3 kau-chian3 e5, li2 kap A-lun5 tioh8 chiau3 in e5 kun-tui7 lai5 tiam2-sng3 i.  4). Mui2 chi-phai3-tiong, tioh8 u7 chit8-lang5, choe3 in e5 chok8-tiuN2 e5, lai5 pang-chan7 lin2.  5). Kap lin2 khia7 choe3-tui e5 lang5, in e5 mia5-ji7 ki3 ti7 e7-toe2.  Siok8 Liu5-pian7 e5, u7 Si7-tiu-jiN2 e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-siok.  6). Siok8 Se-bian7 e5, u7 Sou-li7-sa-tai7 e5 kiaN2 Si7-lou7-biat8.  7). Siok8 Iu5-tai7 e5, u7 A-bi2-na2-tat8 e5 kiaN2, Na2-sun7.  8). Siok8 I2-sat-ka e5, u7 Sou-ap e5 kiaN2, Na2-than2-giap8.  9). Siok8 Se-pou3-lun5 e5, u7 Hi-lun5 e5 kiaN2, I2-li7-ap.  10). Iok-sek e5 kiaN2-sun siok8 I2-hoat-lian5 e5, u7 A-bi2-hut e5 kiaN2, I2-li7-sa-ma2; siok8 Ma2-na2-se e5, u7 Pi2-tai7-siok e5 kiaN2, Ka-ma2-liat8.  11). Siok8 Pian7-nga2-bin2 e5, u7 Ki-to-ni5 e5 kiaN2, A-pi2-tan3.  12). Siok8 Tan3 e5, u7 A-bi2-sa-tai7 e5 kiaN2, A-hi-i2-sia7.  13). Siok8 A-siat e5, u7 Go5-lan5 e5 kiaN2, PhaN3-kiat.  14). Siok8 Ka-tek e5, u7 Tiu-jiN2 e5 kiaN2, I2-li7-nga2-sat.  15). Siok8 Na2-hut-tha-li2 e5, u7 I2-lam5 e5 kiaN2, A-hi-lah8.  16). Chiah-e5 long2 si7 tui3 hoe7-tiong keng2-soan2 e5, tak8-e5 choe3 in pun2 chi-phai3 e5 siu2-leng2, long2 si7 I2-sek-liat8 kun-tui7-tiong e5 thong2-leng2.  17). Mou5-se A-lun5 chiu7 chhoa7 hiah e5 siu7 ki3-mia5 e5 lang5; ti7 ji7-geh8 chhoe-it jit8, tiau3-chip8 hoe7-chiong3;  18). in chiu7 chiau3 in e5 jin5-teng, tui3 ji7-chap8 he3 i2-siong7, chiau3 in e5 mia5-giah8, chiau3 in e5 ke-khau2 chong-chok8, pai5-liat8 in e5 se3-he7.  19). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni beng7-leng7 Mou5-se, i chiu7 ti7 Se-nai2 e5 khong3-ia2 tiam2-sng3 in.
	20). I2-sek-liat8 e5 toa7-kiaN2, Liu5-pian7 kiaN2-sun e5 se3-he7, chiau3 in e5 ke-khau2, in e5 chong-chok8, chiau3 lang5-mia5 e5 siau3-giah8, chiau3 in e5 jin5-teng, tui3 ji7-chap8 he3 i2-chiuN7 e5 ta-pou--e5, oe7 chhut-khi3 kau-chian3--e5;  21). siok8 Liu5-pian7 e5 chi-phai3 ke3-sng3-e5, si3-ban7 lak8-chheng gou7-pah mia5.
	22). Se-bian7 kiaN2-sun e5 se3-he7, chiau3 in e5 ke-khau2, in e5 chong-chok8, ke3-sng3-e5, chiau3 lang5-mia5 e5 siau3-giah8, chiau3 in e5 jin5-teng, tui3 ji7-chap8 he3 i2-chiuN7 e5 ta-pou, oe7 chhut-khi3 kau-chian3-e5;  23). siok8 Se-bian7 e5 chi-phai3 ke3-sng3--e5, gou7-ban7 kau2-chheng saN-pah mia5.
	24). Ka-tek kiaN2-sun e5 se3-he7, chiau3 in e5 ke-khau2, in e5 chong-chok8, chiau3 lang5-mia5 e5 siau3-giah8, tui3 ji7-chap8 he3 i2-chiuN7, oe7 chhut-khi3 kau-chian3-e5;  25). siok8 Ka-tek e5 chi-phai3, ke3-sng3-e5, si3-ban7 gou7-chheng lak8-pah gou7-chap8 mia5.
	26). Iu5-tai7 kiaN2-sun e5 se3-he7, chiau3 in e5 ke-khau2, in e5 chong-chok8, chiau3 lang5-mia5 e5 siau3-giah8, tui3 ji7-chap8 he3 i2-chiuN7, oe7 chhut-khi3 kau-chian3-e5;  27). siok8 Iu5-tai7 e5 chi-phai3, ke3-sng3-e5, chhit-ban7 si3-chheng lak8-pah mia5.
	28). I2-sat-ka kiaN2-sun e5 se3-he7, chiau3 in e5 ke-khau2, in e5 chong-chok8, chiau3 lang5-mia5 e5 siau3-giah8, tui3 ji7-chap8 he3 i2-chiuN7 oe7 chhut-khi3 kau-chian3-e5;  29). siok8 I2-sat-ka e5 chi-phai3, ke3-sng3-e5, gou7-ban7 si3-chheng si3-pah mia5.
	30). Se-pou3-lun5 kiaN2-sun e5 se3-he7, chiau3 in e5 ke-khau2, in e5 chong-chok8, chiau3 lang5-mia5 e5 siau3-giah8, tui3 ji7-chap8 he3 i2-chiuN7, oe7 chhut-khi3 kau-chian3-e5;  31). siok8 Se-pou3-lun5 e5 chi-phai3, ke3-sng3-e5, gou7-ban7 chhit-chheng si3-pah mia5.
	32). Iok-sek e5 kiaN2-sun, siok8 I2-hoat-lian5 kiaN2-sun e5 se3-he7, chiau3 in e5 ke-khau2, in e5 chong-chok8, chiau3 lang5-mia5 e5 siau3-giah8, tui3 ji7-chap8 he3 i2-chiuN7, oe7 chhut-khi3 kau-chian3-e5;  33). siok8 I2-hoat-lian5 e5 chi-phai3, ke3-sng3-e5, si3-ban7 lian5 gou7-pah mia5.
	34). Ma2-na2-se kiaN2-sun e5 se3-he7, chiau3 in e5 ke-khau2, in e5 chong-chok8, chiau3 lang5-mia5 e5 siau3-giah8, tui3 ji7-chap8 he3 i2-chiuN7, oe7 chhut-khi3 kau-chian3-e5;  35). siok8 Ma2-na2-se e5 chi-phai3, ke3-sng3-e5, saN-ban7 nng7-chheng nng7-pah mia5.
	36). Pian7-nga2-bin2 kiaN2-sun e5 se3-he7, chiau3 in e5 ke-khau2, in e5 chong-chok8, chiau3 lang5-mia5 e5 siau3-giah8, tui3 ji7-chap8 he3 i2-chiuN7, oe7 chhut-khi3 kau-chian3-e5;  37). siok8 Pian7-nga2-bin2 e5 chi-phai3, ke3-sng3-e5, saN-ban7 gou7-chheng si3-pah mia5.
	38). Tan3 kiaN2-sun e5 se3-he7, chiau3 in e5 ke-khau2, in e5 chong-chok8, chiau3 lang5-mia5 e5 siau3-giah8, tui3 ji7-chap8 he3 i2-chiuN7, oe7 chhut-khi3 kau-chian3-e5;  39). siok8 Tan3 e5 chi-phai3, ke3-sng3-e5, lak8-ban7 nng7-chheng chhit-pah mia5.
	40). A-siat kiaN2-sun e5 se3-he7, chiau3 in e5 ke-khau2, in e5 chong-chok8, chiau3 lang5-mia5 e5 siau3-giah8, tui3 ji7-chap8 he3 i2-chiuN7, oe7 chhut-khi3 kau-chian3-e5;  41). siok8 A-siat e5 chi-phai3, ke3-sng3-e5, si3-ban7 chit8-chheng gou7-pah mia5.
	42). Na2-hut-tha-li7 kiaN2-sun e5 se3-he7, chiau3 in e5 ke-khau2, in e5 chong-chok8, chiau3 lang5-mia5 e5 siau3-giah8, tui3 ji7-chap8 he3 i2-chiuN7, oe7 chhut-khi3 kau-chian3-e5;  43). siok8 Na2-hut-tha-li7 e5 chi-phai3, ke3-sng3-e5, gou7-ban7 saN-chheng si3-pah mia5.
	44). Chiah-e5 long2 si7 ke3-sng3-e5, si7 Mou5-se A-lun5 kap I2-sek-liat8 chap8-ji7 e5 siu2-leng2 sou2-sng3--e5; in tak8-e5 tai7-piau2 in e5 chong-chok8.  45). An2-ni I2-sek-liat8 lang5 ke3-sng3--e5, chiau3 i e5 chong-chok8, tui3 ji7-chap8 he3 i2-chiuN7, kiN3-na7 I2-sek-liat8-tiong oe7 chhut-khi3 kau-chian3 e5 lang5;  46). chiu7-si7 it-chhe3 ke3-sng3--e5 kiong7 lak8-chap8-ban7 lian5 saN-chheng gou7-chap8 mia5.
	47). Tok8-tok8 Li7-bi7 lang5 chiau3 chou2-chong e5 chi-phai3, bo5 sng3 chai7-lai7.  48). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa bat hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  49). Tok8-tok8 Li7-bi7 chi-phai3 li2 m7-thang tiam2-sng3, ia7 m7-thang ti7 I2-sek-liat8-tiong sng3 in e5 chong2-giah8.  50). Tok8-tok8 tioh8 phai3 Li7-bi7 lang5 koan2-li2 cheng3-ku3 e5 hoe7-bou7, kap ki5-tiong it-chhe3 e5 khi3-ku7, kap it-chhe3 siok8 ti7 hi2 lai7-bin7-e5; in tioh8 kng hoe7-bou7 kap ki5-tiong it-chhe3 e5 khi3-ku7, ia7 tioh8 su-hau7 hoe7-bou7, ti7 i e5 si3-ui5 an-iaN5.  51). Hoe7-bou7 beh khi2-sin e5 si5, tioh8 Li7-bi7 lang5 thiah i; hoe7-bou7 beh tah e5 si5, tioh8 Li7-bi7 lang5 khia7 i; i2-goa7 e5 lang5 kun7-oa2 i, tek-khak tioh8 siu7 si2.  52). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tah pou3-piN5, kok chiau3 in e5 kun-tui7, kok kui in e5 pun2-iaN5, kok kui in e5 toa7-ki5.  53). Tok8-tok8 Li7-bi7 lang5 tioh8 ti7 cheng3-ku3 e5 hoe7-bou7 si3-ui5 an-iaN5, bian2-tit toa7 siu7-khi3 lim5-kau3 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 hoe7-chiong3; Li7-bi7 lang5 ia7 tioh8 siu2 cheng3-ku3 e5 hoe7-bou7 e5 chek-seng5.  54). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chiu7 an2-ni kiaN5; kiN3-na7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beng7-leng7 Mou5-se e5, in chiu7 chiau3 an2-ni kiaN5.

[2]	Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se A-lun5 kong2,  2). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tioh8 tak8-e5 tah i e5 pou3-piN5, ti7 ka-ki7 e5 toa7-ki5-e7, ti7 pun2-chok8 e5 ki5-ho7 hia, ui5-ui5 ng3 hoe7-bou7 chat-iaN5.  3). Ti7 tang--si3 ng3 jit8-chhut e5 sou2-chai7, chiau3 in e5 kun-tui7 chat-iaN5 e5, si7 tioh8 Iu5-tai7 iaN5 e5 toa7-ki5; u7 A-bi2-na2-tat8 e5 kiaN2 Na2-sun7 choe3 Iu5-tai7 lang5 e5 siu2-leng2.  4). I e5 kun-tui7, chiu7-si7 ke3-sng3 e5, kiong7 u7 chhit-ban7 si3-chheng lak8-pah mia5.  5). Oa2-kun7 i chat-iaN5-e5 si7 tioh8 I2-sat-ka e5 chi-phai3, u7 Sou-ap e5 kiaN2 Na2-than2-giap8 choe3 I2-sat-ka lang5 e5 siu2-leng2;  6). i e5 kun-tui7, chiu7-si7 ke3-sng3-e5, kiong7 u7 gou7-ban7 si3-chheng si3-pah mia5.  7). Koh u7 Se-pou3-lun5 e5 chi-phai3; Hi-lun5 e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-ap choe3 Se-pou3-lun5 lang5 e5 siu2-leng2;  8). i e5 kun-tui7, chiu7-si7 ke3-sng3-e5, kiong7 u7 gou7-ban7 chhit-chheng si3-pah mia5.  9). Siok8 Iu5-tai7 iaN5, chiau3 i e5 kun-tui7 long2-chong2 ke3-sng3-e5, kiong7 u7 chap8-poeh-ban7 lak8-chheng si3-pah mia5; in tioh8 choe3-thau5 khi2-sin.
	10). Ti7 lam5-peng5, chiau3 in e5 kun-tui7, si7 Liu5-pian7 iaN5 e5 toa7-ki5, u7 Si7-tiu-jiN2 e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-siok choe3 Liu5-pian7 lang5 e5 siu2-leng2;  11). i e5 kun-tui7, chiu7-si7 ke3-sng3-e5, kiong7 u7 si3-ban7 lak8-chheng gou7-pah mia5.  12). Oa2-kun7 i chat-iaN5-e5 si7 Se-bian7 e5 chi-phai3; Sou-li7-sa-tai7 e5 kiaN2 Si7-lou7-biat8 choe3 Se-bian7 lang5 e5 siu2-leng2;  13). i e5 kun-tui7, chiu7-si7 ke3-sng3-e5, kiong7 u7 gou7-ban7 kau2-chheng saN-pah mia5.  14). Koh u7 Ka-tek e5 chi-phai3; Tiu-jiN2 e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-nga2-sat choe3 Ka-tek lang5 e5 siu2-leng2;  15). i e5 kun-tui7, chiu7-si7 ke3-sng3-e5, kiong7 u7 si3-ban7 gou7-chheng lak8-pah gou7-chap8 mia5.  16). Siok8 Liu5-pian7 iaN5, chiau3 i e5 kun-tui7, long2-chong2 ke3-sng3-e5, kiong7 u7 chap8-gou7 ban7 chit8-chheng si3-pah gou7-chap8 mia5; in tioh8 choe3 te7-ji7 tui7 khi2-sin.
	17). Jian5-au7 hoe7-bou7 tioh8 khi2-sin, u7 Li7-bi7 lang5 e5 iaN5 ti7 chiah e5 iaN5 e5 tiong-kan, in an2-ni chat-iaN5, tioh8 chiau3 an2-ni khi2-sin, kok chiau3 i e5 toa7-ki5.
	18). Ti7 sai-peng5, chiau3 in e5 kun-tui7, si7 I2-hoat-lian5 iaN5 e5 toa7-ki5; A-bi2-hut e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-sa-ma2 choe3 I2-hoat-lian5 lang5 e5 siu2-leng2;  19). i e5 kun-tui7, chiu7-si7 ke3-sng3-e5, kiong7 u7 si3-ban7 lian5 gou7-pah mia5.  20). Oa2-kun7 i e5, si7 Ma2-na2-se e5 chi-phai3; Pi2-tai7-siok e5 kiaN2 Ka-ma2-liat8 choe3 Ma2-na2-se lang5 e5 siu2-leng2;  21). i e5 kun-tui7, chiu7-si7 ke3-sng3-e5, kiong7 u7 saN-ban7 nng7-chheng nng7-pah mia5.  22). Koh u7 Pian7-nga2-bin2 e5 chi-phai3; Ki-to-ni5 e5 kiaN2 A-pi2-tan3 choe3 Pian7-nga2-bin2 lang5 e5 siu2-leng2;  23). i e5 kun-tui7, chiu7-si7 ke3-sng3-e5, kiong7 u7 saN-ban7 gou7-chheng si3-pah mia5.  24). Siok8 I2-hoat-lian5 iaN5, chiau3 i e5 kun-tui7, long2-chong2 ke3-sng3-e5, kiong7 u7 chap8-ban7 lian5 poeh-chheng chit8-pah mia5; in tioh8 choe3 te7-saN tui7 khi2-sin.
	25). Ti7 pak-peng5 chiau3 in e5 kun-tui7, si7 Tan3 e5 iaN5 e5 toa7-ki5; A-bi2-sa-tai7 e5 kiaN2 A-hi-i2-sia7 choe3 Tan3 e5 lang5 e5 siu2-leng2;  26). i e5 kun-tui7, chiu7-si7 ke3-sng3-e5, kiong7 u7 lak8-ban7 nng7-chheng chhit-pah mia5.  27). Oa2-kun7 i chat-iaN5-e5 si7 A-siat e5 chi-phai3; Go5-lan5 e5 kiaN2 PhaN3-kiat choe3 A-siat lang5 e5 siu2-leng2;  28). i e5 kun-tui7, chiu7-si7 ke3-sng3-e5, kiong7 u7 si3-ban7 chit8-chheng gou7-pah mia5.  29). Koh u7 Na2-hut-tha-li7 e5 chi-phai3, I2-lam5 e5 kiaN2 A-hi-lah8 choe3 Na2-hut-tha-li7 lang5 e5 siu2-leng2;  30). i e5 kun-tui7, chiu7-si7 ke3-sng3-e5, kiong7 u7 gou7-ban7 saN-chheng si3-pah mia5.  31). Siok8 Tan3 e5 iaN5, long2-chong2 ke3-sng3-e5, kiong7 u7 chap8-gou7 ban7 chhit-chheng lak8-pah mia5; tioh8 kui in e5 toa7-ki5, choe3 lou7-be2 tui7 khi2-sin.
	32). Chiah-e5 si7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5, chiau3 in e5 chong-chok8 ke3-sng3-e5, chiau3 in e5 kun-tui7, ti7 chiah e5 iaN5-tiong long2-chong2 ke3-sng3-e5, kiong7 u7 lak8-chap8 ban7 lian5 saN-chheng gou7-pah gou7-chap8 mia5.  33). Tok8-tok8 Li7-bi7 lang5 bo5 sng3 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 lai7-bin7; si7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beng7-leng7 Mou2-se e5, I2-sek-liat8 lang5 an2-ni kiaN5;  34). tak8-lang5 chiau3 in e5 ke-khau2, in e5 chong-chok8, kui in e5 toa7-ki5, an2-ni chat-iaN5, an2-ni khi2-sin; long2-si7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beng7-leng7 Mou5-se e5 lai5 kiaN5.

[3]	Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 Se-nai2 soaN, tui3 Mou5-se kong2 e5 jit8, A-lun5 kap Mou5-se e5 se3-he7 chhin-chhiuN7 e7-toe2.  2). A-lun5 e5 kiaN2 e5 mia5 si7 chiah-e5; toa7-kiaN2 mia5-kio3 Na2-tap, koh u7 A-pi2-hou7, I2-li7-a-sat, I2-tha-ma2.  3). Che si7 A-lun5 e5 kiaN2 e5 mia5, long2 si7 siu7 boah-iu5 choe3 che3-si e5; bat ka7 in kiaN5 siat-lip8 e5 le2, lai5 tam-tng che3-si e5 chit-hun7.  4). Na2-tap A-pi2-hou7 ti7 Se-nai2 e5 khong3-ia2, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, hian3 pat8-ho7 he2 e5 si5, chiu7 si2 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5; in ia7 bo5 kiaN2-ji5.  I2-li7-a-sat I2-tha-ma2 ti7 in lau7-pe7 A-lun5 e5 bin7-cheng5, tam-tng che3-si e5 chit-hun7.
	5). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  6). Li2 hou7 Li7-bi7 e5 chi-phai3 kun7-cheng5 lai5, khia7 ti7 che3-si A-lun5 e5 bin7-cheng5, thang hok8-sai7 i.  7). In tioh8 siu2 sou2 hoan-hu3 A-lun5 e5, ia7 tioh8 ti7 hoe7-bou7-cheng5 siu2 sou2 hoan-hu3 hoe7-chiong3--e5, lai5 pan7-li2 hoe7-bou7 e5 su7.  8). In tioh8 kou3-siu2 hoe7-bou7 it-chhe3 e5 khi3-ku7; ia7 tioh8 siu2 sou2 hoan-hu3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5, lai5 pan7-li2 hoe7-bou7 e5 su7.  9). Li2 tioh8 chiong Li7-bi7 lang5 hou7 A-lun5 kap i hiah e5 kiaN2; in si7 tui3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 tiong-kan keng2--chhut-lai5 oan5-choan5 hou7 i e5.  10). Li2 tioh8 hun-phai3 A-lun5 kap i hiah e5 kiaN2, in ia7 tioh8 siu2 in che3-si e5 chit-jim7; kun7-oa2--lai5 e5 goa7-lang5, tek-khak hou7 i si2.
	11). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  12). KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 pun2-sin tui3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 tiong-kan chhu2 Li7-bi7 lang5, thoe3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 it-chhe3 thau5-thai e5 toa7-kiaN2; Li7-bi7 lang5 beh choe3 Goa2-e5.  13). In-ui7 it-chhe3 e5 toa7-kiaN2 long2 si7 Goa2-e5; Goa2 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 phah-si2 it-chhe3 e5 toa7-kiaN2 hit-jit8, chiu7 chiong I2-sek-liat8-tiong it-chhe3 e5 toa7-kiaN2, lang5 kap cheng-siN, long2 hun-piat in choe3-seng3, kui ti7 Goa2; in beh choe3 Goa2-e5; Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
	14). Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 Se-nai2 e5 khong3-ia2 hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  15). Li2 tioh8 chiau3 Li7-bi7 lang5 e5 chong-chok8, ke-khau2, tiam2-sng3 in; kiN3-na7 moa2-geh8 i2-chiuN7 e5 ta-pou gin2-na2, li2 long2 tioh8 tiam2-sng3.  16). Mou5-se chiu7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 lai5 tiam2-sng3 in, chiau3 i sou2 siu7 e5 beng7-leng7.  17). Li7-bi7 chiah e5 kiaN2 e5 mia5, chiu7-si7 Kek-sun7, Ko-hat, Bi2-lah8-li7.  18). Kek-sun7 e5 kiaN2, chiau3 in e5 ke, si7 Lip8-ni5, Si7-mui2.  19). Ko-hat e5 kiaN2, chiau3 in e5 ke, si7 Am3-lan5, I2-su-hap, Hi-pek-lun5, OU-siat.  20). Bi2-lah8-li7 e5 kiaN2, chiau3 in e5 ke, si7 Boat8-li7, Bou2-si7.  Chiah-e5 chiau3 in e5 chong-chok8 si7 Li7-bi7 lang5 e5 ke-khau2.
	21). Siok8 Kek-sun7 e5, u7 Lip8-ni5 chok8 e5 ke, Si7-mui2 chok8 e5 ke; chiah-e5 si7 Kek-sun7 chok8 e5 ke.  22). In ke3-sng3-e5, tui3 moa2-geh8 i2-chiuN7, chiau3 in hiah e5 ta-pou gin2-na2 e5 siau3-giah8, in sou2 ke3-sng3 e5 lang5, kiong7 u7 chhit-chheng gou7-pah mia5.  23). Kek-sun7 chok8 hiah e5 ke-khau2, tioh8 chat-iaN5 ti7 hoe7-bou7-au7 e5 sai--si3.  24). Lah8-i-lek8 e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-nga2-sat choe3 Kek-sun7 lang5 chong-chok8 e5 siu2-leng2.  25). Kek-sun7 e5 kiaN2-sun, ti7 hoe7-bou7-tiong sou2 tioh8 kou3-siu2--e5, chiu7-si7 hoe7-bou7, kap Pou3-piN5, kap i e5 koa3, kap hoe7-bou7 e5 mng5-li5;  26). iN7 e5 pou3-ui5, kap iN7 e5 mng5-li5, (iN7 chiu7-si7 ui5 hoe7-bou7 kap toaN5--e5), kap it-chhe3 sou2 eng7 e5 soh.
	27). Siok8 Ko-hat e5, u7 Am3-lan5 chok8 e5 ke, I2-su-hap chok8 e5 ke, Hi-pek-lun5 chok8 e5 ke, OU-siat chok8 e5 ke; chiah-e5 si7 Ko-hat chok8 e5 ke.  28). Chiau3 ta-pou-teng e5 siau3-giah8, tui3 moa2-geh8 i2-chiuN7, siu2 seng3-sou2 e5 chek-seng5-e5, kiong7 u7 poeh-chheng lak8-pah mia5.  29). Ko-hat kiaN2-sun hiah e5 ke tioh8 chat-iaN5 ti7 hoe7-bou7-piN e5 lam5--si3.  30). OU-siat e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-sat-hoan2 choe3 Ko-hat chong-chok8 ke-khau2 e5 siu2-leng2.  31). In sou2 tioh8 siu2--e5 si7 iok-kui7, toh, teng-tai5, hiah e5 toaN5, kap seng3-sou2 lai7 in sou2 eng7 e5 khi3-ku7, i2-kip8 mng5-li5, kap it-chhe3 choe3 lou7-eng7 e5 mih8.  32). Che3-si A-lun5 e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-a-sat choe3 Li7-bi7 lang5 chiah e5 siu2-leng2 e5 siu2-leng2, tioh8 kam3-chhat hiah e5 kou3-siu2 seng3-sou2 e5 lang5.
	33). Siok8 Bi2-lah8-li7 e5, u7 Boat8-li7 chok8 e5 ke, Bou2-si7 chok8 e5 ke, chiah-e5 si7 Bi2-lah8-li7 hiah e5 ke-khau2.  34). In ke3-sng3 e5, chiau3 in ta-pou-teng e5 siau3-giah8; tui3 moa2-geh8 i2-chiuN7 e5, kiong7 u7 lak8-chheng nng7-pah mia5.  35). A-pi2-hai7 e5 kiaN2 Sou-liat8 choe3 Bi2-lah8-li7 chong-chok8 chiah e5 ke e5 siu2-leng2; in tioh8 chat-iaN5 ti7 hoe7-bou7-piN e5 pak--si3.  36). Bi2-lah8-li7 e5 kiaN2-sun tiaN7-tioh8 e5 chit-hun7 si7 siu2 hoe7-bou7 e5 pan2, i e5 kong5, i e5 thiau7, i e5 cho7, kap it-chhe3 e5 khi3-ku7, it-chhe3 choe3 lou7-eng7 e5 mih8;  37). iN7 si3-ui5 e5 thiau7, i e5 cho7, i sou2 teng3 e5 teng kap soh.
	38). Ti7 hoe7-bou7-cheng5 e5 tang--si3, chiu7-si7 ti7 pou3-piN5-cheng5 ng3 jit8-chhut e5 sou2-chai7, chat-iaN5-e5 si7 Mou5-se A-lun5, kap i hiah e5 kiaN2; in siu2 seng3-sou2 e5 chek-seng5, chiu7-si7 thoe3 I2-sek-liat8 kiaN2-sun e5 chek-seng5; pat8-lang5 na7 kun7-oa2 tek-khak tioh8 hou7 i si2.  39). KiN3-na7 ke3-sng3 e5 Li7-bi7 lang5, chiu7-si7 Mou5-se A-lun5 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 beng7-leng7 sou2 sng3--e5, chiau3 in e5 ke, tui3 moa2-geh8 i2-chiuN7 e5 ta-pou-teng, kiong7 u7 nng7-ban7 nng7-chheng mia5.
	40). Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 tioh8 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 tiong-kan tiam2-sng3 tui3 moa2-geh8 i2-chiuN7 kiN3-na7 thau5-thai e5 ta-pou-teng, ki3 in e5 mia5-giah8.  41). Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, li2 tioh8 ka7 Goa2 chhu2 Li7-bi7 lang5, thoe3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 sou2 u7 e5 thau5-chiuN7-kiaN2; ia7 chhu2 Li7-bi7 lang5 e5 cheng-siN, thoe3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 sou2 u7 thau5-chui2-siN e5 cheng-siN.  42). Mou5-se chiu7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beng7-leng7 e5, sng3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 it-chhe3 e5 thau5-chiuN7-kiaN2.  43). Chiau3 lang5-mia5 e5 siau3-giah8, tui3 moa2-geh8 i2-chiuN7, kiN3-na7 thau5-chiuN7-siN e5 ta-pou-teng ke3-sng3 e5, kiong7 u7 nng7-ban7 nng7-chheng nng7-pah chhit-chap8-saN mia5.
	44). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  45). Li2 tioh8 chhu2 Li7-bi7 lang5 thoe3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 sou2 u7 thau5-chiuN7-siN e5, ia7 chhu2 Li7-bi7 lang5 e5 cheng-siN thoe3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 cheng-siN; chiu7 Li7-bi7 lang5 beh siok8 Goa2, Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  46). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tiong thau5-chiuN7 e5 ta-pou-teng, pi2 Li7-bi7 lang5 khak-choe7 nng7-pah chhit-chap8-saN e5, li2 beh ka7 i siok8--chhut-lai5;  47). chiu7 tioh8 chiau3 jin5-teng, chiau3 seng3-sou2 e5 sia3-khek-lek8, tak8-lang5 chhu2 gou7 sia3-khek-lek8, (chit8 sia3-khek-lek8 si7 ji7-chap8 kui3-lah8).  48). Hiah e5 chhut-giah8 e5 lang5 sou2 siok8-hoe5 e5 gun5, kau-tai3 A-lun5 kap i e5 kiaN2.  49). Mou5-se chiu7 tui3 hiah e5 siu7 Li7-bi7 lang5 sou2 siok8 chhut-giah8 e5 lang5, theh8 siok8-hoe5 e5 gun5.  50). Tui3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 thau5-chiuN7-siN-e5, sou2 theh8 e5 gun5, chiau3 seng3-sou2 e5 sia3-khek-lek8, u7 chit8-chheng saN-pah lak8-chap8-gou7 sia3-khek-lek8.  51). Mou5-se chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7, chiong chiah-e5 e5 siok8-hoe5 e5 gun5, kau-tai3 A-lun5 kap i e5 kiaN2, tu2-tu2 chhin-chhiuN7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beng7-leng7 Mou5-se e5.

[4]	Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se A-lun5 kong2,  2). Li2 tioh8 tui3 Li7-bi7 lang5 e5 tiong-kan sng3 Ko-hat kiaN2-sun e5 chong2-giah8, chiau3 in e5 ke-khau2, chong-chok8.  3). Tui3 saN-chap8 he3 i2-siong7, kau3 gou7-chap8 he3, kiN3-na7 jip8-lai5 tng-chit ti7 hoe7-bou7-lai7 choe3-kang-e5, long2 tioh8 sng3 i.  4). Ko-hat e5 kiaN2-sun ti7 hoe7-bou7 sou2 choe3 e5 kang, chiu7-si7 liau7-li2 chi3-seng3 e5 mih8, ki3 ti7 e7-toe2.  5). IaN5-poaN5 khi2-sin e5 si5, A-lun5 kap i e5 kiaN2 tioh8 jip8-khi3 thng3 jia-chah8 e5 tiuN3-li5, eng7 i lai5 jia-kham3 hoat-kui7.  6). Koh eng7 hai2-kau2-phe5 kham3 ti7 teng2-bin7, koh kham3 choan-choan lam5-sek e5 pou3; jian5-au7 chiah chhng i e5 kng3.  7). Koh eng7 lam5-sek e5 pou3 chhu ti7 pai5-liat8 piaN2 e5 toh; chiong chiah e5 poaN5, si5, oaN2, koan3-tian7 e5 poe, pai5 ti7 hi2 teng2-bin7; ti7-hia ia7 tioh8 u7 siong5-siong5 pai5-siat e5 piaN2.  8). Ti7 hi2 teng2-bin7 koh tioh8 ta3 chu-ang5-sek e5 pou3, koh eng7 hai2-kau2-phe5 choe3 koa3 lai5 kham3, chiah chhng i e5 kng3.  9). In tioh8 theh8 lam5-sek pou3 lai5 kham3 chio3-kng e5 teng-tai5, kap i e5 choaN2, i e5 chian2, i e5 poaN5, kap it-chhe3 choe3 i e5 lou7-eng7 toe2 iu5 e5 khi3-ku7.  10). Koh tioh8 chiong teng-tai5, kap i it-chhe3 e5 khi3-ku7, pau ti7 hai2-kau2-phe5 e5 koa3-lai7, he7 ti7 chha5-ke3-teng2.  11). Ti7 kim-toaN5-teng2 in tioh8 chhu lam5-sek e5 pou3, eng7 hai2-kau2-phe5 choe3 koa3 lai5 kham3, chiah chhng i e5 kng3.  12). Koh tioh8 theh8 sou2 eng7 lai5 hok8-sai7 e5 khi3-ku7, chiu7-si7 ti7 seng3-sou2 eng7 lai5 hok8-sai7-e5, pau ti7 lam5-sek e5 pou3, eng7 hai2-kau2-phe5 choe3 koa3 lai5 kham3, he7 ti7 chha5-ke3-teng2.  13). In tioh8 siu toaN5-teng2 e5 he2-hu, eng7 chi2-sek e5 pou3 chhu ti7 hi2 teng2-bin7.  14). Koh tioh8 eng7 in choe3-kang sou2 eng7 it-chhe3 e5 khi3-ku7, pai5 ti7 teng2-bin7; chiu7-si7 he2-tiaN2, bah-chhe, thuh-a2, poaN5, it-chhe3 siok8 ti7 toaN5 e5 khi3-ku7, koh eng7 hai2-kau2-phe5 choe3 koa3 lai5 ta3 i, chiah chhng i e5 kng3.  15). IaN5-poaN5 beh khi2-sin e5 si5, A-lun5 kap i e5 kiaN2 chiong seng3-sou2, kap seng3-sou2 it-chhe3 e5 khi3-ku7 kham3 beng5-pek8, jian5-au7 Ko-hat e5 kiaN2-sun tioh8 lai5 kng; tok8-tok8 m7-thang bong seng3 e5 mih8, bian2-tit in si2; hoe7-bou7-lai7 chiah e5 mih8-kiaN7 si7 Ko-hat e5 kiaN2-sun sou2 tioh8 kng e5.  16). Che3-si A-lun5 e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-a-sat sou2 tioh8 kou3-siu2 e5, si7 tiam2-teng e5 iu5, kap hiuN-liau7, kap siong5-siong5 hian3 e5 sou3-che3, kap boah e5 iu5; ia7 tioh8 kou3-siu2 choan5 hoe7-bou7 kap hit tiong-kan sou2 u7 e5, kap seng3-sou2, kap seng3-sou2 sou2-u7 e5 khi3-ku7.
	17). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se A-lun5 kong2,  18). Lin2 m7-thang chiong Ko-hat lang5 ke-chok8 e5 chi-phai3 tui3 Li7-bi7 lang5 e5 tiong-kan chian2-tu5--khi3;  19). in oa2-kun7 chi3-seng3 e5 mih8 e5 si5, lin2 tioh8 ka7 in an2-ni siat-hoat, hou7 in oe7 oah8, bian2-tit si2; A-lun5 kap i e5 kiaN2 tioh8 jip8-khi3, phai3 in tak8-lang5 sou2 tioh8 choe3, sou2 tioh8 kng e5.  20). Tok8-tok8 in tiap-a2-ku2 ia7 m7-thang jip8-khi3 khoaN3 seng3-sou2, bian2-tit in si2-bo5.
	21). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  22). Li2 tioh8 sng3 Kek-sun7 kiaN2-sun e5 chong2-giah8, chiau3 in e5 chong-chok8, ke-khau2;  23). tui3 saN-chap8 he3 i2-siong7 kau3 gou7-chap8 he3, kiN3-na7 jip8-lai5 tng-chit ti7 hoe7-bou7-lai7 choe3-kang-e5, long2 tioh8 sng3 i.  24). Kek-sun7 lang5 chiah e5 ke e5 kang-tiaN5, sou2 tioh8 pan7-li2, sou2 tioh8 kng e5, chiu7-si7 chiah-e5.  25). In tioh8 kng hoe7-bou7 hiah e5 tiuN3-pak, i2-kip8 hoe7-bou7, kap i e5 koa3, kap ti7 hi2 teng2-bin7 hai2-kau2-phe5 choe3 e5 koa3, kap hoe7-bou7 e5 mng5-li5;  26). iN7 e5 pou3-ui5; kap iN7-mng5 e5 mng5-li5, (iN7 chiu7-si7 ui5 hoe7-bou7 kap toaN5 e5,) soh-a2, kap sou2 eng7 e5 khi3-ku7, bo5-lun7 choe3 sim2-mih8 lou7-eng7 e5, in long2 tioh8 liau7-li2.  27). Kek-sun7 e5 kiaN2-sun ti7 in it-chhe3 sou2 kng e5 mih8, sou2 pan7 e5 su7, long2 tioh8 chiau3 A-lun5 kap i e5 kiaN2-sun sou2 beng7-leng7 e5 lai5 pan7, in sou2 eng-kai kng e5, lin2 tioh8 phai3 in kou3-siu2.  28). Che si7 Kek-sun7 kiaN2-sun chiah e5 ke, ti7 hoe7-bou7-lai7 sou2 choe3 e5 kang, in sou2 kou3-siu2 e5, tioh8 ti7 che3-si A-lun5 e5 kiaN2 I2-tha-ma2 e5 chhiu2-e7.
	29). Lun7-kau3 Bi2-lah8-li7 e5 kiaN2-sun, li2 tioh8 chiau3 in e5 ke-khau2, chong-chok8, ka7 in tiam2-sng3.  30). Tui3 saN-chap8 he3 i2-siong7, kau3 gou7-chap8 he3, kiN3-na7 jip8-lai5 tng-chit ti7 hoe7-bou7-lai7 choe3-kang-e5, long2 tioh8 sng3 i.  31). In sou2 tam-tng e5 chek-seng5, chiau3 hoe7-bou7 chiah e5 kang-tiaN5, chiu7-si7 hoe7-bou7 e5 pan2, kap i e5 kong5, i e5 thiau7, i e5 cho7,  32). iN7 si3-ui5 e5 thiau7, kap i e5 cho7; sou2 teng3 e5 teng, kap soh-a2, kap it-chhe3 sou2 eng7 e5 khi3-ku7; in tam-tng sou2 kng e5 khi3-ku7, lin2 tioh8 chiau3-mia5 chi2 tiaN7-tioh8.  33). Che si7 Bi2-lah8-li7 kiaN2-sun chiah e5 ke e5 kang, chiu7-si7 in ti7 hoe7-bou7-lai7 sou2 choe3 e5 kang, long2 ti7 che3-si A-lun5 e5 kiaN2 I2-tha-ma2 e5 chhiu2-e7.
	34). Mou5-se A-lun5 kap hoe7-chiong3 chiah e5 siu2-leng2, chiong Ko-hat e5 kiaN2-sun chiau3 in e5 chong-chok8, ke-khau2;  35). tui3 saN-chap8 he3 i2-siong7 kau3 gou7-chap8 he3, kiN3-na7 jip8-lai5 tng-chit ti7 hoe7-bou7-lai7 choe3-kang-e5, long2 ke3-sng3 i.  36). Chiau3 in e5 ke-khau2 ke3-sng3 e5, kiong7 u7 nng7-chheng chhit-pah gou7-chap8 mia5.  37). Che si7 Ko-hat chok8 chiah e5 ke ke3-sng3 e5, si7 kiN3-na7 ti7 hoe7-bou7-lai7 choe3-kang-e5, chiu7-si7 Mou5-se A-lun5, chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa thok Mou5-se sou2 beng7-leng7 tiam2-sng3 e5.
	38). Kek-sun7 e5 kiaN2-sun ke3-sng3-e5, chiau3 in e5 ke-khau2, chong-chok8,  39). tui3 saN-chap8 he3 i2-siong7 kau3 gou7-chap8 he3, kiN3-na7 jip8-lai5 tng-chit ti7 hoe7-bou7-lai7 choe3-kang-e5;  40). ki5-tiong ke3-sng3-e5, chiau3 in e5 ke-khau2, chong-chok8, kiong7 u7 nng7-chheng lak8-pah saN-chap8 mia5.  41). Che si7 Kek-sun7 kiaN2-sun chiah e5 ke ke3-sng3 e5; si7 kiN3-na7 ti7 hoe7-bou7-lai7 choe3-kang-e5, chiu7-si7 Mou5-se A-lun5 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beng7-leng7 lai5 tiam2-sng3 e5.
	42). Bi2-lah8-li7 kiaN2-sun chiah e5 ke, ke3-sng3-e5, chiau3 in e5 ke-khau2, in e5 chong-chok8,  43). tui3 saN-chap8 he3 i2-siong7 kau3 gou7-chap8 he3, kiN3-na7 jip8-lai5 tng-chit ti7 hoe7-bou7-lai7 choe3-kang-e5;  44). ki5-tiong ke3-sng3-e5, chiau3 in e5 ke-khau2, kiong7 u7 saN-chheng nng7-pah mia5.  45). Che si7 Bi2-lah8-li7 kiaN2-sun chiah e5 ke ke3-sng3-e5; chiu7-si7 Mou5-se A-lun5 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa thok Mou5-se sou2 beng7-leng7 tiam2-sng3 e5.  46). KiN3-na7 ke3-sng3 e5 Li7-bi7 lang5, chiu7-si7 Mou5-se, A-lun5, kap I2-sek-liat8 chiah e5 siu2-leng2, chiau3 in e5 ke-khau2, in e5 chong-chok8, sou2 tiam2-sng3-e5,  47). tui3 saN-chap8 he3 i2-siong7 kau3 gou7-chap8 he3, kiN3-na7 jip8-lai5 tng-chit ti7 hoe7-bou7-lai7 choe3 kng-mih8 e5 kang e5;  48). ki5-tiong ke3-sng3-e5 kiong7 u7 poeh-chheng gou7-pah poeh-chap8 mia5.  49). In hou7 Mou5-se tiam2-sng3, chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beng7-leng7-e5, tak8-lang5 chiau3 i sou2 pan7 e5 su7, chiau3 i sou2 kng e5 mih8; in an2-ni hou7 i tiam2-sng3, si7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beng7-leng7 Mou5-se e5.

[5]	Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  2). Li2 tioh8 beng7-leng7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 hou7 it-chhe3 hoan7-tioh8 thai2-ko-e5, hoan7-tioh8 ha7-siau-cheng3 e5, kap in-ui7 si2-si bo5 chheng-khi3 e5, long2 chhut-khi3 iaN5-goa7.  3). Bo5-lun7 lam5-lu2 lin2 long2 tioh8 hou7 in chhut-khi3, chiu7-si7 chhut-khi3 kau3 iaN5-goa7, bian2-tit phah la5-sam5 in e5 iaN5-poaN5, in-ui7 Goa2 khia7-khi2 ti7 in e5 tiong-kan.  4). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chiau3 an2-ni kiaN5, hou7 in chhut-khi3 iaN5-goa7; Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni hoan-hu3 Mou5-se, I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chiu7 an2-ni kiaN5.
	5). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  6). Li2 tioh8 ka7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kong2, Bo5-lun7 lam5-lu2, na7 kiaN5 lang5 sou2 kiaN5 e5 choe7, ti3-kau3 kan-hoan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, hit-lang5 chiu7 u7 choe7.  7). In tioh8 jin7 in sou2 hoan7 e5 choe7, chiau3 siau3-giah8 pe5 i, leng7-goa7 ke gou7-hun7 e5 chit8-hun7, kui hou7 i sou2 khek-khui e5 lang5.  8). Chong2-si7 hit-lang5 na7 bo5 chhin-lang5 thang nia2-siu7 in-ui7 choe7 sou2 pe5 e5, chiu7 hit-e5 in-ui7 choe7 sou2 pe5 e5, tioh8 heng5 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, lai5 kui che3-si; lun7 hit-chiah siok8-choe7 e5 iuN5-kang2, chiu7-si7 eng7 lai5 ka7 i siok8-choe7--e5, si7 sng3 chai7-goa7.  9). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 it-chhe3 e5 seng3-mih8 tiong, sou2 hong7 hou7 che3-si e5 ku2-che3, long2 tioh8 kui hou7 che3-si.  10). KiN3-na7 lang5 sou2 hun-piat choe3-seng3 e5 mih8, tioh8 kui hou7 che3-si; lang5 eng7 sim2-mih8 hou7 che3-si e5, long2 tioh8 kui ti7 i.
	11). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  12). Li2 tioh8 hoan-hu3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tui3 i kong2, Lang5 e5 bou2 na7 kiaN5-chho3 tek-choe7 i e5 tiong7-hu,  13). u7 lang5 kap i kiaN5-im5, su7-cheng5 pi3-bit8, i e5 tiong7-hu m7-chai, ia7 bo5 lou7-chhut; chong2-si7 i siu7 phah la5-sam5, ia7 bo5 lang5 choe3 kan-cheng3, ia7 bo5 liah8-tioh8 i,  14). i e5 tiong7-hu siN-khi2 giau5-gi5 e5 sim, giau5-gi5 i e5 bou2, i e5 bou2 si7 phah la5-sam5; a2-si7 i e5 tiong7-hu siN-khi2 giau5-gi5 e5 sim, giau5-gi5 i e5 bou2, i e5 bou2 peng7-bo5 siu7 phah la5-sam5,  15). hit e5 lang5 tioh8 chhoa7 i e5 bou2 kau3 che3-si hia, ia7 ui7-tioh8 i toa3 toa7-beh8 e5 mi7-hun2 i-hoat chap8-hun7-chit8 choe3 i e5 le2-mih8, m7-thang thin5 iu5, ia7 m7-thang chham ju2-hiuN, in-ui7 che si7 giau5-gi5 e5 sou3-che3, si7 ki3-tit e5 sou3-che3, hou7 lang5 oe7 ki3-tit choe7.  16). Che3-si tioh8 hou7 hit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 kun7-oa2 lai5, hou7 i khia7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5.  17). Che3-si tioh8 eng7 seng3 e5 chui2 toe2 ti7 hui5 e5 khi3-ku7-lai7, koh tui3 hoe7-bou7 e5 thou5-kha theh8 chit8 tiam2-a2 thou5-hun2, he7 ti7 chui2-tiong.  18). Che3-si tioh8 hou7 hit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 khia7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, phah-soaN3 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 thau5-mng5, chiong ki3-tit e5 sou3-che3, chiu7-si7 giau5-gi5 e5 sou3-che3, he7 ti7 i e5 chhiu2-tiong; che3-si e5 chhiu2 tioh8 theh8 ti3-kau3 chiu3-chou2 e5 khou2-chui2.  19). Che3-si tioh8 kah hu7-jin5-lang5 chiu3-choa7, tui3 i kong2, Na7 bo5 lang5 kap li2 kiaN5-im5, li2 i2-keng siu7 tiong7-hu e5 iok-sok, bo5 kiaN5-chho3 ti3-kau3 phah la5-sam5, li2 chiu7 kap chit e5 chiu3-chou2 e5 khou2-chui2 bo5 kan-siap8.  20). Chong2-si7 li2 i2-keng siu7 tiong7-hu e5 iok-sok, na7 u7 kiaN5-chho3 siu7 phah la5-sam5, ti7 li2 e5 tiong7-hu i2-goa7 u7 lang5 kap li2 kiaN5-im5;  21). che3-si chiu7 hou7 hu7-jin5-lang5 eng7 chiu3-chou2 lai5 chiu3-choa7, che3-si tui3 hu7-jin5-lang5 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 li2 e5 toa7-thui2 noa7, pak-tou2 tiong3 e5 si5, goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 li2 ti7 li2 e5 peh-siN3-tiong chiaN5-choe3 chiu3-chou2, chiaN5-choe3 chiu7-choa7 e5 oe7-piN3.  22). Koh chit-e5 ti3-kau3 chiu3-chou2 e5 chui2 beh jip8 li2 e5 tng5-a2-lai7, hou7 li2 e5 pak-tou2 tiong3, toa7-thui2 noa7; hu7-jin5-lang5 tioh8 in3 kong2, A-beng7, A-beng7.  23). Che3-si tioh8 sia2 chiah e5 chiu3-chou2 e5 oe7 ti7 chheh--nih, eng7 hiah e5 ji7 boah8-jip8 ti7 khou2-chui2--nih.  24). Koh hou7 hu7-jin5-lang5 lim chit e5 chiu3-chou2 e5 khou2-chui2, ti3-kau3 chiu3-chou2 e5 chui2 jip8 i e5 lai7-bin7 chiaN5-choe3 khou2.  25). Che3-si tioh8 tui3 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 chhiu2 theh8 giau5-gi5 e5 sou3-che3, io5 hit e5 sou3-che3 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, toa3 kau3 toaN5-cheng5.  26). Che3-si tioh8 tui3 sou3-che3-tiong theh8-chhut chit8-pe2 choe3 ki3-liam7, sio ti7 toaN5-teng2, jian5-au7 hou7 hu7-jin5-lang5 lim chit e5 chui2.  27). I2-keng hou7 hu7-jin5-lang5 lim hit e5 chui2, i na7 siu7 bak la5-sam5 tek-choe7 i e5 tiong7-hu, chit-e5 ti3-kau3 chiu3-chou2 e5 chui2 beh jip8 i e5 lai7-bin7, chiaN5-choe3 khou2; i e5 pak-tou2 chiu7 beh kou2-tiong3, toa7-thui2 chiu7 beh noa7, hit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 chiu7 beh ti7 i e5 peh-siN3-tiong chiaN5-choe3 chiu3-chou2 e5 oe7-piN3.  28). Na7 hu7-jin5-lang5 bo5 siu7 phah la5-sam5, sit8-chai7 si7 chheng-khi3, chiu7 bian2 siu7 chai-e7, koh beh hoai5-in7.  29). Bou2 i2-keng siu7 tiong7-hu e5 iok-sok, na7 u7 kiaN5-chho3 bak-tioh8 la5-sam5, che chiu7-si7 giau5-gi5 e5 le7.  30). A2-si7 lang5 siN-chhut giau5-gi5 e5 sim, lai5 giau5-gi5 i e5 bou2, chiu7 tioh8 hou7 i e5 bou2 khia7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, che3-si chiu7 tioh8 ka7 i chin7 chit e5 le7 lai5 kiaN5.  31). An2-ni ta-pou-lang5 chiu7 bo5 choe7, hu7-jin5-lang5 tioh8 tam-tng ka-ki7 e5 choe7.

[6]	Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou2-se kong2,  2). Li2 tioh8 hoan-hu3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 ka7 in kong2, Bo5-lun7 lam5-lu2 he7 tek8-piat8 e5 goan7, chiu7-si7 Na2-se3-jiN2 lang5 e5 goan7, ka-ki7 hun-piat kui hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa,  3). i chiu7 tioh8 li7-khui chiu2 kap kau7-chiu2, ia7 m7-thang lim sim2-mih8 chiu2 e5 chhou3, kap kau7-chiu2 e5 chhou3, m7-thang lim sim2-mih8 phu5-to5 e5 chiap, ia7 m7-thang chiah8 chhiN e5 phu5-to5, kap ta e5 phu5-to5.  4). Ti7 it-chhe3 ka-ki7 hun-piat e5 jit8, kiN3-na7 phu5-to5-chhiu7 sou2 chhut e5, tui3 hut8 kau3 phe5, long2 m7-thang chiah8.  5). Ti7 i he7-goan7 ka-ki7 hun-piat hiah e5 jit8, m7-thang hou7 thi3-thau5-to kau3 i e5 thau5-khak; kau3 i ka-ki7 hun-piat kui hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 jit8 moa2, i tioh8 choe3-seng3, chhut-chai7 i e5 thau5-mng5 hoat-tng5.  6). Ti7 i ka-ki7 hun-piat kui Ia5-ho5-hoa hiah e5 jit8, m7-thang oa2-kun7 sin-si.  7). I e5 lau7-pe7, a2-si7 lau7-bu2, a2-si7 hiaN-ti7, a2-si7 chi2-be7, si2 e5 si5, i m7-thang ui7-tioh8 in hou7 ka-ki7 bo5 chheng-khi3; in-ui7 i ka-ki7 hun-piat kui Siong7-te3 e5 pin5-ku3 si7 ti7 i e5 thau5-khak.  8). Ti7 i ka-ki7 hun-piat hiah e5 jit8, i si7 kui ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3-seng3.  9). Na7 ti7 i e5 sin-piN hut-jian5 u7 lang5 si2, ti3-kau3 bak-tioh8 i ka-ki7 hun-piat e5 thau5-khak, chiu7 i tioh8 ti7 ka-ki7 chheng-khi3 e5 jit8 thi3-thau5, chiu7-si7 ti7 te7-chhit jit8 thi3 i.  10). Te7-poeh jit8 i tioh8 eng7 nng7 chiah ka-chui, a2-si7 nng7 chiah chiN2-a2-kiaN2, toa3 kau3 hoe7-bou7 mng5-khau2, kau-tai3 che3-si.  11). Che3-si tioh8 hian3 chit8-chiah choe3 siok8-choe7-che3, chit8-chiah choe3 sio-che3, ka7 i siok8-choe7; in-ui7 i tui3 sin-si lai5 u7 choe7; koh tioh8 ti7 hit-jit8 hou7 i e5 thau5-khak choe3-seng3.  12). I tioh8 koh eng7 i hun-piat e5 jit8, hun-piat lai5 kui Ia5-ho5-hoa, koh tioh8 khan chit8 chiah be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2, choe3 pou2-ke3-sit e5 che3; chong2-si7 i2-cheng5 e5 jit8 bo5 sng3-siau3, in-ui7 i e5 ka-ki7 hun-piat i2-keng siu7 bak la5-sam5.
	13). Na2-se3-jiN2 lang5 ka-ki7 hun-piat e5 jit8 i2-keng moa2, hit e5 le7 chiu7-si7 an2-ni; lang5 tioh8 chhoa7 i kau3 hoe7-bou7 e5 mng5-khau2.  14). I tioh8 chiong i e5 le2-mih8 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, chiu7-si7 chit8-chiah bo5 ha5-chhu5 be7-moa2-ni5 e5 mi5-iuN5-kang2-a2, choe3 sio-che3, chit8-chiah bo5 ha5-chhu5 be7-moa2-ni5 e5 mi5-iuN5-bu2-a2, choe3 siok8-choe7 che3, kap chit8-chiah bo5 ha5-chhu5 e5 mi5-iuN5-kang2, choe3 sia7-un e5 che3;  15). koh chit8-kheng e5 bo5-kaN3 piaN2, chiu7-si7 tiau-ho5 iu5 iu3-mi7-hun2 choe3 e5 piaN2, kap boah-iu5 bo5-kaN3 e5 poh8-piaN2, i2-kip8 i e5 sou3-che3, kap koan3-tian7 e5 che3.  16). Che3-si tioh8 theh8 chiah-e5 kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, lai5 hian3 hit-lang5 e5 siok8-choe7 che3, kap sio-che3.  17). I ia7 tioh8 chiong hit chiah iuN5-kang2, kap hit kheng bo5-kaN3 piaN2, hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 sia7-un e5 che3; che3-si ia7 tioh8 soa3 hian3 i e5 sou3-che3 kap koan3-tian7.  18). Na2-se3-jiN2 lang5 tioh8 ti7 hoe7-bou7 mng5-khau2 thi3 ka-ki7 hun-piat e5 thau5, chiong ka-ki7 hun-piat e5 thau5-mng5, he7 ti7 sia7-un-che3 e7-bin7 e5 he2-teng2.  19). Na2-se3-jiN2 lang5 thi3 i ka-ki7 hun-piat e5 thau5-mng5 liau2-au7, che3-si chiu7 tioh8 chhu2 i2-keng chu2 e5 iuN5-kang2 chit8 ki cheng5-thui2, koh tui kheng-a2-lai7 theh8 chit8 e5 bo5-kaN3 piaN2, kap chit8 e5 bo5-kaN3 e5 poh8-piaN2, long2 he7 ti7 i e5 chhiu2.  20). Che3-si tioh8 theh8 chiah-e5 choe3 io5-che3, io5 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5; che kap sou2 io5 e5 heng, sou2 ku2 e5 thui2, long2 choe3 seng3-mih8, kui hou7 che3-si; jian5-au7 Na2-se3-jiN2 lang5 thang lim-chiu2.  21). He7-goan7 e5 Na2-se3-jiN2 lang5 ui7-tioh8 i hun-piat ka-ki7 sou2 hian3 e5 le2-mih8, kap i i2-goa7 sou2 oe7 tit-tioh8-e5, hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, chiu7-si7 chit e5 le7; i an2-ni he7-goan7 chiu7 tioh8 chiau3 hun-piat ka-ki7 e5 le7 lai5 kiaN5.
	22). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  23). Li2 tioh8 hoan-hu3 A-lun5 kap i e5 kiaN2 kong2, Lin2 tioh8 an2-ni ka7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chiok-hok, tui3 in kong2:
24). Goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa su3-hok li2, po2-hou7 li2;
25). Goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 I e5 bin7 e5 kng chio3 li2, si-un hou7 li2;
26). Goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa hoaN-hi2 e5 bin7 khoaN3 li2, siuN2-su3 li2 peng5-an.
27). An2-ni in beh eng7 Goa2 e5 mia5 he7 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 teng2-bin7; Goa2 ia7 beh su3-hok in.

[7]	Mou5-se khi2 hoe7-bou7 beng5-pek8, chiu7 eng7 iu5 boah i, hun-piat i choe3-seng3; koh chiong ki5-tiong e5 khi3-ku7 kap toaN5, kap i e5 khi3-ku7, long2 boah i, hun-piat i choe3-seng3.  2). Hit-jit8 I2-sek-liat8 e5 cheng3 siu2-leng2, chiu7-si7 in tak8-chok8 e5 chok8-tiuN2, long2 lai5 hong7-hian3; in chiu7-si7 tak8 chi-phai3 e5 siu2-leng2, koan2-li2 hiah e5 ke3-sng3 e5 lang5;  3). in eng7 in e5 le2-mih8 sang3 kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, chiu7-si7 lak8 tiuN u7 jia-kham3 e5 chhia, kap chap8-ji7 chiah gu5-kang2; mui2 nng7 e5 siu2-leng2 chit8 tiuN chhia, tak8 e5 siu2-leng2 chit8 chiah gu5; in chiong chiah-e5 long2 toa3 kau3 hoe7-bou7-cheng5.  4). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  5). Li2 tioh8 tui3 in siu--lai5, thang choe3 hoe7-bou7 e5 lou7-eng7; chiong hiah-e5 hou7 Li7-bi7 lang5, kok chiau3 in sou2 choe3 e5 kang.  6). Tui3 an2-ni Mou5-se chiu7 siu chhia kap gu5, kau hou7 Li7-bi7 lang5.  7). Chiong nng7 tiuN chhia, si3 chiah gu5, kau Kek-sun7 e5 kiaN2-sun, chiau3 in sou2 choe3 e5 kang.  8). Koh chiong si3-tiuN chhia, poeh chiah gu5, kau hou7 Bi2-lah8-li7 e5 kiaN2-sun, chiau3 in sou2 choe3 e5 kang; in long2 hou7 che3-si A-lun5 e5 kiaN2 I2-tha-ma2 koan2-hat.  9). Chong2-si7 chhia kap gu5 bo5 kau hou7 Ko-hat e5 kiaN2-sun, in-ui7 seng3-sou2 e5 kang siok8 ti7 in, eng7 keng-thau5 kng i.  10). Eng7 iu5 boah toaN5 e5 jit8, siu2-leng2 long2 lai5, kiaN5 hian3-toaN5 e5 le2; tak8 e5 siu2-leng2 chiu7 ti7 toaN5-cheng5 hian3 in e5 le2-mih8.  11). Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 Mou5-se kong2, Chiah e5 siu2-leng2 hian3 le2-mih8, tak8-e5 tioh8 ti7 i e5 jit8 lai5 hian3, lai5 kiaN5 hian3-toaN5 e5 le2.
	12). Thau5-chit8 jit8 hian3 le2-mih8 e5, si7 siok8 Iu5-tai7 e5 chi-phai3 A-bi2-na2-tat8 e5 kiaN2 Na2-sun7;  13). i e5 le2-mih8 si7 chit8 e5 gun5-poaN5, tang7 chit8-pah saN-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, chit8 e5 gun5-oaN2, tang7 chhit-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, long2 si7 chiau3 seng3-sou2 e5 sia3-khek-lek8, chi2 nng7-e5 toe2-moa2 tiau-ho5 iu5 e5 iu3-mi7-hun2, choe3 sou3-che3;  14). chit8 e5 kim-au, tang7 chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, toe2 hiuN moa2-moa2;  15). chit8 chiah gu5-kang2-a2, chit8 chiah mi5-iuN5-kang2, chit8 chiah be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2, choe3 sio-che3;  16). chit8 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2 choe3 siok8-choe7-che3;  17). nng7 chiah gu5-kang2, gou7 chiah mi5-iuN5 kang2, gou7 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2, gou7 chiah be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2, choe3 sia7-un che3; chiah-e5 si7 A-bi2-na2-tat8 e5 kiaN2 Na2-sun7 e5 le2-mih8.
	18). Te7-ji7 jit8 I2-sat-ka e5 siu2-leng2, Sou-ap e5 kiaN2 Na2-than2-giap8, lai5 hian3;  19). i sou2 hian3 e5 le2-mih8, chiu7-si7 chit8 e5 gun5-poaN5, tang7 chit8-pah saN-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, chit8 e5 gun5-oaN2, tang7 chhit-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, long2 si7 chiau3 seng3-sou2 e5 sia3-khek-lek8, chi2 nng7-e5 toe2-moa2 tiau-ho5 iu5 e5 iu3-mi7-hun2, choe3 sou3-che3;  20). chit8 e5 kim-au, tang7 chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, toe2 hiuN moa2-moa2;  21). chit8 chiah gu5-kang2-a2, chit8 chiah mi5-iuN5-kang2, chit8 chiah be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2, choe3 sio-che3;  22). chit8 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2, choe3 siok8-choe7-che3;  23). nng7 chiah gu5-kang2, gou7 chiah mi5-iuN5 kang2, gou7 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2, gou7 chiah be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2, choe3 sia7-un che3; chiah-e5 si7 Sou2-ap e5 kiaN2 Na2-than2-giap8 e5 le2-mih8.
	24). Te7-saN jit8 si7 Se-pou3-lun5 kiaN2-sun e5 siu2-leng2, Hi-lun5 e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-ap;  25). i e5 le2-mih8 chiu7-si7 chit8 e5 gun5-poaN5, tang7 chit8-pah saN-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, chit8 e5 gun5-oaN2, tang7 chhit-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, long2 si7 chiau3 seng3-sou2 e5 sia3-khek-lek8, chi2 nng7-e5 toe2-moa2 tiau-ho5 iu5 e5 iu3-mi7-hun2, choe3 sou3-che3;  26). chit8 e5 kim-au, tang7 chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, toe2 hiuN moa2-moa2;  27). chit8 chiah gu5-kang2-a2, chit8 chiah mi5-iuN5-kang2, chit8 chiah be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2, choe3 sio-che3;  28). chit8 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2 choe3 siok8-choe7-che3;  29). nng7 chiah gu5-kang2, gou7 chiah mi5-iuN5-kang2, gou7 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2, gou7 chiah be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2, choe3 sia7-un-che3; chiah-e5 si7 Hi-lun5 e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-ap e5 le2-mih8.
	30). Te7-si3 jit8 si7 Liu5-pian7 kiaN2-sun e5 siu2-leng2, Si7-tiu-jiN2 e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-siok;  31). i e5 le2-mih8 chiu7-si7 chit8 e5 gun5-poaN5, tang7 chit8-pah saN-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, chit8 e5 gun5-oaN2, tang7 chhit-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, long2 si7 chiau3 seng3-sou2 e5 sia3-khek-lek8; chi2 nng7-e5 toe2-moa2 tiau-ho5 iu5 e5 iu3-mi7-hun2, choe3 sou3-che3;  32). chit8 e5 kim-au, tang7 chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, toe2 hiuN moa2-moa2;  33). chit8 chiah gu5-kang2-a2, chit8 chiah mi5-iuN5-kang2, chit8 chiah be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2, choe3 sio-che3;  34). chit8 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2 choe3 siok8-choe7-che3;  35). nng7 chiah gu5-kang2, gou7 chiah mi5-iuN5-kang2, gou7 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2, gou7 chiah be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2, choe3 sia7-un-che3; chiah-e5 si7 Si7-tiu-jiN2 e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-siok e5 le2-mih8.
	36). Te7-gou7 jit8 si7 Se-bian7 kiaN2-sun e5 siu2-leng2, Sou-li7-sa-tai7 e5 kiaN2 Si7-lou7-biat8;  37). i e5 le2-mih8 chiu7-si7 chit8 e5 gun5-poaN5, tang7 chit8-pah saN-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, chit8 e5 gun5-oaN2, tang7 chhit-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, long2 si7 chiau3 seng3-sou2 e5 sia3-khek-lek8; chi2 nng7-e5 toe2-moa2 tiau-ho5 iu5 e5 iu3-mi7-hun2, choe3 sou3-che3;  38). chit8 e5 kim-au, tang7 chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, toe2 hiuN moa2-moa2;  39). chit8 chiah gu5-kang2-a2, chit8 chiah mi5-iuN5-kang2, chit8 chiah be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2, choe3 sio-che3;  40). chit8 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2 choe3 siok8-choe7-che3;  41). nng7 chiah gu5-kang2, gou7 chiah mi5-iuN5-kang2, gou7 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2, gou7 chiah be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2, choe3 sia7-un-che3; chiah-e5 si7 Sou-li7-sa-tai7 e5 kiaN2 Si7-lou7-biat8 e5 le2-mih8.
	42). Te7-lak8 jit8 si7 Ka-tek kiaN2-sun e5 siu2-leng2, Tiu-jiN2 e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-nga2-sat;  43). i e5 le2-mih8 chiu7-si7 chit8 e5 gun5-poaN5, tang7 chit8-pah saN-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, chit8 e5 gun5-oaN2, tang7 chhit-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, long2 si7 chiau3 seng3-sou2 e5 sia3-khek-lek8; chi2 nng7-e5 toe2-moa2 tiau-ho5 iu5 e5 iu3-mi7-hun2, choe3 sou3-che3;  44). chit8 e5 kim-au, tang7 chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, toe2 hiuN moa2-moa2;  45). chit8 chiah gu5-kang2-a2, chit8 chiah mi5-iuN5-kang2, chit8 chiah be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2, choe3 sio-che3;  46). chit8 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2, choe3 siok8-choe7-che3;  47). nng7 chiah gu5-kang2, gou7 chiah mi5-iuN5-kang2, gou7 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2, gou7 chiah be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2, choe3 sia7-un-che3; chiah-e5 si7 Tiu-jiN2 e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-nga2-sat e5 le2-mih8.
	48). Te7-chhit jit8 si7 I2-hoat-lian5 kiaN2-sun e5 siu2-leng2, A-bi2-hut e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-sa-ma2;  49). i e5 le2-mih8 chiu7-si7 chit8 e5 gun5-poaN5, tang7 chit8-pah saN-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, chit8 e5 gun5-oaN2, tang7 chhit-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, long2 si7 chiau3 seng3-sou2 e5 sia3-khek-lek8, chi2 nng7-e5 toe2-moa2 tiau-ho5 iu5 e5 iu3-mi7-hun2, choe3 sou3-che3;  50). chit8 e5 kim-au, tang7 chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, toe2 hiuN moa2-moa2;  51). chit8 chiah gu5-kang2-a2, chit8 chiah mi5-iuN5-kang2, chit8-chiah be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2, choe3 sio-che3;  52). chit8 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2 choe3 siok8-choe7-che3;  53). nng7 chiah gu5-kang2, gou7 chiah mi5-iuN5-kang2, gou7 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2, gou7 chiah be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2, choe3 sia7-un-che3; chiah-e5 si7 A-bi2-hut e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-sa-ma2 e5 le2-mih8.
	54). Te7-poeh jit8 si7 Ma2-na2-se kiaN2-sun e5 siu2-leng2, Pi2-tai7-siok e5 kiaN2 Ka-ma2-liat8;  55). i e5 le2-mih8 chiu7-si7 chit8 e5 gun5-poaN5, tang7 chit8-pah saN-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, chit8 e5 gun5-oaN2, tang7 chhit-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, long2 si7 chiau3 seng3-sou2 e5 sia3-khek-lek8; chi2 nng7-e5 toe2-moa2 tiau-ho5 iu5 e5 iu3-mi7-hun2, choe3 sou3-che3;  56). chit8 e5 kim-au, tang7 chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, toe2 hiuN moa2-moa2;  57). chit8 chiah gu5-kang2-a2, chit8 chiah mi5-iuN5-kang2, chit8 chiah be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2, choe3 sio-che3;  58). chit8 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2 choe3 siok8-choe7-che3;  59). nng7 chiah gu5-kang2, gou7 chiah mi5-iuN5-kang2, gou7 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2, gou7 chiah be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2, choe3 sia7-un-che3; chiah-e5 si7 Pi2-tai7-siok e5 kiaN2 Ka-ma2-liat8 e5 le2-mih8.
	60). Te7-kau2 jit8 si7 Pian7-nga2-bin2 kiaN2-sun e5 siu2-leng2, Ki-to-ni5 e5 kiaN2 A-pi2-tan3;  61). i e5 le2-mih8 chiu7-si7 chit8 e5 gun5-poaN5, tang7 chit8-pah saN-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, chit8 e5 gun5-oaN2, tang7 chhit-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, long2 si7 chiau3 seng3-sou2 e5 sia3-khek-lek8; chi2 nng7-e5 toe2-moa2 tiau-ho5 iu5 e5 iu3-mi7-hun2, choe3 sou3-che3;  62). chit8 e5 kim-au, tang7 chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, toe2 hiuN moa2-moa2;  63). chit8 chiah gu5-kang2-a2, chit8 chiah mi5-iuN5-kang2, chit8 chiah be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2, choe3 sio-che3;  64). chit8 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2, choe3 siok8-choe7-che3;  65). nng7 chiah gu5-kang2, gou7 chiah mi5-iuN5-kang2, gou7 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2, gou7 chiah be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2, choe3 sia7-un-che3; chiah-e5 si7 Ki-to-ni5 e5 kiaN2 A-pi2-tan3 e5 le2-mih8.
	66). Te7-chap8 jit8 si7 Tan3 kiaN2-sun e5 siu2-leng2, A-bi2-sa-tai7 e5 kiaN2 A-hi-i2-sia7;  67). i e5 le2-mih8 chiu7-si7 chit8 e5 gun5-poaN5, tang7 chit8-pah saN-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, chit8 e5 gun5-oaN2, tang7 chhit-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, long2 si7 chiau3 seng3-sou2 e5 sia3-khek-lek8, chi2 nng7-e5 toe2-moa2 tiau-ho5 iu5 e5 iu3-mi7-hun2, choe3 sou3-che3;  68). chit8 e5 kim-au, tang7 chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, toe2 hiuN moa2-moa2;  69). chit8 chiah gu5-kang2-a2, chit8 chiah mi5-iuN5-kang2, chit8 chiah be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2, choe3 sio-che3;  70). chit8 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2, choe3 siok8-choe7-che3;  71). nng7 chiah gu5-kang2, gou7 chiah mi5-iuN5-kang2, gou7 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2, gou7 chiah be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2, choe3 sia7-un-che3; chiah-e5 si7 A-bi2-sa-tai7 e5 kiaN2 A-hi-i2-sia7 e5 le2-mih8.
	72). Te7-chap8-it jit8 si7 A-siat kiaN2-sun e5 siu2-leng2, Go5-lan5 e5 kiaN2 PhaN3-kiat;  73). i e5 le2-mih8 chiu7-si7 chit8 e5 gun5-poaN5, tang7 chit8-pah saN-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, chit8 e5 gun5-oaN2, tang7 chhit-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, long2 si7 chiau3 seng3-sou2 e5 sia3-khek-lek8, chi2 nng7-e5 toe2-moa2 tiau-ho5 iu5 e5 iu3-mi7-hun2, choe3 sou3-che3;  74). chit8 e5 kim-au, tang7 chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, toe2 hiuN moa2-moa2;  75). chit8 chiah gu5-kang2-a2, chit8 chiah mi5-iuN5-kang2, chit8 chiah be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2, choe3 sio-che3;  76). chit8 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2, choe3 siok8-choe7-che3;  77). nng7 chiah gu5-kang2, gou7 chiah mi5-iuN5-kang2, gou7 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2, gou7 chiah be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2, choe3 sia7-un-che3; chiah-e5 si7 Go5-lan5 e5 kiaN2 PhaN3-kiat e5 le2-mih8.
	78). Te7-chap8-ji7 jit8 si7 Na2-hut-tha-li7 kiaN2-sun e5 siu2-leng2, I2-lam5 e5 kiaN2 A-hi-lah8;  79). i e5 le2-mih8 chiu7-si7 chit8 e5 gun5-poaN5, tang7 chit8-pah saN-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, chit8 e5 gun5-oaN2, tang7 chhit-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, long2 si7 chiau3 seng3-sou2 e5 sia3-khek-lek8, chi2 nng7-e5 toe2-moa2 tiau-ho5 iu5 e5 iu3-mi7-hun2, choe3 sou3-che3;  80). chit8 e5 kim-au, tang7 chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, toe2 hiuN moa2-moa2;  81). chit8 chiah gu5-kang2-a2, chit8 chiah mi5-iuN5-kang2, chit8 chiah be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2, choe3 sio-che3;  82). chit8 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2, choe3 siok8-choe7-che3;  83). nng7 chiah gu5-kang2, gou7 chiah mi5-iuN5-kang2, gou7 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2, gou7 chiah be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2, choe3 sia7-un-che3; chiah-e5 si7 I2-lam5 e5 kiaN2 A-hi-lah8 e5 le2-mih8.
	84). Eng7 iu5 boah-toaN5 e5 jit8, I2-sek-liat8 chiah e5 siu2-leng2, i tioh8 kiaN5 hian3-toaN5 e5 le2 sou2 hian3-e5, chiu7-si7 gun5-poaN5 chap8-ji7 e5, gun5-oaN2 chap8-ji7 e5, kim-au chap8-ji7 e5;  85). tak8 e5 gun5-poaN5 tang7 chit8-pah saN-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8, tak8 e5 oaN2 tang7 chhit-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8; it-chhe3 khi3-ku7 e5 gun5, chiau3 seng3-sou2 e5 sia3-khek-lek8, kiong7 u7 nng7-chheng si3-pah sia3-khek-lek8;  86). chap8-ji7 e5 kim-au toe2 hiuN moa2-moa2, chiau3 seng3-sou2 e5 sia3-khek-lek8, tak8 e5 au tang7 chap8 sia3-khek-lek8; chiah e5 au e5 kim, tang7 kiong7 chit8-pah ji7-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8;  87). choe3 sio-che3 e5 cheng-siN, kiong7 gu5-kang2 chap8-ji7 chiah, iuN5-kang2 chap8-ji7 chiah, be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2 chap8-ji7 chiah, kap tang5 hian3 e5 sou3-che3 choe3 siok8-choe7-che3 e5 soaN-iuN5-kang2 chap8-ji7 chiah;  88). choe3 sia7-un-che3 e5 cheng-siN, kiong7 gu5-kang2 ji7-chap8-si3 chiah, mi5-iuN5-kang2 lak8-chap8 chiah, soaN-iuN5-kang2 lak8-chap8 chiah, be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2 lak8-chap8 chiah; chiah-e5 chiu7-si7 eng7 iu5 boah-toaN5 liau2-au7, ui7-tioh8 kiaN5 hian3-toaN5 e5 le2 sou2 hian3-e5.  89). Mou5-se jip8 hoe7-bou7, beh kap Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2 oe7 e5 si5, thiaN-kiN3 hoat-kui7 si-un-sou2 e5 teng2-bin7, nng7 e5 ki-lou7-peng e5 tiong-kan, kap i kong2-oe7 e5 SiaN, chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kap i kong2.

[8]	Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  2). Li2 hoan-hu3 A-lun5 ka7 i kong2, Li2 tiam2 teng e5 si5, chhit-choaN2 teng long2 tioh8 chio3-kng teng-tai5 cheng5.  3). A-lun5 chiau3 an2-ni kiaN5, tiam2 teng chio3-kng ti7 teng-tai5 cheng5, si7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa beng7-leng7 Mou5-se e5.  4). Chit e5 teng-tai5 e5 choe3-hoat, si7 eng7 kim phah-e5, lian5 i e5 cho7 kap i e5 hoe long2 si7 phah e5.  Mou5-se che3-cho7 teng-tai5, si7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 chi2-si7 e5 khoan2-sit.
	5). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  6).  Li2 tioh8 tui3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 tiong-kan keng2-chhut Li7-bi7 lang5, hou7 in chheng-khi3.  7). Hou7 in chheng-khi3 tioh8 an2-ni kiaN5; eng7 tu5-khi3 choe7 e5 chui2 hiu3 ti7 in seng-khu; koh kah in eng7 thi3-thau5-to, thi3 thong seng-khu, soe2 i-hok8, chheng-khi3 pun2-sin.  8). Au7-lai5 in tioh8 chhu2 chit8 chiah gu5-kang2-a2, kap i e5 sou3-che3, chiu7-si7 tiau-ho5 iu5 e5 iu3-mi7-hun2; li2 tioh8 leng7-goa7 chhu2 chit8 chiah gu5-kang2-a2 choe3 siok8-choe7-che3.  9). Li2 tioh8 chhoa7 Li7-bi7 lang5 kau3 hoe7-bou7 cheng5, chu7-chip8 I2-sek-liat8 chok8 e5 choan5-hoe7.  10). Koh chhoa7 Li7-bi7 lang5 kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5; I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tioh8 hoaN7-chhiu2 ti7 Li7-bi7 lang5 e5 teng2-bin7.  11). A-lun5 tioh8 hian3 Li7-bi7 lang5 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, choe3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 io5-che3, hou7 in thang choe3 hok8-sai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 kang.  12). Li7-bi7 lang5 tioh8 hoaN7-chhiu2 ti7 hiah e5 gu5-kang2-a2 e5 thau5-khak-teng2; Li2 tioh8 hian3 chit8-chiah choe3 siok8-choe7-che3, koh hian3 chit8-chiah choe3 sio-che3, hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, ka7 Li7-bi7 lang5 siok8-choe7.  13). Li2 tioh8 hou7 Li7-bi7 lang5 khia7 ti7 A-lun5 kap i e5 kiaN2 e5 bin7-cheng5, hian3 in choe3 io5-che3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  14). An2-ni, li2 tioh8 tui3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 hun-piat Li7-bi7 lang5, chiu7 Li7-bi7 lang5 beh kui ti7 Goa2.  15). Chit-tiap8 liau2-au7 Li7-bi7 lang5 tioh8 jip8-khi3 choe3 hoe7-bou7 e5 kang; li2 tioh8 hou7 in chheng-khi3, hian3 in choe3 io5-che3.  16). In-ui7 in si7 tui3 I2-sek-liat8 tiong oan5-choan5 kui Goa2--e5; Goa2 keng2 in siok8 ti7 Goa2, lai5 thoe3 it-chhe3 thau5-the--e5, chiu7-si7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 thau5-chiuN7--e5.  17). In-ui7 I2-sek-liat8 tiong it-chhe3 thau5-chiuN7-siN--e5, hek8-si7 lang5, hek8-si7 cheng-siN, long2 si7 Goa2-e5.  Goa2 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 phah-si2 it-chhe3 thau5-chiuN7-siN--e5 hit-jit8, i2-keng hun-piat in choe3-seng3, kui ti7 Goa2.  18). Goa2 keng2 Li7-bi7 lang5, thoe3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 it-chhe3 thau5-chiuN7-siN--e5.  19). Goa2 tui3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tiong, keng2 Li7-bi7 lang5, siuN2-su3 A-lun5 kap i e5 kiaN2-sun, thang thoe3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 choe3 hoe7-bou7 e5 chhe-eng7, koh ui7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 siok8-choe7; bian2-tit I2-sek-liat8 lang5 oa2-kun7 seng3-sou2 e5 si5, u7 chai-e7 kau3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 tiong-kan.  20). Mou5-se A-lun5 kap I2-sek-liat8 lang5 choan5-hoe7, chiu7 tui3 Li7-bi7 lang5 an2-ni kiaN5; kiN3-na7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lun7-khi2 Li7-bi7 lang5 sou2 beng7-leng7 Mou5-se e5, I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chiu7 tui3 in an2-ni kiaN5.  21). Tui3 an2-ni Li7-bi7 lang5 chheng-khi3 ka-ki7, tu5-khi3 choe7, soe2 in e5 i-hok8; A-lun5 chiong in hian3-choe3 io5-che3 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5; A-lun5 koh ui7 in siok8-choe7 lai5 chheng-khi3 in.  22). Jian5-au7 Li7-bi7 lang5 jip8-khi3, ti7 A-lun5 kap i e5 kiaN2 e5 bin7-cheng5, ti7 hoe7-bou7 tiong choe3 in e5 kang; Ia5-ho5-hoa lun7 Li7-bi7 lang5 lai5 beng7-leng7 Mou5-se e5, I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chiu7 an2-ni tui3 in kiaN5.
	23).  Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  24). Lun7 Li7-bi7 lang5 si7 an2-ni:  tui3 ji7-chap8-gou7 he3 i2-siong7, in tioh8 lai5 hoe7-bou7, choe3 chhe-eng7.  25). Kau3 gou7-chap8 he3 chiu7 theng5-kang, bo5 koh choe3 chhe-eng7;  26). tok8-tok8 tioh8 ti7 hoe7-bou7, kap in e5 hiaN-ti7 saN-kap su-hau7, siu2 sou2 kau-tai3 e5, bo5 koh choe3 kang; lun7-kau3 sou2 kau-tai3 Li7-bi7 lang5--e5, li2 tioh8 tui3 in an2-ni kiaN5.

[9]	Chhut Ai-kip8 ji7--ni5 chiaN-geh8, Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 Se-nai2 khong3-ia2, beng7-leng7 Mou5-se kong2,  2). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 eng-kai ti7 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 jit8-ki5 siu2 poaN5-ke3-choeh;  3). ti7 pun2-geh8 chap8-si3 jit8 hong5-hun e5 si5, lin2 tioh8 ti7 sou2 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 jit8 siu2 i, chiau3 i it-chhe3 e5 lut8-le7, it-chhe3 e5 hoat-tou7 lai5 siu2 i.  4). Tui3 an2-ni Mou5-se hoan-hu3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 siu2 poaN5-ke3-choeh.  5). ChiaN-geh8 chap8-si3 jit8 hong5-hun e5 si5, in chiu7 ti7 Se-nai2 e5 khong3-ia2, siu2 poaN5-ke3-choeh; kiN3-na7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beng7-leng7 Mou5-se e5, I2-sek-liat8 lang5 long2 chiau3 an2-ni kiaN5.
	6). U7 kui2-na7 lang5 hou7 lang5 e5 sin-si bak la5-sam5, boe7-oe7 ti7 hit-jit8 siu2 poaN5-ke3-choeh; tng hit-jit8 in kau3 Mou5-se A-lun5 e5 bin7-cheng5.  7). Hiah e5 lang5 ka7 in kong2, Goan2 in-ui7 hou7 lang5 e5 sin-si bak la5-sam5, siaN2-su7 chou2-tong3 goan2 boe7 thang ti7 I2-sek-liat8 tiong, ti7 sou2 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 jit8-ki5 hian3 le2-mih8 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah?  8). Mou5-se ka7 in kong2, Lin2 khia7-teh theng3-hau7, goa2 beh thiaN Ia5-ho5-hoa chaiN2-iuN7 hoan-hu3 lin2.
	9). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  10). Li2 tioh8 hoan-hu3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kong2, Hek8-si7 lin2 a2-si7 lin2 e5 hou7-e3 e5 tiong-kan, na7 u7 lang5 hou7 sin-si bak la5-sam5, a2-si7 hng7-hng7 ti7 lou7--nih, iu5-goan5 tioh8 siu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 poaN5-ke3-choeh.  11). In tioh8 ti7 ji7-geh8 chap8-si3 jit8 hong5-hun e5 si5 lai5 siu2 i, chham bo5-kaN3 piaN2 kap khou2-chhai3 lai5 chiah8.  12). M7-thang lau5 chit8-tiam2-a2 kau3 keh cha2-khi2, iuN5-a2 e5 kut chit8-ki ia7 m7-thang phah-chih8; in tioh8 chiau3 poaN5-ke3-choeh chiah e5 lut8-le7 lai5 siu2 i.  13). Chong2-si7 lang5 na7 chheng-khi3 ia7 m7-si7 ti7 lou7-tiong, na7 ka-ki7 the-si5 m7 siu2 poaN5-ke3-choeh, tioh8 tui3 i e5 peh-siN3-tiong chian2-tu5 hit e5 lang5, in-ui7 i ti7 sou2 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 jit8 bo5 hian3 le2-mih8 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, hit-lang5 tioh8 tam-tng i e5 choe7.  14). Na7 u7 goa7-lang5 kia3-kha ti7 lin2 tiong-kan, ai3 siu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 poaN5-ke3-choeh, i tioh8 chiau3 poaN5-ke3-choeh e5 lut8-le7 hoat-tou7 lai5 kiaN5; chhut-goa7 lang5 kap pun2-toe7 lang5 tioh8 tang5 chit8 e5 lut8-le7 lai5 kiaN5.
	15). Khi2 hoe7-bou7 hit-jit8, u7 hun5 jia i e5 hoe7-bou7, chiu7-si7 cheng3-ku3 e5 pou3-piN5; tui3 e5-hng kau3 cha2-khi2, u7 chhin-chhiuN7 he2 e5 khoan2-sit kham3 ti7 hoe7-bou7.  16). Siong5-siong5 si7 an2-ni; hun5 jia i, mi5-si5 chhin-chhiuN7 he2 e5 khoan2-sit.  17). Hun5 tui3 pou3-piN5 siu chiuN7--khi3, I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chiu7 khi2-sin; hun5 theng5 e5 sou2-chai7, I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chiu7 chat-iaN5 ti7-hia.  18). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 beng7-leng7 khi2-sin, ia7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 beng7-leng7 an-iaN5; hun5 theng5 ti7 hoe7-bou7-teng2 e5 si5, in iu5-goan5 an-iaN5 ti7-hia.  19). Hun5 ti7 hoe7-bou7-teng2 theng5 choe7-choe7 jit8, I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chiu7 siu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 kau-tai3 e5, bo5 khi2-sin.  20). U7-si5 hun5 ti7 hoe7-bou7-teng2 kui2-na7 jit8, in chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 beng7-leng7 iu5-goan5 an-iaN5 ti7-hia, ia7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 beng7-leng7 khi2-sin.  21). U7-si5 hun5 jia--teh tui3 e5-hng kau3 cha2-khi2, cha2-khi2 si5 hun5 siu chiuN7-khi3, in chiu7 khi2-sin; bo5-lun7 jit8--si5 mi5--si5 hun5 siu chiuN7--khi3, in chiu7 khi2-sin.  22). Hun5 theng5 ti7 hoe7-bou7, bo5-lun7 si7 nng7-jit8, si7 chit8-geh8-jit8, si7 chit8-ni5, I2-sek-liat8 lang5 iu5-goan5 an-iaN5 ti7-hia, bo5 khi2-sin; chong2-si7 hun5 siu chiuN7--khi3, in chiu7 khi2-sin.  23). In than3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 beng7-leng7 an-iaN5, ia7 than3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 beng7-leng7 khi2-sin; in siu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 kau-tai3 e5, long2 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa thok Mou5-se sou2 beng7-leng7 e5.

[10]	Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  2). Li2 tioh8 eng7 gun5 phah nng7 ki ho7-thau5, eng7 phah e5 hoat lai5 choe3, hou7 li2 eng7 lai5 chu7-chip8 hoe7-chiong3, ia7 hou7 tak8-iaN5 khi2-sin.  3). Pun5 hiah-e5 e5 si5, choan5-hoe7 cheng3-lang5 tioh8 kau3 li2 hia, chu7-chip8 ti7 hoe7-bou7 mng5-khau2.  4). Na7 kan-ta pun5 chit8-ki, cheng3 siu2-leng2, chiu7-si7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 chok8-tiuN2, tioh8 chu7-chip8 kau3 li2 hia.  5). Pun5 toa7-siaN e5 si5, tang-peng5 sou2 an e5 iaN5 long2 tioh8 khi2-sin.  6). Te7-ji7 pai2 pun5 toa7-siaN e5 si5, lam5-peng5 sou2 an e5 iaN5 tioh8 khi2-sin; in beh khi2-sin tek-khak pun5 toa7-siaN.  7). Na7 beh chu7-chip8 hoe7-chiong3, lin2 tioh8 pun5 ho7-thau5, chong2-si7 m7-thang pun5 toa7-siaN.  8). A-lun5 e5 kiaN2-sun choe3 che3-si e5, tioh8 pun5 hiah e5 ho7-thau5; che beh choe3 lin2 tai7-tai7 eng2-oan2 e5 le7.  9). Lin2 ti7 pun2-toe7 kap khi-ap lin2 e5 tui3-tek8 kau-chian3, chiu7 tioh8 eng7 ho7-thau5 pun5 toa7-siaN, chiu7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 ki3-liam7, ia7 beh tit-tioh8 kiu3 thoat-li7 lin2 e5 tui3-tek8.  10). Ia7 ti7 lin2 khoai3-lok8 e5 jit8, kap choeh-ki5, kap geh8 e5 chhoe-it, si7 ti7 lin2 hian3 sio-che3 kap sia7-un-che3 e5 si5, ia7 tioh8 pun5 ho7-thau5; che long2 beh ti7 lin2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5 choe3 ki3-liam7; Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3.
	11). Te7-ji7 ni5 ji7-geh8 ji7-chap8 jit8, hun5 tui3 cheng3-ku3 e5 hoe7-bou7 siu chiuN7--khi3.  12). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chiu7 chiau3 in e5 lou7-cham7 khi2-sin, li7-khui Se-nai2 e5 khong3-ia2; hun5 theng5 ti7 Pa-lan5 e5 khong3-ia2.  13). Che si7 in chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa thok Mou5-se sou2 beng7-leng7-e5, thau5-chit8-pai2 khi2-sin.  14). Chiau3 in e5 kun-tui7 choe3-thau5 khi2-sin e5, si7 Iu5-tai7 chok8 e5 iaN5 e5 toa7-ki5; kun-tui7 e5 thong2-leng2 si7 A-bi2-na2-tat8 e5 kiaN2 Na2-sun7.  15). I2-sat-ka chi-phai3 kun-tui7 e5 thong2-leng2 si7 Sou-ap e5 kiaN2 Na2-than2-giap8.  16). Se-pou3-lun5 e5 chi-phai3 kun-tui7 e5 thong2-leng2 si7 Hi-lun5 e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-ap.  17). Hoe7-bou7 chiu7 thiah--khi2-lai5; kng hoe7-bou7--e5, Kek-sun7 e5 kiaN2-sun kap Bi2-lah8-li7 e5 kiaN2-sun khi2-sin kiaN5.  18). Chiau3 i e5 kun-tui7, Liu5-pian7 iaN5 e5 toa7-ki5 khi2-sin; i e5 kun-tui7 e5 thong2-leng2 si7 Si7-tiu-jiN2 e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-siok.  19). Se-bian7 chi-phai3 kun-tui7 e5 thong2-leng2 si7 Sou-li7-sa-tai7 e5 kiaN2 Si7-lou7-biat8.  20). Ka-tek chi-phai3 kun-tui7 e5 thong2-leng2 si7 Tiu-jiN2 e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-nga2-sat.  21). Ko-hat lang5 kng seng3-mih8--e5 khi2-sin kiaN5; in be7 kau3 e5 tai7-seng, hiah e5 lang5 hoe7-bou7 i2-keng tah ho2.  22). Chiau3 i e5 kun-tui7, I2-hoat-lian5 iaN5 e5 toa7-ki5 khi2-sin; i e5 kun-tui7 e5 thong2-leng2 si7 A-bi2-hut e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-sa-ma2.  23). Ma2-na2-se chi-phai3 kun-tui7 e5 thong2-leng2 si7 Pi2-tai7-siok e5 kiaN2 Ka-ma2-liat8.  24). Pian7-nga2-bin2 chi-phai3 kun-tui7 e5 thong2-leng2 si7 Ki-to-ni5 e5 kiaN2 A-pi2-tan3.  25). Choe3 chiah e5 iaN5 e5 lou7-be2 tui7 e5, si7 Tan3 e5 iaN5 e5 toa7-ki5, chiau3 i e5 kun-tui7 khi2-sin; i e5 kun-tui7 e5 thong2-leng2 si7 A-bi2-sa-tai7 e5 kiaN2 A-hi-i2-sia7.  26). A-siat chi-phai3 kun-tui7 e5 thong2-leng2 si7 Go5-lan5 e5 kiaN2 PhaN3-kiat.  27). Na2-hut-tha-li7 chi-phai3 kun-tui7 e5 thong2-leng2 si7 I2-lam5 e5 kiaN2 A-hi-lah8.  28). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chiau3 i e5 kun-tui7 khi2-sin, i e5 tui7-ngou2 chiu7-si7 an2-ni.
	29). Mou5-se tui3 i e5 goa7-chhek Bi2-tian5 lang5 Liu5-jiN2 e5 kiaN2 Ho5-pa kong2, Goan2 beh khi3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 bat kong2, Goa2 eng7 i siuN2-su3 lin2 e5 toe7, chhiaN2 li2 kap goan2 lai5-khi3, goan2 beh ho2 khoan2-thai7 li2; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa i2-keng eng3-un2 su3 hok-khi3 hou7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5.  30). I in3 kong2, Goa2 m7 khi3, goa2 beh to3-khi3 goa2 e5 pun2-toe7 pun2-chok8 hia.  31). Mou5-se kong2, Kiu5 li2 m7-thang li7-khui goan2, in-ui7 li2 chai goan2 ti7 khong3-ia2 tioh8 chaiN2-iuN7 chat-iaN5; li2 thang choe3 goan2 e5 bak8-chiu.  32). Li2 na7 beh kap goan2 khi3, kiN3-na7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hou7 goan2 e5 hok-khi3, goan2 ia7 tek-khak an2-ni hou7 li2.
	33). In li7-khui Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 soaN, khi2-sin kiaN5 saN-jit8 e5 lou7-cham7; Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 iok-kui7 ti7 thau5-cheng5 kiaN5 saN-jit8 e5 lou7-cham7, ka7 in chhe7 an-hioh e5 sou2-chai7.  34). In thiat-iaN5 khi2-sin, jit8--si5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 hun5 ti7 in e5 teng2-bin7.
	35). Iok-kui7 khi2-sin e5 si5, Mou5-se chiu7 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 khi2-lai5; goan7 Li2 e5 tui3-tek8 si3-soaN3; goan7 oan3-hun7 Li2 e5 lang5 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 to5-chau2.  36). Iok-kui7 theng5 e5 si5, i chiu7 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 to3-lai5 kau3 I2-sek-liat8 chheng-chheng ban7-ban7 lang5 e5 tiong-kan.

[11]	Cheng3 peh-siN3 ngauh8-ngauh8-liam7, in e5 phaiN2-oe7 kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 hi7-khang; Ia5-ho5-hoa thiaN-kiN3 chiu7 toa7 siu7-khi3.  Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 he2 toh8 ti7 in tiong-kan, sio ti7 iaN5 e5 piN-kak.  2). Peh-siN3 tui3 Mou5-se ai-kiu5, Mou5-se ki5-kiu5 Ia5-ho5-hoa; hit e5 he2 chiu7 sit.  3). Hit sou2-chai7 chiu7 kio3 choe3 Tha-pi7-lah8, in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 he2 sio ti7 in tiong-kan.
	4). In tiong-kan chap8-sek lang5 toa7 heng-khi2 tham-iok8 e5 sim; I2-sek-liat8 lang5 koh thi5-khau3 kong2, Chi7-chui7 hou7 goan2 bah thang chiah8 ah?  5). Goan2 ki3-tit ti7 Ai-kip8 e5 si5, chiah8 hi5 bian2 chiN5, ia7 ki3-tit u7 ng5-koe, si-koe, ku2-chhai3, chhang-a2, soan3-a2.  6). TaN goan2 e5 cheng-lek8 kou-ta5, bo5 poaN3-hang7 mih8; tu5 ma2-na2 i2-goa7, ti7 goan2 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5 e5 bo5 pat8-hang7 mih8.  7). Chit e5 ma2-na2 chhin-chhiuN7 oan5-sui-jin5, khoan2-sit chhin-chhiuN7 chin-chu e5 khoan2.  8). Peh-siN3 si3-koe3 kiaN5 khioh i, u7-e5 eng7 bo7 bo7 i, u7-e5 eng7 khu7 cheng i, ti7 tiaN2--nih pek choe3 piaN2; chu-bi7 chhin-chhiuN7 tiau-ho5 iu5 e5 chiah8-mih8.  9). Mi5--si5 lou7-chui2 loh8 ti7 iaN5-tiong, ma2-na2 ia7 te3 i loh8.  10). Mou5-se thiaN-kiN3 peh-siN3 e5 tak8-ke tak8-lang5 ti7 ka-ki7 e5 pou3-piN5 mng5-khau2 teh thi5-khau3; Ia5-ho5-hoa toa7 siu7-khi3, Mou5-se ia7 bo5 hoaN-hi2.  11). Mou5-se tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Li2 siaN2-su7 phaiN2 khoan2-thai7 Li2 e5 lou5-pok8; goa2 chaiN2-iuN7 bo5 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 un-tian2, Li2 keng2-jian5 eng7 chiah e5 peh-siN3 e5 taN3 he7 ti7 goa2 e5 sin-chiuN7?  12). Chiah e5 peh-siN3 kiam2 si7 goa2 hoai5-in7 e5? Kiam2 si7 goa2 siN e5 mah, Li2 keng2-jian5 tui3 goa2 kong2, Pho7 in ti7 heng-cheng5, chhin-chhiuN7 iuN2-chhi7 gin2-na2 e5 lau7-pe7 pho7 chiah8-leng e5 eN-a2, kau3 ti7 Li2 chiu3-choa7 siuN2-su3 in e5 chou2-kong e5 toe7?  13). Goa2 beh tui3 tah-loh8 tit-tioh8 bah hou7 chiah e5 peh-siN3? in-ui7 in long2 tui3 goa2 thi5-khau3 kong2, Li2 tioh8 eng7 bah hou7 goan2, hou7 goan2 thang chiah8.  14). Chiah e5 peh-siN3 e5 taN3 siuN tang7, goa2 ka-ki7 tam-tng boe7 khi2.  15). Li2 na7 an2-ni khoan2-thai7 goa2, goa2 na7 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 un-tian2, kiu5 Li2 chek-si5 ka7 goa2 thai5-si2, bian2 hou7 goa2 khoaN3-kiN3 pun2-sin e5 khou2-cheng5.
	16). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 tioh8 chu7-chip8 I2-sek-liat8 e5 tiuN2-lo2, chhit-chap8 lang5, lai5 Goa2 chia, chiu7-si7 li2 sou2 chai choe3 peh-siN3 e5 tiuN2-lo2 kap koaN-tiuN2 e5, chhoa7 in kau3 hoe7-bou7, hou7 in kap li2 khia7 ti7-hia.  17). Goa2 beh kang3-lim5 ti7-hia kap li2 kong2-oe7 , ia7 beh chiong kang3-loh8 ti7 li2 teng2-bin7 e5 sin5, ia7 kang3-loh8 ti7 in; in chiu7 kap li2 saN-kap tam-tng peh-siN3 e5 taN3, bian2-tit li2 ka-ki7 tam-tng.  18). Ia7 tioh8 ka7 peh-siN3 kong2, Lin2 tioh8 hou7 ka-ki7 choe3-seng3, pi7-pan7 bin5-a2-jit8 thang chiah8-bah, in-ui7 lin2 u7 thi5-khau3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa thiaN-kiN3, kong2, Chi7-chui7 hou7 goan2 chiah8 bah? in-ui7 goan2 ti7 Ai-kip8 chin ho2; sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh hou7 lin2 bah, hou7 lin2 thang chiah8.  19). Lin2 m7-si7 chiah8 chit8-jit8, nng7 jit8, gou7-jit8, chap8 jit8, ji7-chap8 jit8;  20). beh chiah8 kau3 chit8-geh8-jit8 moa2, kau3 bah tui3 lin2 e5 phiN7-khang chhut-lai5, hou7 lin2 iam3-ouN3; in-ui7 lin2 khi3-sak tiam3-ti7 lin2 tiong-kan e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa, ti7 I e5 bin7-cheng5 thi5-khau3 kong2, Goan2 siaN2-su7 chhut Ai-kip8 ah?  21). Mou5-se kong2, Chiah-e5 kap goa2 tiam3 e5 peh-siN3, pou7-kiaN5 e5 toa7-lang5 u7 lak8-chap8-ban7, ia7 Li2 kong2, Goa2 beh hou7 in chiah8 bah, hou7 in thang chiah8 kau3 chit8-geh8-jit8 moa2.  22). Kiam2 beh ui7 in thai5 iuN5-kun5, gu5-kun5, hou7 in chiah8 kau3-giah8? a2-si7 ui7-tioh8 in chu7-chip8 hai2-lai7 sou2 u7 e5 hi5, hou7 in chiah8 kau3-giah8 mah?  23). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 chhiu2 kiam2 si7 te2 mah? TaN li2 beh khoaN3 Goa2 e5 oe7, tui3 li2 eng3-giam7 a2-bo5.
	24). Mou5-se chhut-khi3 chiong Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 ka7 peh-siN3 kong2; ia7 chio-chip8 peh-siN3 e5 tiuN2-lo2 chhit-chap8 lang5, hou7 in khia7 ti7 Pou3-piN5 e5 si3-ui5.  25). Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 hun5-tiong kang3-lim5, tui3 Mou5-se kong2-oe7, chiong kang3-loh8 ti7 i teng2-bin7 e5 sin5, ia7 kang3-loh8 ti7 chhit-chap8 e5 tiuN2-lo2; sin5 lim5-kau3 in e5 si5, in chiu7 kong2 sian-ti e5 oe7, i2-au7 chiu7 bo5 koh kong2.  26). Chong2-si7 u7 nng7-lang5 iu5-goan5 ti7 iaN5-lai7, chit8-e5 mia5-kio3 I-li7-tat8, chit8-e5 mia5-kio3 Bi2-tat8, in ia7 ki3-mia5 chai7-lai7, chong2-si7 bo5 kau3 Pou3-piN5 hia; sin5 lim5-kau3 in, in chiu7 ti7 iaN5-lai7 kong2 sian-ti e5 oe7.  27). U7 chit8 e5 siau3-lian5 lang5 chau2-lai5 ka7 Mou5-se kong2, I-li7-tat8 Bi2-tat8 ti7 iaN5-lai7 kong2 sian-ti e5 oe7.  28). Kun-sui5 Mou5-se e5, Lun3 e5 kiaN2 Iok-su-a, chiu7-si7 siu7-keng2 e5 chit8-lang5, kong2, ChhiaN2 goa2 e5 chu2 Mou5-se kim3-chi2 in.  29). Mou5-se tui3 i kong2, Li2 thoe3 goa2 tou3-khi7 mah? Goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 peh-siN3 long2 choe3 sian-ti, Ia5-ho5-hoa eng7 I e5 sin5 kang3-loh8 ti7 in e5 teng2-bin7.  30). Mou5-se kap I2-sek-liat8 e5 tiuN2-lo2 chiu7 to3-khi3 iaN5-lai7.  31). U7 hong tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhut, chiong ian-chhun tui3 hai2--nih chhe--lai5, tui7-loh8 ti7 iaN5-piN, chit-peng5 iok-liok8 chit8-jit8 e5 lou7-cham7, hit-peng5 iok-liok8 chit8-jit8 e5 lou7-cham7, ti7 iaN5 e5 si3-ui5 pian3-pian3 si7, li7 toe7 iok-liok8 u7 nng7 tiu2.  32). Peh-siN3 khi2-lai5, thong-jit8 thong-mi5, kap keh-jit8 e5 thong-jit8, liah8 ian-chhun; kek8-chio2-e5 ia7 liah8 chap8 ho7-mui5-jiN2; ui7 pun2-sin pai5-liat8 ti7 iaN5 e5 si3-ui5.  33). Bah ti7 in e5 chhui3-khi2, iau2 chiah8 be7 liau2, Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 tui3 peh-siN3 hoat siu7-khi3; Ia5-ho5-hoa kang3 toa7 chai-e7 lai5 phah peh-siN3.  34). Hit e5 sou2-chai7 ho7-mia5 kio3 Ki-phok-lo5-hap-tha-oa2, in-ui7 ti7-hia bai5-chong3 tham-iok8 e5 peh-siN3.  35). Peh-siN3 tui3 Ki-phok-lo5-hap-tha-oa2 kiaN5 kau3 Hap-se2-liok8; chiu7 tiam3 ti7 Hap-se2-liok8.

[12]	Bi2-li7-am3 kap A-lun5 hiam5 Mou5-se, ui7-tioh8 i sou2 chhoa7 Kou2-sit8 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2; in-ui7 Mou5-se bat chhoa7 Kou2-sit8 lang5 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 choe3 bou2.  2). In kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa kiam2 toaN-toaN kap Mou5-se kong2-oe7? Kiam2 ia7 bo5 kap goan2 kong2-oe7 mah? Chit e5 oe7 Ia5-ho5-hoa thiaN-kiN3.  3). Hit e5 Mou5-se choe3-lang5 kek8-ki5 un-jiu5, iaN5-ke3 se3-chiuN7 e5 cheng3-lang5.
	4). Ia5-ho5-hoa hut-jian5 tui3 Mou5-se A-lun5 Bi2-li7-am3, kong2, Lin2 saN-lang5 chhut-lai5 kau3 hoe7-bou7 chia; in saN-lang5 chiu7 chhut-lai5.  5). Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 hun5-thiau7-tiong kang3-lim5, khia7 ti7 Pou3-piN5 mng5-khau2, tiau3 A-lun5 kap Bi2-li7-am3; in nng7 lang5 chiu7 chhut-lai5.  6). I kong2, Tioh8 thiaN Goa2 e5 oe7; lin2 tiong-kan na7 u7 sian-ti, Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh eng7 iN7-siong7 hou7 in bat Goa2, ti7 bin5-bang7-tiong kap in kong2-oe7.  7). Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 Mou5-se m7-si7 an2-ni; i chin7-tiong ti7 Goa2 e5 choan5-ke.  8). Goa2 beh bin7 tui3 bin7 kap i kong2-oe7, chiu7-si7 beng5-beng5 kong2, bo5 eng7 chhai-gu2; koh i beh khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 heng5-iong5; lin2 hiam5 Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 Mou5-se, siaN2-su7 bo5 kiaN ah?  9). Ia5-ho5-hoa siu7-khi3 in, chiu7 khi3.  10). Hun5 tui3 Pou3-piN5-teng2 soa2-khui; khoaN3 ah, Bi2-li7-am3 thai2-ko chhin-chhiuN7 seh.  A-lun5 khoaN3 Bi2-li7-am3, khoaN3 ah, i si7 thai2-ko.  11). A-lun5 tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Goa2 e5 chu2 ah, kiu5 li2 boh8-tit in-ui7 goan2 e5 gu5-gong7 hoan7-choe7, chiong chit e5 choe7 kui ti7 goan2.  12). Kiu5 li2 m7-thang hou7 i chhin-chhiuN7 i2-keng si2, chiah tui3 lau7-bu2 e5 thai chhut, bah i2-keng noa7 chit8-poaN3.  13). Mou5-se chiu7 ai-kiu5 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 i-ho2 i.  14). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Siat-su2 i e5 lau7-pe7 phui3-noa7 ti7 i e5 bin7, i kiam2 bo5 kian3-siau3 chhit-jit8 mah? TaN tioh8 ka7 i koaiN ti7 iaN5-goa7 chhit-jit8, jian5-au7 chiah thang chhoa7 i jip8--lai5.  15). Tui3 an2-ni koaiN Bi2-li7-am3 ti7 iaN5-goa7 chhit-jit8; peh-siN3 bo5 khi2-sin, theng3-hau7 Bi2-li7-am3 koh jip8--lai5.  16). Au7-lai5 peh-siN3 tui3 Hap-se2-liok8 khi2-sin, ti7 Pa-lan5 e5 khong3-ia2 an-iaN5.

[13]	Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  2). Li2 tioh8 chhe lang5 khi3 thau-khoaN3 Goa2 sou2 su3 hou7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 Ka-lam5 toe7, tioh8 tui3 in chou2-kong tak8 chi-phai3 tiong chhe chit8-lang5, long2 si7 ti7 in tiong-kan choe3 siu2-leng2 e5.  3). Mou5-se chiu7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 beng7-leng7, tui3 Pa-lan5 e5 khong3-ia2 chhe in khi3, in long2 si7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 chok8-tiuN2.  4). In e5 mia5 ki3 ti7 e7-toe2; siok8 Liu5-pian7 e5 chi-phai3, Sat-khek e5 kiaN2 Sa-bou2-a;  5). siok8 Se-bian7 e5 chi-phai3, Ho5-li7 e5 kiaN2 Sa-hoat;  6). siok8 Iu5-tai7 e5 chi-phai3, Ia5-hu-ni5 e5 kiaN2 Ka-lek8;  7). siok8 I2-sat-ka e5 chi-phai3, Iok-sek e5 kiaN2 I2-ka;  8). siok8 I2-hoat-lian5 e5 chi-phai3, Lun3 e5 kiaN2 Ho5-se-a;  9). siok8 Pian7-nga2-bin2 e5 chi-phai3, Lah8-hu e5 kiaN2 PhaN3-the5;  10). siok8 Se-pou3-lun5 e5 chi-phai3, So-ti2 e5 kiaN2 Ka-tiap8;  11). Iok-sek e5 kiaN2-sun, siok8 Ma2-na2-se e5 chi-phai3, Sou-se e5 kiaN2 Ka-ti2;  12). siok8 Tan3 e5 chi-phai3, Ki-ma2-li7 e5 kiaN2 A-bi2-li7;  13). siok8 A-siat e5 chi-phai3, Bi2-ka-lek8 e5 kiaN2 Se-thiap;  14). siok8 Na2-hut-tha-li7 e5 chi-phai3, Pok8-se e5 kiaN2 Na2-pi2;  15). siok8 Ka-tek e5 chi-phai3, Ma2-ki e5 kiaN2 Kiu7-li7.  16). Chiah-e5 chiu7-si7 Mou5-se sou2 chhe khi3 thau-khoaN3 hit e5 toe7 e5 lang5 e5 mia5.  Mou5-se chiu7 chheng Lun3 e5 kiaN2 Ho5-se-a choe3 Iok-su-a.  17). Mou5-se chhe in khi3 thau-khoaN3 Ka-lam5 toe7, tui3 in kong2, Lin2 tui3 chit e5 lam5-hng chiuN7-khi3, soa3 peh-chiuN7 in e5 soaN,  18). khoaN3 hit e5 toe7 chaiN2-iuN7; ki5-tiong sou2 khia7 e5 peh-siN3 si7 kiong5 a2-si7 jiok8, si7 chio2 a2-si7 choe7;  19). sou2 khia7-khi2 e5 toe7 si7 sim2-mih8 khoan2, si7 ho2 a2-si7 phaiN2; sou2 khia7 e5 sou2-chai7 sim2-mih8 khoan2, si7 iaN5-poaN5 a2-si7 kian-kou3 e5 siaN5;  20). koh khoaN3 hit e5 toe7-thou2 chaiN2-iuN7, si7 pui5 a2-si7 san2; hit tiong-kan u7 chhiu7-bak8 a2-bo5.  Lin2 tioh8 ho2-taN2, chiong hit sou2-chai7 e5 ke2-chi2 toa3 koa2-a2 lai5; hit-si5 tu2-a2 si7 phu5-to5 khi2-thau5 sek8 e5 si5.
	21). In chiu7 khi3 thau-khoaN3 hit e5 toe7, tui3 Sim5 e5 khong3-ia2 kau3 Li7-hap8, kau3 jip8 Hap-ma2 e5 lou7-khau2.  22). In tui3 lam5-hng chiuN7-khi3, kau3 Hi-pek-lun5; ti7-hia u7 A-lap8 chok8 e5 lang5, A-hi-ban7, Si7-su, That-mai2.  (Hi-pek-lun5 siaN5 khi2-cho7 pi2 Ai-kip8 e5 So2-an siaN5 khah-cha2 chhit-ni5.)  23). In kau3 I2-sit8-kok e5 soaN-kok, tui3-hia chho3 phu5-to5-chhiu7 chit8-ki, teng2-bin7 u7 chit8-pha phu5-to5, nng7-lang5 eng7 kng3-a2 kng i; koh toa3 koa2-a2 siah8-liu5, kap bu5-hoa-ko2 lai5.  24). In-ui7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tui3-hia chho3 chit8 pha phu5-to5, hit sou2-chai7 chiah ho7-choe3 I2-sit8-kok e5 soaN-kok.
	25). In thau-khoaN3 hit e5 toe7 si3-chap8 jit8 ku2 chiah to3-lai5.  26). Kau3 Pa-lan5 e5 khong3-ia2 e5 Ka-te-su, kiN3 Mou5-se, A-lun5, kap I2-sek-liat8 e5 hoe7-chiong3, he5-hok in kap choan5-hoe7; koh eng7 hit sou2-chai7 e5 ke2-chi2 hou7 in khoaN3.  27). Koh ka7 i kong2, Goan2 kau3 li2 sou2 chhe goan2 khi3 e5 toe7, ko2-jian5 si7 lau5 lin kap bit8 e5 toe7; che chiu7-si7 hit e5 toe7 e5 ke2-chi2.  28). Chong2-si7 hit sou2-chai7 e5 peh-siN3 iong2-chong3, siaN5 ia7 kian-kou3 khoah-toa7; goan2 ti7-hia ia7 khoaN3-kiN3 A-lap8 chok8.  29). A-ma2-lek8 lang5 tiam3 ti7 lam5-hng; Hek lang5, Ia5-pou3-su lang5, A-mou5-li7 lang5, tiam3 ti7 soaN-toe7; Ka-lam5 lang5 tiam3 ti7 hai2-piN, kap Iok-tan3 ho5-piN.  30). Ka-lek8 ti7 Mou5-se e5 bin7-cheng5 an-ui3 peh-siN3, kong2, Lan2 tioh8 lip8-khek chiuN7-khi3 lai5 tit-tioh8 hit sou2-chai7; lan2 u7 kau3-giah8 e5 lat8 oe7 khah-iaN5 in.  31). Tok8-tok8 hiah-e5 kap i chiuN7-khi3 e5 lang5 kong2, Lan2 boe7-oe7 chiuN7-khi3 kong-kek hiah e5 peh-siN3; in-ui7 in pi2 lan2 khah iong2-chong3.  32). In hiah e5 lang5, lun7 sou2 thau-khoaN3 e5 toe7, tui3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 po3 phaiN2 siau-sit, kong2, Goan2 sou2 keng-ke3 thau-khoaN3 e5 toe7, si7 thun-chiah8 hiah e5 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 e5 toe7; goan2 ti7-hia sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 peh-siN3 long2 chin toa7-han3.  33). Goan2 ti7-hia khoaN3-kiN3 A-lap8 chok8 lang5, chiu7-si7 toa7-han3 lang5, in si7 toa7-han3 lang5 e5 hou7-e3; chiau3 goan2 khoaN3 ka-ki7 chhin-chhiuN7 chhau2-meh, chiau3 in khoaN3 goan2 ia7 si7 an2-ni.

[14]	Hoe7-chiong3 chiu7 chhut-siaN, toa7 au5-kio3; hit-mi5 peh-siN3 long2 thi5-khau3.  2). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 ai-oan3 Mou5-se A-lun5; hoe7-chiong3 tui3 in kong2, M7-tat8-tioh8 goan2 si2 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7! m7-tat8-tioh8 si2 ti7 chi2 khong3-ia2!  3). Ia5-ho5-hoa siaN2-su7 chhoa7 goan2 kau3 chit sou2-chai7, hou7 goan2 to2 ti7 to-e7 ah? Goan2 e5 bou2 kap kiaN2 beh siu7 liah8; goan2 to3-khi3 Ai-kip8 kiam2 bo5 khah-ho2 mah?  4). In saN-kap kong2, Lan2 tioh8 lip8 chit8 e5 siu2-leng2, to3--khi3 Ai-kip8.  5). Mou5-se A-lun5 chiu7 phak-loh8 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 choan5-hoe7 cheng3-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5.  6). Thau-khoaN3 toe7 e5 lang5 e5 tiong-kan, Lun3 e5 kiaN2 Iok-su-a, kap Ia5-hu-ni5 e5 kiaN2 Ka-lek8, thiah-lih8 in e5 saN;  7). tui3 I2-sek-liat8 choan5-hoe7 kong2, Goan2 sou2 keng-ke3 thau-khoaN3 e5 toe7, si7 kek8-ho2 e5 toe7.  8). Ia5-ho5-hoa na7 hoaN-hi2 lan2, chiu7 beh chhoa7 lan2 kau3 hit e5 toe7, chiong toe7 siuN2-su3 lan2; hit e5 toe7 si7 lau5 lin kap bit8 e5 toe7.  9). Chong2-si7 lin2 m7-thang poe7-poan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, ia7 boh8-tit kiaN hit sou2 -chai7 e5 peh-siN3, in-ui7 in si7 choe3 lan2 e5 chiah8-mih8; koh ti3-im3 in e5 i2-keng li7-khui in; koh u7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kap lan2 ti7-teh; m7 bian2 kiaN in.  10). Chong2-si7 choan5-hoe7 kong2, Eng7 chioh8-thau5 tim3-si2 in.  Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 eng5-kng ti7 hoe7-bou7 ng3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chhut-hian7.
	11). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Chit e5 peh-siN3 khoaN3-khin Goa2 beh kau3 ti7-si5 ah? Goa2 ti7 in tiong-kan kiaN5 che it-chhe3 e5 sin5-jiah, in iau2-ku2 m7-sin3 Goa2, beh kau3 ti7-si5?  12). Goa2 beh eng7 un-ek8 lai5 phah in, hou7 in boe7 tit-tioh8 seng5-chiap giap8; hou7 li2 chiaN5-choe3 toa7-kok, pi2 in khah-kiong5.  13). Mou5-se tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, An2-ni, Ai-kip8 lang5 beh thiaN-kiN3; in-ui7 Li2 eng7 Li2 e5 koan5-leng5, chhoa7 chiah e5 peh-siN3 tui3 in tiong-kan chiuN7-lai5.  14). In beh eng7 chiah e5 su7 ka7 chit sou2-chai7 khia7-khi2 e5 lang5 kong2.  In i2-keng thiaN-kiN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa Li2 ti7 chiah e5 peh-siN3 e5 tiong-kan; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa Li2 tng-bin7 hou7 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3, koh Li2 e5 hun5 theng5 ti7 in e5 teng2-bin7, Li2 jit8--si5 ti7 hun5-thiau7 tiong, mi5--si5 ti7 he2-thiau7 tiong, ti7 in e5 bin7-cheng5 kiaN5.  15). TaN Li2 na7 thai5-si2 chiah e5 peh-siN3, chhin-chhiuN7 thai5-si2 chit8-lang5, hiah e5 thiaN-kiN3 Li2 e5 mia5-siaN e5 liat8-kok beh gi7-lun7 kong2,  16). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa boe7-oe7 chhoa7 chiah e5 peh-siN3 jip8 I tui3 in chiu3-choa7 eng3-un2 e5 toe7, sou2-i2 ti7 khong3-ia2 thai5-si2 in.  17). TaN kiu5 Chu2 hian2-chhut toa7 koan5-leng5, chiau3 Li2 sou2 bat kong2 e5, kong2,  18). Ia5-ho5-hoa bo5 khoai3 siu7-khi3, koh u7 hong-seng7 e5 chu5-ai3, sia3-bian2 choe7-koa3 ke3-sit, koat-toan3 bo5 liah8 u7-choe7 e5 choe3 bo5 choe7, tek-khak kui-kiu7 i e5 choe7, tui3 pe7 kau3 kiaN2, kau3 saN-si3 tai7.  19). Kiu5 Li2 chiau3 Li2 e5 toa7 chu5-ai3 sia3-bian2 chit e5 peh-siN3 e5 choe7, chhin-chhiuN7 Li2 tui3 Ai-kip8 kau3 taN, siong5-siong5 sia3-bian2 in chit8-iuN7.  20). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 chiau3 li2 e5 oe7 u7 sia3-bian2 in.  21). Chong2-si7 Goa2 ki2 Goa2 e5 oah8-mia7 lai5 kong2, Pian3-toe7 beh chhiong-moa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 eng5-kng.  22). In-ui7 chiah e5 lang5 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 Goa2 e5 eng5-kng, i2-kip8 Goa2 sou2 kiaN5 ti7 Ai-kip8 kap khong3-ia2 e5 sin5-jiah, iau2-ku2 chhi3 Goa2 chap8-pai2, m7 thiaN-than3 Goa2 e5 oe7;  23). in koat-toan3 boe7 tit-tioh8 khoaN3-kiN3 Goa2 tui3 in e5 liat8-chou2 sou2 chiu3-choa7 eng3-un2 e5 toe7; hoan7-na7 khoaN3-khin Goa2-e5 long2 boe7 tit-tioh8 khoaN3-kiN3.  24). Tok8-tok8 Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 Ka-lek8, in-ui7 i leng7-goa7 u7 chit8 e5 sim-chi3, oan5-choan5 te3 Goa2, Goa2 beh chhoa7 i jip8 i sou2 kiaN5-kau3 e5 toe7, i e5 hou7-e3 ia7 beh tit-tioh8 hit e5 toe7 choe3 giap8.  25). A-ma2-lek8 lang5 kap Ka-lam5 lang5 tiam3 ti7 soaN-kok tiong; bin5-a2-jit8 lin2 tioh8 oat8-to3-tng2, tui3 Ang5-hai2 e5 lou7 khi3 khong3-ia2.
	26). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se A-lun5 kong2,  27). Chiah e5 phaiN2 e5 hoe7-chiong3 tui3 Goa2 hoat-chhut oan3-gian5, Goa2 thun-lun2 in beh kau3 ti7-si5 ah? I2-sek-liat8 lang5 ai-oan3 Goa2 e5 oan3-gian5, Goa2 long2 thiaN-kiN3 lah.  28). Tioh8 ka7 in kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 ki2 Goa2 e5 oah8-mia7 lai5 kong2, Lin2 hou7 Goa2 thiaN-kiN3 e5 oe7, Goa2 beh chiau3 an2-ni khoan2-thai7 lin2.  29). Lin2 e5 sin-si beh to2 ti7 chi2 khong3-ia2, kiN3-na7 lin2 tiong-kan ke3-sng3 e5 lang5, chiau3 i e5 siau3-giah8, tui3 ji7-chap8 he3 i2-chiuN7, tui3 Goa2 chhut oan3-gian5 e5,  30). tek-khak boe7 tit-tioh8 jip8 Goa2 chiu3-choa7 eng3-un2 lin2 khia7-khi2 e5 toe7; tok8-tok8 Ia5-hu-ni5 e5 kiaN2 Ka-lek8, kap Lun3 e5 kiaN2 Iok-su-a, beh jip8--khi3.  31). Chong2-si7 lin2 e5 gin2-a2, chiu7-si7 lin2 sou2 kong2 beh siu7-liah8 e5, Goa2 beh chhoa7 in jip8--khi3, in chiu7 chai lin2 sou2 khi3-sak hit e5 toe7.  32). Lun7-kau3 lin2, lin2 e5 sin-si beh to2 ti7 chi2 khong3-ia2.  33). Lin2 e5 kiaN2-ji5 beh ti7 khong3-ia2 phiau-liu5 si3-chap8 ni5, tam-tng lin2 im5-heng7 e5 choe7, tit8-kau3 lin2 e5 sin-si ti7 khong3-ia2 siau-biat8.  34). Chiau3 lin2 thau-khoaN3 hit e5 toe7 e5 jit8-chi2, kiong7 si3-chap8 jit8, chit8-jit8 ti2 chit8-ni5, lin2 tioh8 tam-tng choe7 si3-chap8 ni5; lin2 chiu7 chai Goa2 khi3-sak lin2.  35). Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa i2-keng kong2, Goa2 beh an2-ni khoan2-thai7 che it-chhe3 chu7-chip8 tui3-tek8 Goa2 e5 phaiN2 hoe7-chiong3; in beh ti7 chi2 khong3-ia2 siau-biat8, si2 ti7-chia.  36). Mou5-se sou2 chhe thau-khoaN3 hit e5 toe7, to3-tng2 lai5 po3 hit sou2-chai7 e5 phaiN2 siau-sit, ti3-kau3 choan5-hoe7 ai-oan3 i;  37). hiah e5 po3 hit sou2-chai7 phaiN2 siau-sit e5 lang5, long2 tu2-tioh8 un-ek8, si2 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5.  38). Thau-khoaN3 hit sou2-chai7 e5 lang5 e5 tiong-kan, chi2-u7 Lun3 e5 kiaN2 Iok-su-a, kap Ia5-hu-ni5 e5 kiaN2 Ka-lek8, iau2-ku2 oah8-teh.  39). Mou5-se chiong chiah e5 oe7 ka7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 cheng3-lang5 kong2, peh-siN3 chiu7 chin iu-bun7.  40). In cha2-cha2 khi2-lai5 chiuN7-khi3 soaN-teng2, kong2, KhoaN3 ah, goan2 ti7-chia, beh chiuN7-khi3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 eng3-un2 e5 toe7, in-ui7 goan2 u7 hoan7-choe7.  41). Mou5-se kong2, Lin2 siaN2-su7 ui5-poe7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 beng7-leng7 ah? chit e5 su7 boe7-oe7 heng-thong.  42). Boh8-tit chiuN7--khi3, in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa bo5 ti7 lin2 tiong-kan, kiaN-liau2 lin2 hou7 tui3-tek8 phah-pai7.  43). In-ui7 A-ma2-lek8 lang5, kap Ka-lam5 lang5, long2 ti7-hia ti7 lin2 e5 thau5-cheng5, lin2 beh to2 ti7 to-e7; in-ui7 lin2 oat8-thau5 bo5 te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa; sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa bo5 beh kap lin2 ti7-teh.  44). Chong2-si7 in chu7-choan chiuN7 soaN-teng2; na7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 iok-kui7 kap Mou5-se bo5 chhut-iaN5.  45). Tui3 an2-ni A-ma2-lek8 lang5, kap Ka-lam5 lang5, khia7-khi2 ti7 soaN--nih e5, long2 loh8-lai5 kong-kek in, phah-pai7 in, kau3 ti7 Ho5-jiN2-ma2.

[15]	Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  2). Li2 tioh8 hoan-hu3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5, ka7 in kong2, Lin2 na7 kau3 Goa2 sou2 siuN2-su3 lin2 khia7-khi2 e5 toe7,  3). na7 ai3 tui3 gu5-kun5 a2 iuN5-kun5 hian3-hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 he2-che3, chiu7-si7 sio-che3, a2-si7 pat8-ho7 e5 che3, beh sia7-goan7, a2-si7 choe3 hoaN-hi2 hian3 e5 che3, a2-si7 kau3 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 choeh-ki5, choe3 phang-phang hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa;  4). hit e5 hian3 le2-mih8 e5, tak8 chiah iuN5-a2 tioh8 phoe3 iu3 e5 mi7-hun2 i-hoat chap8-hun7-chit8, kap iu5 chit8-him si3-hun7-chit8, tiau-ho5 choe3 sou3-che3;  5). chiu2 ia7 tioh8 chit8-him si3-hun7 e5 chit8, lai5 choe3 koan3-tian7; bo5-lun7 sio-che3, a2-si7 pat8-mih8 che3, long2 tioh8 an2-ni lai5 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  6). Ui7-tioh8 mi5-iuN5-kang2, li2 tioh8 pi7-pan7 iu3 e5 mi7-hun2 i-hoat chap8-hun7-nng7, kap iu5 chit8-him saN-hun7-chit8, tiau-ho5 choe3 sou3-che3;  7). koh eng7 chiu2 chit8-him saN-hun7-chit8 choe3 koan3-tian7-che3, choe3 phang-phang lai5 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  8). Li2 na7 pi7-pan7 gu5-kang2-a2 choe3 sio-che3, a2-si7 pat8-ho7 e5 che3, lai5 sia7-goan7, a2-si7 choe3 sia7-un-che3, lai5 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa,  9). chiu7-si7 eng7 iu3 e5 mi7-hun2 i-hoat chap8-hun7-saN, kap iu5 poaN3-him, tiau-ho5 choe3 sou3-che3, kap gu5-kang2-a2 saN-kap hian3;  10). koh eng7 chiu2 poaN3-him choe3 koan3-tian7 e5 che3, hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 phang-phang e5 he2-che3.  11). Hek8-si7 ui7-tioh8 chit8-chiah gu5-kang2, a2-si7 chit8-chiah mi5-iuN5-kang2, a2-si7 chit8-chiah mi5-iuN5-a2, a2-si7 soaN-iuN5-a2, long2 tioh8 an2-ni choe3.  12). Chiau3 lin2 sou2 pi7-pan7 e5 siau3-giah8, chiau3 tak8-chiah e5 giah8-siau3, long2 tioh8 an2-ni choe3.  13). KiN3-na7 pun2-toe7 lang5, chiong phang-phang e5 he2-che3 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, long2 tioh8 an2-ni choe3 chiah e5 tai7-chi3.  14).
