Na7 u7 goa7-bin7 lang5 chhut-goa7 ti7 lin2 tiong-kan, a2-si7 tak8 se3-tai7 u7 lang5 khia7-khi2 ti7 lin2 tiong-kan, beh hian3 he2-che3, phang-phang ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, lin2 an2-ni kiaN5, in ia7 tioh8 an2-ni kiaN5.  15). Lun7 hoe7-chiong3, lin2 kap khia7-khi2 ti7 lin2 tiong-kan e5 chhut-goa7 lang5, long2 tang5-chit8-iuN7 e5 le7, choe3 lin2 tak8 se3-tai7 eng2-oan2 e5 le7, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5; lin2 an2-ni, chhut-goa7 lang5 ia7 tioh8 an2-ni.  16). Lin2 kap goa7-bin7 lang5 chhut-goa7 ti7 lin2 tiong-kan e5, tioh8 tang5-chit8-iuN7 e5 le7, chit8-iuN7 e5 hoat-tou7.
	17). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  18). Li2 tioh8 hoan-hu3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 ka7 in kong2, Lin2 kau3 Goa2 sou2 chhoa7 lin2 jip8--khi3 hit e5 toe7.  19). chiah8 hit sou2-chai7 e5 bi2-niu5, chiu7 tioh8 hian3 ku2-che3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  20). Lin2 tioh8 eng7 khi2-thau5 sek8 e5 beh8-hun2 chhong3 piaN2, hian3 choe3 ku2-che3; lin2 ku2-khi2, chhin-chhiuN7 ku2-khi2 gou7-kak-tiuN5 e5 gou7-kak chit8-iuN7.  21). Lin2 tak8 se3-tai7 tioh8 eng7 lin2 khi2-thau5-sek8 e5 beh8-hun2, choe3 ku2-che3, hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
	22). Lin2 u7 chho3-gou7 e5 si5, bo5 siu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3 Mou5-se chiah e5 it-chhe3 e5 beng7-leng7,  23). chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa thok Mou5-se it-chhe3 sou2 beng7-leng7 lin2 e5, tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa beng7-leng7 lin2 e5 jit8, kau3 ti7 lin2 e5 tak8 se3-tai7,  24). na7 u7 chho3-gou7 kiaN5, hoe7-chiong3 ia7 m7-chai, au7-lai5 hoe7-chiong3 tioh8 hian3 chit8 chiah gu5-kang2-a2 choe3 sio-che3, ia7 chiau3 hoat-tou7 eng7 i e5 sou3-che3, kap koan3-tian7 e5 che3, saN-kap choe3 phang-phang, hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa; koh tioh8 hian3 chit8 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2 choe3 siok8-choe7 e5 che3.  25). Che3-si tioh8 ui7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 hoe7-chiong3 siok8-choe7, in chiu7 tit-tioh8 sia3-bian2; in-ui7 che si7 chho3-gou7, in ia7 in-ui7 in e5 chho3-gou7, toa3 in e5 le2-mih8, chiu7-si7 hian3-hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 he2-che3, kap siok8-choe7-che3, long2 toa3 kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5;  26). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 hoe7-chiong3, kap kia3-kha ti7 in tiong-kan e5 goa7-lang5, chiu7 beh tit-tioh8 sia3-bian2; in-ui7 chit e5 choe7 si7 peh-siN3 chho3-gou7 hoan7 e5.
	27). Na7 u7 chit8-lang5 chho3-gou7 hoan7-choe7, i chiu7 tioh8 hian3 be7-moa2-ni5 e5 soaN-iuN5-bu2 choe3 siok8-choe7-che3.  28). Hit e5 chho3-gou7 kiaN5 e5 lang5 ti7 i chho3-gou7 hoan7-choe7 e5 si5, che3-si tioh8 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 ka7 i siok8-choe7; ka7 i siok8-choe7, i chiu7 beh tit-tioh8 sia3-bian2.  29). I2-sek-liat8 tiong e5 pun2-toe7 lang5, kap kia3-kha ti7 in tiong-kan e5 chhut-goa7 lang5, na7 chho3-gou7 kiaN5 sim2-mih8 su7, tioh8 tang5 chit8 e5 le7.  30). Chong2-si7 hit e5 chu7-choan kiaN5 tai7-chi3 e5, bo5-lun7 si7 pun2-toe7 lang5, a2-si7 kia3-kha-e5, i siat-tok8 Ia5-ho5-hoa, tioh8 tui3 i e5 peh-siN3-tiong chian2-tu5 khi3.  31). In-ui7 i biau2-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7, poe7-gek8 I e5 beng7-leng7, hit-lang5 tioh8 it-chin7 chian2-tu5; i e5 choe7-koa3 beh kui ti7 i.
	32). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 ti7 khong3-ia2 e5 si5, tu2-tioh8 chit8-lang5 ti7 an-hioh-jit8 khioh-chha5.  33). Hiah e5 tu2-tioh8 hit e5 khioh-chha5 e5 lang5, toa3 i kau3 Mou5-se, A-lun5, kap hoe7-chiong3 hia.  34). In chiu7 ka7 i koaiN-kim3, in-ui7 iau2-be7 chi2-beng5 tioh8 chaiN2-iuN7 pan7 i.  35). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Hit-lang5 tek-khak tioh8 hou7 i si2, hoe7-chiong3 tioh8 ti7 iaN5-goa7 eng7 chioh8-thau5 tim3 i.  36). Hoe7-chiong3 chhoa7 hit-lang5 chhut iaN5-goa7, eng7 chioh8-thau5 tim3 i kau3 si2; si7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beng7-leng7 Mou5-se e5.
	37). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  38). Li2 tioh8 hoan-hu3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 ka7 in kong2, hou7 in tai7-tai7 ti7 saN-a2-kiN5 choe3 chhiu, koh ti7 e7-toe2 piN e5 chhiu-teng2, tio3 chit8 tiau5 lam5-sek e5 iu3-toa3.  39). Beh ka7 lin2 choe3 chhiu, hou7 lin2 khoaN3-kiN3, thang ki3--tit Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 beng7-leng7 lai5 kiaN5 i, bian2-tit lin2 hong3-chhiong3 ka-ki7 e5 sim-i3, ka-ki7 e5 bak8-chiu, lai5 kiaN5 im5-heng7, chhin-chhiuN7 lin2 peng5-sou3 sou2 kiaN5-e5 chit8-iuN7;  40). hou7 lin2 ki3--tit lai5 kiaN5 Goa2 it-chhe3 e5 beng7-leng7, chiaN5-choe3 seng3 kui lin2 e5 Siong7-te3.  41). Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3, chhoa7 lin2 chhut Ai-kip8 toe7, beh choe3 lin2 e5 Siong7-te3; Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin2 e5 Siong7-te3.

[16]	Li7-bi7 e5 cheng-sun, Ko-hat e5 sun, I2-su-hap e5 kiaN2 Kho2-lah8, kap Liu5-pian7 e5 kiaN2-sun-tiong I2-li7-ap e5 kiaN2 Tai7-tan, A-pi2-lan5, kap Pi2-lek8 e5 kiaN2 An,  2). kiat chit8-tong2, kap I2-sek-liat8 tiong e5 lang5, chiu7-si7 hoe7-tiong e5 siu2-leng2 nng7-pah gou7-chap8 lang5, si7 u7 beng5-bong7 siu7 keng2-tiau3 hu3-hoe7 e5 lang5, saN-kap khi2-lai5 ti7 Mou5-se e5 bin7-cheng5.  3). In chu7-chip8 kong-kek Mou5-se A-lun5 kong2, Lin2 chhiam3-koan5, choan5-hoe7 tak8-lang5 long2 si7 seng3, Ia5-ho5-hoa ia7 ti7 in tiong-kan; lin2 siaN2-su7 chu7-ko poaN5-ke3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 hoe7-chiong3 ah?  4). Mou5-se thiaN-kiN3 chit e5 oe7 chiu7 phak ti7 toe7--nih,  5). tui3 Kho2-lah8 kap i e5 choan5-tong2 e5 lang5 kong2, Kau3 bin5-a2-cha2-khi2, Ia5-ho5-hoa beh chi2-si7 sim2-mih8 lang5 si7 siok8 I e5, sim2-mih8 lang5 si7 seng3, chiu7 beh hou7 hit-lang5 chhin-kun7 I; I sou2 keng2-soan2 e5 lang5 beh hou7 in chhin-kun7 I.  6). Lin2 tioh8 an2-ni kiaN5; Kho2-lah8 kap i e5 tong2, tioh8 theh8 hiuN-lou5;  7). bin5-a2-jit8 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, eng7 he2 toe2 ti7 hi2 lai7-bin7, he7 hiuN ti7 hit teng2-bin7; Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 keng2 e5 lang5, i beh choe3 seng3; lin2 Li7-bi7 e5 kiaN2-sun chhiam3-koan5 lah.  8). Mou5-se koh tui3 Kho2-lah8 kong2, Li7-bi7 e5 kiaN2-sun ah, lin2 tioh8 thiaN;  9). I2-sek-liat8 e5 Siong7-te3, tui3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 hoe7-tiong hun-piat lin2, hou7 lin2 chhin-kun7 I, pan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa hoe7-bou7 e5 su7, ia7 khia7 ti7 hoe7-chiong3 e5 bin7-cheng5 lai5 choe3 in e5 chhe-eng7.  10). I koh hou7 li2, kap li2 long2-chong2 e5 hiaN-ti7 Li7-bi7 e5 kiaN2-sun, saN-kap chhin-kun7 I, lin2 liah8 che choe3 sio2-khoa2 mah? Lin2 iau2-ku2 iau-kiu5 che3-si e5 chit mah?  11). Sou2-i2 li2 kap li2 e5 tong2 chu7-chip8, si7 teh kong-kek Ia5-ho5-hoa; A-lun5 si7 sim2-mih8, lin2 keng2-jian5 ai-oan3 i ah?
	12). Mou5-se chhe lang5 khi3 kio3 I2-li7-ap e5 kiaN2 Tai7-tan, A-pi2-lan5; in kong2, Goan2 m7 chiuN7-khi3;  13). li2 chhoa7 goan2 tui3 siong5-siong5 lau5 lin kap bit8 e5 toe7 chiuN7--lai5, beh ti7 khong3-ia2 thai5-si2 goan2, che kiam2 si7 sio2-khoa2, li2 iau2-ku2 beh ka-ki7 siat-lip8 choe3 jin5-kun lai5 koan2-hat goan2 mah?  14). Koh li2 bo5-iaN2 chhoa7 goan2 kau3 lau5 lin kap bit8 e5 toe7, ia7 bo5 eng7 chhan5-hng5, kap phu5-to5-hng5, hou7 goan2 choe3 giap8; chong2 bo5 li2 beh iah chiah e5 lang5 e5 bak8-chiu mah? Goan2 bo5 beh chiuN7-khi3.  15). Mou5-se siu7-khi3 kau3-kek8, tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Kiu5 Li2 boh8-tit kam3-lap8 in sou2 hian3 e5; goa2 peng7 bo5 khan in chit8 chiah lu5, ia7 bo5 hai7 in chit8-lang5.  16). Mou5-se tui3 Kho2-lah8 kong2, Li2 kap li2 e5 tong2 hiah e5 lang5, kap A-lun5, bin5-a2-jit8 long2 tioh8 lai5 khia7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5.  17). Lin2 tak8-lang5 toa3 i e5 hiuN-lou5, kiong7 nng7-pah gou7-chap8 e5, he7 hiuN ti7 hi2 teng2-bin7, tak8-lang5 toa3 i e5 hiuN-lou5 kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5; li2 kap A-lun5 ia7 kok toa3 ka-ki7 e5 hiuN-lou5.  18). Tui3 an2-ni in tak8-lang5 theh8 i e5 hiuN-lou5, toe2 he2 ti7 hi2 lai7-bin7, he7 hiuN ti7 hit teng2-bin7, kap Mou5-se A-lun5 khia7 ti7 hoe7-bou7 mng5-khau2.  19). Kho2-lah8 chio-chip hoe7-chiong3 kau3 hoe7-bou7 mng5-khau2, kong-kek in; Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 eng5-kng hian2-hian7 ti7 hoe7-chiong3.
	20). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se A-lun5 kong2,  21). Lin2 tioh8 li7-khui chit e5 hoe7-tiong, Goa2 thang ti7 chit8-bak8-nih-ku2 e5 tiong-kan chau5-biat8 in.  22). In chiu7 phak ti7 toe7--nih, kong2, Siong7-te3 ah, siuN2-su3 oah8-mia7 hou7 kiN3-na7 u7 jiok8-the2--e5 e5 Siong7-te3 ah, chit8-lang5 hoan7-choe7, Li2 chiu7 beh siu7-khi3 choan5-hoe7 mah?  23). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  24). Li2 tioh8 hoan-hu3 hoe7-chiong3 tui3 in kong2, Lin2 tioh8 li7-khui Kho2-lah8, Tai7-tan, A-pi2-lan5 pou3-piN5 e5 si3-ui5.  25). Mou5-se khi2-lai5 khi3 Tai7-tan, A-pi2-lan5 hia, I2-sek-liat8 e5 tiuN2-lo2 ia7 te3 i khi3.  26). I hoan-hu3 hoe7-chiong3 kong2, Lin2 tioh8 li7-khui chiah e5 phaiN2-lang5 e5 pou3-piN5. in e5 mih8-kiaN7 long2 m7-thang bong, kiaN-liau2 lin2 ia7 siu7 biat8 ti7 in e5 choe7-tiong.  27). In chiu7 li7-khui Kho2-lah8, Tai7-tan, A-pi2-lan5 pou3-piN5 e5 si3-ui5; Tai7-tan, A-pi2-lan5 kap in e5 bou2, in e5 kiaN2, in e5 soe3-kiaN2, long2 chhut-lai5 khia7 ti7 in ka-ki7 e5 pou3-piN5 mng5-khau2.  28). Mou5-se kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa chhe Goa2 kiaN5 che it-chhe3 e5 su7, lin2 tui3 an2-ni thang chai, in-ui7 goa2 m7-si7 chu7-choan lai5 kiaN5.  29). Siat-su2 chiah e5 lang5 si2 chhin-chhiuN7 peng5-siong5 lang5 si2, in sou2 tu2-tioh8 chhin-chhiuN7 peng5-siong5 lang5 sou2 tu2-tioh8, chiu7 Ia5-ho5-hoa bo5 chhe goa2.  30). Siat-su2 Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 chit8-hang7 sin e5 su7, hou7 toe7 khui-chhui3, chiong in kap it-chhe3 siok8 in-e5 long2 thun--loh8-khi3, hou7 in oah8-oah8 tui7-loh8 im-kan, lin2 chiu7 chai chiah e5 lang5 si7 biau2-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  31). Chiah e5 oe7 i tu2-a2 kong2 soah, in e7-bin7 e5 toe7 chiu7 lih8-khui.  32). Toe7 chiu7 khui-chhui3, chiong in kap in e5 ke-koan3, i2-kip8 it-chhe3 siok8 Kho2-lah8 e5 jin5-teng chai5-but8, long2 thun--loh8-khi3.  33). Hiah e5 lang5 kap it-chhe3 siok8 in-e5, long2 oah8-oah8 loh8 im-kan; toe7 chiu7 koh hap8-oa2 ti7 in e5 teng2-bin7, in chiu7 tui3 hoe7-tiong biat8-bo5.  34). Ti7 in si3-ui5 e5 I2-sek-liat8 lang5, thiaN-kiN3 in au5-kio3, chiu7 long2 to5-chau2 kong2, KiaN-liau2 toe7 ia7 ka7 lan2 thun--loh8-khi3.  35). Koh u7 he2 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa hia chhut, thun-biat8 hiah e5 hian3-hiuN e5 nng7-pah gou7-chap8 lang5.
	36). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  37). Li2 tioh8 hoan-hu3 che3-si A-lun5 e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-a-sat, tui3 he2-tiong khioh hiah e5 hiuN-lou5 khi2-lai5, phah-soaN3 ti7-hia e5 he2; in-ui7 hiah e5 hiuN-lou5 i2-keng si7 seng3.  38). Eng7 hiah e5 hoan7-choe7 hai7 ka-ki7 e5 siN3-mia7 e5 lang5 e5 hiuN-lou5, tui5 choe3 kui-phiN3, lai5 an che3-toaN5; in-ui7 in hian3 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, sou2-i2 si7 seng3--e5, thang hou7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 choe3 kam3-kai3.  39). Che3-si I2-li7-a-sat chiu7 theh8 hiah e5 lang5 sou2 hian3 e5 tang5-lou5, tui5 choe3 kui-phiN3, lai5 an che3-toaN5, hou7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 choe3 kam3-kai3;  40). hou7 goa7-bin7 lang5, m7-si7 siok8 A-lun5 e5 hou7-e3 e5, boe7 thang oa2-kun7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lai5 sio-hiuN, bian2-tit in chhin-chhiuN7 Kho2-lah8 kap i e5 tong2; che si7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa thok Mou5-se sou2 beng7-leng7 e5.
	41). Keh-jit8 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 choan5-hoe7 long2 ai-oan3 Mou5-se A-lun5, kong2, Lin2 hai7-si2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 peh-siN3.  42). Hoe7-chiong3 chu7-chip8 kong-kek Mou5-se A-lun5 e5 si5, ng3 hoe7-bou7 khoaN3, khoaN3 ah, u7 hun5 kham3 i, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 eng5-kng hian2-hian7.  43). Mou5-se A-lun5 chiu7 kau3 hoe7-bou7 cheng5.  44). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  45). Lin2 tioh8 li7-khui chit e5 hoe7-tiong, hou7 Goa2 thang ti7 chit8-bak8-nih-ku2 e5 tiong-kan biat8-bo5 in; in nng7-lang5 chiu7 phak ti7 toe7--nih.  46). Mou5-se tui3 A-lun5 kong2, Theh8 hit e5 hiuN-lou5, eng7 toaN5-teng2 e5 he2 toe2 ti7 hi2 tiong-kan, he7 hiuN ti7 hi2 teng2-bin7, kin2-kin2 toa3 kau3 hoe7-chiong3 hia, ka7 in siok8-choe7; in-ui7 u7 toa7 siu7-khi3 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa chhut, un-ek8 i2-keng hoat-choh.  47). A-lun5 chiau3 Mou5-se sou2-kong2-e5 theh8-lai5, chau2 kau3 hoe7-tiong; khoaN3 ah, un-ek8 i2-keng hoat ti7 peh-siN3-tiong, i chiu7 he7 hiuN, ka7 peh-siN3 siok8-choe7.  48). I khia7 ti7 oah8-lang5 si2-lang5 e5 tiong-kan, un-ek8 chiu7 soah.  49). Tu5--khi3 in-ui7 Kho2-lah8 e5 tai7-chi3 si2-e5 i2-goa7, tu2-tioh8 un-ek8 si2 e5, kiong7 u7 chit8-ban7 si3-chheng chhit-pah lang5.  50). A-lun5 to3--lai5 kau3 Mou5-se hia, kau3 hoe7-bou7 mng5, un-ek8 chiah soah.

[17]	Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  2). Li2 ka7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kong2, tui3 in kiah8 koaiN2-a2, tak8 chi-phai3 chit8-ki, chiu7-si7 tui3 hiah e5 chi-phai3 e5 siu2-leng2, kiong7 kiah8 chap8-ji7 ki; li2 sia2 tak8-lang5 e5 mia5 ti7 i e5 koaiN2-a2.  3). Ti7 Li7-bi7 hit-ki koaiN2-a2 tioh8 sia2 A-lun5 e5 mia5; in-ui7 tak8 chi-phai3 e5 thau5-lang5 long2 u7 chit8 ki koaiN2-a2.  4). Li2 tioh8 chiong hiah-e5 he7 ti7 hoe7-bou7-lai7 hoat-kui7 e5 thau5-cheng5, chiu7-si7 Goa2 kap lin2 siong-hoe7 e5 sou2-chai7.  5). Goa2 sou2 keng2 hit-lang5, i e5 koaiN2-a2 beh puh-ge5; an2-ni Goa2 beh hou7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 ai-oan3 e5 oe7, chiu7-si7 in sou2 ai-oan3 lin2 e5 oe7, long2 soah, bo5 koh hou7 Goa2 thiaN-kiN3.  6). Mou5-se chiu7 ka7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kong2; in e5 siu2-leng2 chiu7 eng7 koaiN2-a2 kau hou7 i, chiau3 in e5 chi-phai3 chit8 e5 siu2-leng2 chit8-ki, kiong7 chap8-ji7 ki koaiN2-a2; A-lun5 e5 koaiN2-a2 ia7 ti7 hiah e5 koaiN2-a2 e5 tiong-kan.  7). Mou2-se chiu7 chiong hiah e5 koaiN2-a2 he7 ti7 hoat-kui7 e5 pou3-piN5-lai7, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5.  8). Bin5-a2-jit8 Mou5-se jip8-khi3 hoat-kui7 e5 pou3-piN5; khoaN3 ah, siok8 Li7-bi7 e5 ke, A-lun5 e5 koaiN2-a2, i2-keng puh-ge5, siN hoe-m5, khui-hoe, kiat-chiaN5 heng7-jin5.  9). Mou5-se tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 kiah8 hiah e5 koaiN2-a2 chhut-lai5, kau3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 cheng3-lang5 hia; in khoaN3-kiN3 tak8-lang5 kiah8 in e5 koaiN2-a2.  10). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Eng7 A-lun5 e5 koaiN2-a2 iu5-goan5 he7 ti7 hoat-kui7 cheng5, lau5-teh, choe3 chiah e5 poe7-gek8 e5 lang5 e5 kam3-kai3; an2-ni li2 chiu7 hou7 in tui3 Goa2 ai-oan3 e5 oe7 soah, bian2-tit in si2-bo5.  11). Mou5-se an2-ni kiaN5, si7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beng7-leng7-e5 lai5 kiaN5.
	12). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tui3 Mou5-se kong2, KhoaN3 ah, goan2 si2 lah, goan2 biat8-bo5 lah, long2 biat8-bo5 lah.  13). KiN3-na7 oa2-kun7, chiu7-si7 oa2-kun7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 hoe7-bou7 e5, long2 si2; goan2 beh long2-chong2 si2 mah?

[18]	Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 A-lun5 kong2, Li2 kap li2 chiah e5 kiaN2, kap li2 e5 pun2-chok8, tioh8 saN-kap tam-tng seng3-sou2 e5 choe7; li2 kap li2 chiah e5 kiaN2 ia7 tioh8 tam-tng lin2 che3-si-chit e5 choe7.  2). Li2 tioh8 chhoa7 li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 Li7-bi7 e5 chi-phai3, li2 e5 chou2-kong e5 chi-phai3, chin3-cheng5 lai5, hou7 in kap li2 lian5-hap8 lai5 su-hau7 li2; na7-si7 li2 kap li2 e5 kiaN2, long2 tioh8 ti7 hoat-kui7 e5 hoe7-bou7-cheng5.  3). In tioh8 choe3 li2 e5 chhe-eng7, ia7 tioh8 choe3 Pou3-piN5 e5 chhe-eng7; tok8-tok8 m7-thang kun7 seng3-sou2 e5 khi3-ku7 kap toaN5, bian2-tit in kap lin2 long2 si2.  4). In tioh8 kap li2 lian5-hap8, ia7 tioh8 choe3 hoe7-bou7 e5 chhe-eng7, liau7-li2 Pou3-piN5 long2-chong2 e5 kang; tok8-tok8 goa7-bin7 lang5 m7-thang oa2-kun7 lin2.  5). Lin2 tioh8 choe3 seng3-sou2 e5 chhe-eng7, kap toaN5 e5 chhe-eng7, bian2-tit siu7-khi3 koh kau3 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5.  6). Goa2, khoaN3 ah, Goa2 bat tui3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 tiong-kan keng2 lin2 e5 hiaN-ti7 Li7-bi7 lang5 lai5 siuN2-su3 lin2, kap kui Ia5-ho5-hoa, lai5 liau7-li2 hoe7-bou7 e5 kang.  7). Sou2-i2 li2 kap li2 e5 kiaN2 tioh8 saN-kap siu2 che3-si e5 chit, liau7-li2 toaN5 kap tiuN3-li5-lai7 it-chhe3 e5 kang; lin2 tioh8 an2-ni hok8-bu7; Goa2 i2-keng siuN2-su3 li2 che3-si e5 chit-jim7 e5 kang, chhin-chhiuN7 sang3 mih8; kiN3-na7 goa7-bin7 lang5 kun7-oa2-e5, tek-khak hou7 i si2.
	8). Ia5-ho5-hoa koh ka7 A-lun5 kong2, Goa2, khoaN3 ah, Goa2 i2-keng eng7 hian3 hou7 Goa2 e5 ku2-che3, chiu7-si7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 hun-piat choe3-seng3 e5 mih8, kau li2 siu2 i; in-ui7 li2 siu7 boah-iu5, chiah e5 mih8 kui li2 kap li2 e5 kiaN2-sun, choe3 eng2-oan2 e5 hun7-giah8.  9). Bo5 keng-ke3 he2, chi3-seng3 e5 mih8 e5 tiong-kan, siok8 ti7 li2-e5 si7 chiah-e5:  kiN3-na7 in e5 le2-mih8, in e5 sou3-che3, in e5 siok8-choe7-che3, in e5 pou2-ke3-sit-che3, in sou2 hian3 hou7 Goa2 e5, long2 choe3 chi3-seng3, kui hou7 li2 kap li2 e5 kiaN2-sun.  10). Li2 tioh8 khoaN3 chiah-e5 choe3 chi3-seng3 lai5 chiah8 i; kiN3-na7 ta-pou-teng long2 thang chiah8; li2 tioh8 liah8 chit e5 mih8 choe3-seng3.  11). Chiah-e5 ia7 si7 li2 e5, le2-mih8 e5 ku2-che3, i2-kip8 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 sou2 hian3 e5 io5-che3, Goa2 long2 siuN2-su3 li2, kap li2 e5 kiaN2, cha-bou2-kiaN2, choe3 eng2-oan2 e5 hun7-giah8; kiN3-na7 ti7 li2 ke-tiong chheng-khi3 e5 lang5 long2 thang chiah8.  12). Siong7-ho2 e5 iu5, siong7-ho2 e5 chiu2, siong7-ho2 e5 gou7-kak, chiu7-si7 in khi2-thau5-sek8 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5, Goa2 long2 siuN2-su3 li2.  13). In e5 toe7 khi2-thau5-sek8 e5 mih8, sou2 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5, long2 kui hou7 li2; li2 ke-lai7 chheng-khi3 e5 lang5 long2 thang chiah8.  14). I2-sek-liat8 tiong kiN3-na7 siu7 hun-piat hian3-chin7 e5, long2 tioh8 kui hou7 li2.  15). KiN3-na7 u7 jiok8-the2 thau5-chiuN7-siN-e5, bo5-lun7 lang5 a2-si7 cheng-siN, in sou2 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5, long2 kui ti7 li2; tok8-tok8 lang5 thau5-chiuN7-siN-e5 li2 tioh8 siok8 i; bo5 chheng-khi3 e5 cheng-siN thau5-chiuN7-siN-e5, li2 ia7 tioh8 siok8 i.  16). Ti7 moa2-geh8 i2-goa7 sou2 tioh8 siok8 e5, tioh8 chiau3 li2 sou2 kou2 e5 ke3, chiau3 seng3-sou2 e5 sia3-khek-lek8, eng7 gun5 gou7 sia3-khek-lek8 siok8-hoe5 i; chit8 sia3-khek-lek8 si7 ji7-chap8 kui3-lah8.  17). Tok8-tok8 thau5-chiuN7-siN e5 gu5, thau5-chiuN7-siN e5 mi5-iuN5, thau5-chiuN7-siN e5 soaN-iuN5, li2 m7-thang siok8; che si7 seng3, tioh8 hiu3 i e5 huih ti7 toaN5--nih, tioh8 sio i e5 iu5 choe3 he2-che3, choe3 phang-phang hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  18). Hiah e5 bah kui ti7 li2, chhin-chhiuN7 sou2 io5 e5 heng kap chiaN3-thui2 kui ti7 li2 chit8-iuN7.  19). KiN3-na7 seng3-mih8 e5 ku2-che3, si7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5, Goa2 long2 siuN2-su3 li2, kap li2 e5 kiaN2, cha-bou2-kiaN2, choe3 eng2-oan2 tit-tioh8 e5 hun7-giah8; che si7 hou7 li2 kap li2 e5 hou7-e3, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, choe3 eng2-oan2 boe7-hoe3 e5 iok.  20). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 A-lun5 kong2, Li2 ti7 in e5 toe7-hng m7-thang u7 san2-giap8, ti7 in e5 tiong-kan ia7 m7-thang u7 hun7-giah8; ti7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tiong Goa2 chiu7-si7 li2 e5 hun7-giah8, si7 li2 e5 san2-giap8.
	21). KhoaN3 ah, ti7 I2-sek-liat8 tiong sou2 thiu e5 chap8-hun7-chit8, Goa2 i2-keng siuN2-su3 Li7-bi7 e5 kiaN2-sun choe3 giap8; in-ui7 in sou2 choe3 e5 kang si7 hoe7-bou7 e5 kang, sou2-i2 siuN2-su3 in, lai5 po3-tap in e5 tioh8-boa5.  22). Tui3 taN i2-au7, I2-sek-liat8 lang5 m7-thang oa2-kun7 hoe7-bou7, bian2-tit in tam-tng choe7 lai5 si2.  23). Tok8-tok8 Li7-bi7 lang5 tioh8 choe3 hoe7-bou7 e5 kang, tam-tng in e5 choe7; che beh choe3 lin2 tak8 se3-tai7 eng2-oan2 e5 le7; in ti7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 tiong-kan m7-thang u7 san2-giap8.  24). In-ui7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 sou2 thiu e5 chap8-hun7-chit8, sou2 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 ku2-che3 e5, Goa2 i2-keng siuN2-su3 Li7-bi7 lang5 choe3-giap8; sou2-i2 Goa2 tui3 in kong2, in ti7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 tiong-kan m7-thang u7 san2-giap8.
	25). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  26). Li2 tioh8 hoan-hu3 Li7-bi7 lang5 ka7 in kong2, Lin2 tui3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 tiong-kan thiu chap8-hun7-chit8, chiu7-si7 Goa2 hou7 lin2 choe3 giap8 e5; hit-si5 lin2 tioh8 tui3 hit e5 chap8-hun7-chit8 e5 tiong-kan koh thiu chap8-hun7-chit8, choe3 ku2-che3, hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  27). Li2 e5 ku2-che3 beh ka7 lin2 sng3 choe3 gou7-kak-tiuN5 e5 beh8, kap moa2 ti7 phu5-to5-khut e5 chiu2.  28). An2-ni, lin2 tui3 I2-sek-liat8 tiong sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 chap8-hun7-chit8, tioh8 tui3 hit-e5 hian3 ku2-che3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa; lin2 tioh8 tui3 hit-e5, eng7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 ku2-che3 hou7 che3-si A-lun5.  29). Lin2 sou2 tit-tioh8 it-chhe3 e5 le2-mih8, tioh8 tui3 hit tiong-kan, chiong te7-it ho2-e5, chiu7-si7 hun-piat choe3-seng3 e5 hun7-giah8, hian3 hiah e5 ku2-che3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  30). Sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 tui3 in kong2, Lin2 i2-keng tui3 hit tiong-kan ku2-khi2 hit e5 chi3-ho2-e5, che chiu7-si7 ka7 Li7-bi7 lang5 sng3 choe3 gou7-kak-tiuN5 e5 ngou2-kok, ia7 chhin-chhiuN7 chiu2-khut e5 chiu2.  31). Lin2 kap lin2 e5 ke-koan3, tak8 sou2-chai7 thang chiah8 i; che si7 lin2 e5 kang-chiN5, si7 po3-tap lin2 ti7 hoe7-bou7-lai7 sou2 choe3 e5 kang.  32). Lin2 i2-keng tui3 hit tiong-kan ku2-khi2 hit e5 chi3-ho2-e5, chiu7 bo5 in-ui7 an2-ni lai5 hoan7-choe7; lin2 m7-thang phah la5-sam5 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 seng3-mih8, bian2-tit lin2 si2-bo5.

[19]	Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se A-lun5 kong2,  2). Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beng7-leng7 lut8-hoat e5 tiau5-le7 si7 an2-ni kong2, Li2 tioh8 hoan-hu3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 eng7 chit8-chiah sun5-choan5 bo5 ha5-chhu5, be7-bat koa3-taN, chhiah-sek e5 gu5-bu2, khan kau3 li2 chia.  3). Li2 tioh8 chiong i kau hou7 che3-si I2-li7-a-sat, thang toa3 chhut iaN5-goa7; lang5 chiu7 thai5 gu5 ti7 i e5 bin7-cheng5.  4). Che3-si I2-li7-a-sat tioh8 eng7 chng2-thau5-a2 theh8 i e5 huih tam7-poh8, ng3 hoe7-bou7-cheng5 hiu3 huih chhit-pai2.  5). Tioh8 u7 chit8-lang5 ti7 che3-si e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5, sio bu2 e5 gu5-a2, chiu7-si7 sio i e5 phe5, i e5 bah, i e5 huih, i e5 pun3.  6). Che3-si tioh8 chiong pek-hiuN-chha5, giu5-chhek-chhau2, chu-ang5-sek mi5, long2 hiat ti7 sio gu5 e5 he2-tiong.  7). Che3-si tioh8 soe2 i e5 saN, eng7 chui2 soe2 seng-khu, jian5-au7 jip8 iaN5; che3-si beh bo5 chheng-khi3 kau3 e5-hng.  8). Sio gu5-a2 e5 lang5 tioh8 eng7 chui2 soe2 i e5 saN, eng7 chui2 soe2 seng-khu, beh bo5 chheng-khi3 kau3 e5-hng.  9). Tioh8 u7 chit8 e5 chheng-khi3 e5 lang5 siu-sip8 gu5-bu2 e5 hu, he7 ti7 iaN5-goa7 chheng-khi3 e5 sou2-chai7, lau5-teh choe3 I2-sek-liat8 hoe7-chiong3 tu5 khi3 la5-sam5 e5 chui2; che ia7-si7 tu5-khi3 choe7.  10). Siu-sip8 gu5-bu2 e5 hu e5 lang5 tioh8 soe2 i e5 saN, beh bo5 chheng-khi3 kau3 e5-hng; che beh hou7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kap kia3-kha ti7 in tiong-kan e5 goa7-lang5 choe3 eng2-oan2 e5 le7.  11). Bong--tioh8 lang5 e5 sin-si e5, chiu7 beh chhit-jit8 ku2 bo5 chheng-khi3.  12). Hit-lang5 kau3 te7-saN jit8, tioh8 eng7 hit e5 chui2 chheng-khi3 pun2-sin; kau3 te7-chhit jit8 chiah chheng-khi3; i na7 ti7 te7-saN jit8 bo5 chheng-khi3 pun2-sin, kau3 te7-chhit jit8 chiu7 bo5 chheng-khi3.  13). KiN3-na7 bong--tioh8 lang5 e5 sin-si, bo5 chheng-khi3 ka-ki7 e5, chiu7 phah la5-sam5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 hoe7-bou7, chit e5 lang5 tioh8 tui3 I2-sek-liat8 tiong chian2-tu5; in-ui7 tu5-khi3 la5-sam5 e5 chui2 bo5 hiu3 ti7 i e5 seng-khu, i chiu7 bo5 chheng-khi3, i e5 bo5 chheng-khi3 iau2-ku2 ti7 i.  14). Lang5 si2 ti7 pou3-piN5-lai7, hit e5 tiau5-le7 si7 an2-ni:  kiN3-na7 jip8 hit e5 pou3-piN5, kap it-chhe3 ti7 pou3-piN5-lai7 e5, long2 tioh8 bo5 chheng-khi3 chhit-jit8 ku2.  15). KiN3-na7 hian-khui e5 khi3-ku7, chiu7-si7 koa3 bo5 kham3-bat8 e5, ia7 si7 bo5 chheng-khi3.  16). Bo5-lun7 sim2-mih8 lang5 ti7 chhan5-ia2 bong--tioh8 hou7 to thai5-si2-e5, a2-si7 sin-si, a2-si7 lang5 e5 kut-thau5, a2-si7 hun5-bong7, chiu7 chhit-jit8 ku2 bo5 chheng-khi3.  17). Tioh8 ui7-tioh8 chit-e5 bo5 chheng-khi3 e5 lang5 theh8 tam7-poh8 sou2 sio tu5-khi3 choe7 e5 he2-hu, he7 ti7 khi3-ku7-lai7, to3 oah8-chui2 ti7 hi2 teng2-bin7.  18). Tioh8 u7 chit8 e5 chheng-khi3 e5 lang5 theh8 giu5-chhek-chhau2 un3 ti7 chit e5 chui2, chiong chui2 hiu3 ti7 pou3-piN5, kap long2-chong2 e5 khi3-ku7, i2-kip8 hit lai7-bin7 e5 lang5; koh hiu3 bong--tioh8 kut-thau5 e5, a2-si7 bong--tioh8 siu7 thai5-e5, a2-si7 bong-tioh8 si2-si e5, a2-si7 bong--tioh8 hun5-bong7 e5.  19). Te7-saN jit8 kap te7-chhit jit8, chheng-khi3-e5 tioh8 ka7 hit e5 bo5 chheng-khi3-e5 hiu3 chui2, kau3 te7-chhit jit8 thang hou7 i chheng-khi3; hit-lang5 tioh8 soe2-saN, eng7 chui2 soe2 seng-khu; kau3 e5-hng chiah chheng-khi3.  20). Chong2-si7 hit e5 bo5 chheng-khi3 e5 lang5 ia7 bo5 chheng-khi3 ka-ki7 e5, tioh8 tui3 hoe7-tiong chian2-tu5 i; in-ui7 i phah la5-sam5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 seng3-sou2; tu5-khi3 la5-sam5 e5 chui2 bo5 hiu3 ti7 i e5 seng-khu, i si7 bo5 chheng-khi3 e5 lang5.  21). Che beh ka7 in choe3 eng2-oan2 e5 le7; koh hit-e5 ka7 lang5 hiu3 tu5-khi3 la5-sam5 e5 chui2, hit-lang5 tioh8 soe2 i e5 saN; kiN3-na7 bong hit e5 tu5-khi3 la5-sam5 e5 chui2--e5, tek-khak bo5 chheng-khi3 kau3 e5-hng.  22). KiN3-na7 bo5 chheng-khi3 e5 lang5 sou2 bong--tioh8-e5, chiu7 bo5 chheng-khi3; bong--tioh8 i e5, tek-khak bo5 chheng-khi3 kau3 e5-hng.

[20]	ChiaN-geh8-kan, I2-sek-liat8 lang5 choan5-hoe7 lai5 kau3 Sim5 e5 khong3-ia2, peh-siN3 chiu7 tiam3 ti7 Ka-te-su.  Bi2-li7-am3 si2 ti7-hia, chiu7 bai5-chong3 ti7-hia.  2). Hoe7-chiong3 bo5 chui2 thang lim; in chiu7 chu7-chip8 kong-kek Mou5-se A-lun5.  3). Peh-siN3 chiu7 kap Mou5-se ke3-kau3 kong2, Cheng5 goan2 e5 hiaN-ti7 si2 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, goan2 m7-tat8-tioh8 hit-si5 soa3 si2.  4). Lin2 siaN2-su7 chhoa7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 hoe7-chiong3 kau3 chit e5 khong3-ia2, hou7 goan2 kap goan2 e5 cheng-siN si2 ti7-chia ah?  5). Lin2 siaN2-su7 hou7 goan2 chhut Ai-kip8, chhoa7 goan2 kau3 chit e5 phaiN2 sou2-chai7 ah? Bo5 sou2-chai7 thang ia7-cheng2, ia7 bo5 bu5-hoa-ko2, bo5 phu5-to5, bo5 siah8-liu5, koh bo5 chui2 thang lim.  6). Mou5-se A-lun5 li7-khui hoe7-chiong3 kau3 hoe7-bou7 mng5-khau2, phak ti7 toe7--nih; Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 eng5-kng tui3 in hian2-hian7.  7). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  8). Li2 tioh8 kiah8 koaiN2-a2, li2 kap li2 e5 hiaN A-lun5 chio-chip8 hoe7-chiong3; ti7 in e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5 lin2 beng7-leng7 chioh8-poaN5 chhut-chui2, li2 ui7-tioh8 peh-siN3 hou7 chui2 tui3 chioh8-poaN5 chhut, hou7 hoe7-chiong3 kap in e5 cheng-siN lim.  9). Mou5-se than3 beng7-leng7, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 kiah8 koaiN2-a2.  10). Mou5-se A-lun5 chio-chip8 hoe7-chiong3 kau3 chioh8-poaN5-cheng5, Mou5-se tui3 in kong2, Lin2 chiah e5 poe7-gek8 e5 lang5 tioh8 thiaN ah, goan2 tioh8 hou7 chui2 tui3 chit e5 chioh8-poaN5 lau5-chhut-lai5 hou7 lin2 mah?  11). Mou5-se kiah8-khi2 chhiu2, eng7 koaiN2-a2 phah chioh8-poaN5 nng7-e7, chiu7 u7 choe7-choe7 chui2 lau5-chhut, hoe7-chiong3 kap in e5 cheng-siN long2 lim.  12). Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 tui3 Mou5-se A-lun5 kong2, In-ui7 lin2 m7 sin3 Goa2, bo5 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5 chun-keng3 Goa2 choe3-seng3, sou2-i2 lin2 boe7-tit-thang chhoa7 chiah e5 hoe7-chiong3 jip8 Goa2 sou2 su3-hou7 in e5 toe7.  13). Chiah e5 chui2 mia5 kio3 Bi2-li7-pa e5 chui2; si7 in-ui7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kap Ia5-ho5-hoa ke3-kau3; Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 tui3 in hian2-beng5 ka-ki7 choe3-seng3.
	14). Mou5-se tui3 Ka-te-su chhe su3-chia2 khi3 kiN3 I2-tong ong5, kong2, Li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 I2-sek-liat8 an2-ni kong2, Li2 chai goan2 sou2 tu2-tioh8 it-chhe3 e5 kan-khou2.  15). Goan2 e5 liat8-chou2 loh8-khi3 Ai-kip8, goan2 toa3 ti7 Ai-kip8 ku2-ku2; Ai-kip8 lang5 phaiN2 khoan2-thai7 goan2 kap goan2 e5 liat8-chou2.  16). Goan2 ai-kiu5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 si5, I thiaN goan2 e5 siaN, chhe-khian2 su3-chia2 chhoa7 goan2 chhut Ai-kip8; taN goan2 ti7 li2 kek8 piN-thau5 e5 siaN5 Ka-te-su.  17). Kiu5 li2 iong5-un2 goan2 keng-ke3 li2 e5 toe7, goan2 bo5 beh tui3 chhan5-hng5 kap phu5-to5-hng5 keng-ke3, ia7 bo5 lim chiah e5 chiN2 e5 chui2; tok8-tok8 kiaN5 toa7-lou7, bo5 phian-cho2 phian-iu7, tit8-tit8 keng-ke3 li2 e5 toe7-kai3.  18). I2-tong ong5 kong2, Li2 m7-thang tui3 goa2 chia keng-ke3, bian2-tit goa2 kiah8 to chhut-lai5 ti2-tek8 li2.  19). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 ka7 i kong2, Goan2 beh tui3 toa7-lou7 kiaN5-khi3; siat-su2 goan2 kap cheng-siN lim li2 e5 chui2, goan2 beh heng5 li2 ke3-chiN5; chun2 goa2 pou7-kiaN5 ke3--khi3, bo5 chhap pat8-hang7.  20). I kong2, Li2 m7-thang keng-ke3.  I2-tong ong5 chiu7 chhoa7 choe7-choe7 lang5 chhut-lai5, eng7 kong-ngi7 e5 chhiu2 ti2-tek8 i.  21). An2-ni I2-tong m7 chun2 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tui3 i e5 toe7-kai3 keng-ke3; I2-sek-liat8 chiu7 oat8-tng2 li7-khui i.
	22). In tui3 Ka-te-su khi2-sin, I2-sek-liat8 e5 choan5-hoe7 kau3 Ho5-jiN2 soaN.  23). Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 oa2-kun7 I2-tong piN-kai3 e5 Ho5-jiN2 soaN, hoan-hu3 Mou5-se A-lun5 kong2,  24). A-lun5 beh to3-chou2, in-ui7 i boe7-tit-thang jip8 Goa2 siuN2-su3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 toe7, in-ui7 ti7 Bi2-li7-pa e5 chui2 lin2 ui5-keh8 Goa2 e5 beng7-leng7.  25). Li2 toa3 A-lun5 kap i e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-a-sat chiuN7 Ho5-jiN2 soaN,  26). thng3 A-lun5 e5 saN, ka7 i e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-a-sat chheng7; A-lun5 beh si2 ti7-hia, to3-khi3.  27). Mou5-se chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beng7-leng7-e5 kiaN5; in saN-lang5 tng hoe7-chiong3 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5 chiuN7 Ho5-jiN2 soaN.  28). Mou5-se thng3 A-lun5 e5 saN, ka7 i e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-a-sat chheng7; A-lun5 ti7-hia si2 ti7 soaN-teng2; Mou5-se kap I2-li7-a-sat loh8-soaN.  29). Hoe7-chiong3 khoaN3-kiN3 A-lun5 i2-keng si2, chiu7 ui7 A-lun5 thi5-khau3 saN-chap8 jit8; I2-sek-liat8 choan5-ke ia7 long2 an2-ni.

[21]	Khia7-khi2 ti7 lam5-hng e5 Ka-lam5 lang5, A-lah8-tek ong5, thiaN-kiN3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tui3 A-tha-lim5 lou7 lai5, chiu7 kap I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kau-chian3, liah8 in kui2-na7 lang5.  2). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa hoat-goan7 kong2, Li2 na7 chin-chiaN3 chiong chit e5 peh-siN3 kau goa2 e5 chhiu2, goa2 chiu7 it-chin7 chau5-biat8 in e5 siaN5.  3). Ia5-ho5-hoa thiaN I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 siaN, chiong Ka-lam5 lang5 kau-tai3 in; in chiu7 it-chin7 biat8 in, kap in e5 siaN5; hit sou2-chai7 e5 mia5 chiu7 kio3 Ho5-jiN2-ma2.
	4). In tui3 Ho5-jiN2 soaN khi2-sin, tui3 Ang5-hai2 e5 lou7 khi3, beh seh8 I2-tong e5 toe7; peh-siN3 ui7-tioh8 sou2 kiaN5 e5 lou7, sim put-chi2 loe2-chi3.  5). Chiu7 hiam5 Siong7-te3 kap Mou5-se kong2, Lin2 siaN2-su7 chhoa7 goan2 chhut Ai-kip8, hou7 goan2 si2 ti7 chit e5 khong3-ia2 ah? In-ui7 bo5 piaN2, bo5 chui2, goan2 e5 sim iam3-chian7 chit e5 chheng-tam7 e5 chiah8-mih8.  6). Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 chhe he2-choa5 jip8 peh-siN3 e5 tiong-kan, ka7 peh-siN3; I2-sek-liat8 lang5 si2 choe7-choe7.  7). Peh-siN3 kau3 Mou5-se hia, kong2, Goan2 u7 hoan7-choe7, in-ui7 goan2 u7 hiam5 Ia5-ho5-hoa kap li2; chhiaN2 li2 kiu5 Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 chiah e5 choa5 li7-khui goan2.  Mou5-se chiu7 thoe3 peh-siN3 kiu5.  8). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 choe3 chit8-be2 he2-choa5, kui3 ti7 ki5-koaN-teng2; kiN3-na7 hou7 i ka7-tioh8 e5, chit8-e7 khoaN3, chiu7 oe7 oah8.  9). Mou5-se chiu7 choe3 chit8-be2 tang5-choa5, kui3 ti7 ki5-koaN-teng2; kiN3-na7 hou7 choa5 ka7-tioh8--e5, chit8-e7 khoaN3 chit e5 tang5-choa5, chiu7 oah8.
	10). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 O-pok8.  11). Koh tui3 O-pok8 khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 I2-ia5-a-pa-lim5, chiu7-si7 ng3 jit8-chhut e5 sou2-chai7, kap Mou5-ap saN-tui3 e5 khong3-ia2.  12). Tui3-hia khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Sat-liat8 e5 soaN-kok.  13). Tui3-hia khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 A-lun3 e5 hit-peng5, chiu7-si7 ti7 khong3-ia2, tui3 A-mou5-li7 e5 toe7-kai3 chhut-lai5; in-ui7 A-lun3 si7 Mou5-ap e5 kau-kai3, ti7 Mou5-ap kap A-mou5-li7 e5 tiong-kan.  14). Sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa kau-chian3 e5 chheh u7 kong2:
	Sou-hoat e5 Oa-hap-pek,
	Kap A-lun3 hiah e5 soaN-kok;
15).	I2-kip8 chiah e5 soaN-kok e5 chui2-choaN5,
	Chiu7-si7 ng3 A-jiN2 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7,
	Oa2-kun7 Mou5-ap e5 keng2-kai3.
16). In tui3 hia kau3 Pi2-jiN2; che chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa bat tui3 Mou5-se sou2 kong2-khi2 e5 chiN2, kong2, Li2 chu7-chip8 peh-siN3, Goa2 beh eng7 chui2 hou7 in.  17). Hit-si5 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chhiuN3-koa kong2,
	ChiN2 ah, chheng3--chhut-lai5; lin2 tioh8 tui3 i chhiuN3-koa;
18). 	Chit e5 chiN2 si7 siu2-leng2 khui i, 
	Peh-siN3 chun-kui3 e5 lang5,
	Eng7 koan5-peng3, eng7 in e5 koaiN2-a2 kut8 e5.
In tui3 khong3-ia2 khi3 Ma2-tha-na2;  19). Tui3 Ma2-tha-na2 kau3 Na2-hap8-liat8, tui3 Na2-hap-liat8 kau3 Pa-boat8.  20). Tui3 Pa-boat8 kau3 Mou5-ap toe7 e5 soaN-kok, kau3 hit e5 khoaN3 loh8-ke7, oe7 khoaN3-kiN3 khong3-ia2 e5 Pi5-su-ka e5 soaN-chiam.
	21). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chhe su3-chia2 khi3 kiN3 A-mou5-li7 lang5 e5 ong5 Se-hong5, kong2,  22). Kiu5 li2 iong5-un2 goa2 tui3 li2 e5 toe7 keng-ke3; goan2 bo5 phian ti7 chhan5-hng5, kap phu5-to5-hng5; goan2 ia7 bo5 beh lim chiN2--nih e5 chui2; tok8-tok8 kiaN5 toa7-lou7, tit8-tit8 keng-ke3 li2 e5 toe7-kai3.  23). Se-hong5 m7-chun2 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 keng-ke3 i e5 keng2-kai3; Se-hong5 chiu7 chu7-chip8 i e5 cheng3 peh-siN3, chhut-lai5 kau3 khong3-ia2, beh ti2-tek8 I2-sek-liat8 lang5, kau3 Nga2-chap8; kap I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kau-chian3.  24). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 eng7 to thai5 i, chiam3 i e5 toe7, tui3 A-lun3 kau3 Nga2-phok, tit8-tit8 kau3 A-bun5 lang5 hia; in-ui7 A-bun5 lang5 e5 toe7-kai3 chin kian-kou3.  25). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chhu2 i it-chhe3 e5 siaN5, I2-sek-liat8 lang5 ia7 khia7-khi2 A-mou5-li7 e5 siaN5, ti7 Hi-sit8-pun2, kap i it-chhe3 e5 siaN5.  26). Chit e5 Hi-sit8-pun2 si7 A-mou5-li7 ong5 Se-hong5 e5 siaN5; i bat kap Mou5-ap cheng5 e5 ong5 kau-chian3, tui3 i e5 chhiu2 chhiuN2 choan5-toe7, tit8-kau3 A-lun3.  27). Sou2-i2 choe3-si e5 lang5 liam7, kong2:
	Lin2 tioh8 lai5 Hi-sit8-pun2,
	Goan7 Se-hong5 e5 siaN5 tit-tioh8 khi2-cho7, koh kian-kou3;
28).	In-ui7 u7 he2 tui3 Hi-sit8-pun2 chhut,
	U7 he2-iam7 tui3 Se-hong5 e5 siaN5 hoat,
	Sio-hui2 Mou5-ap e5 A-jiN2,
	Kap A-lun3 koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7 e5 chu2.
29).	Mou5-ap ah, li2 u7 chai-e7!
	Ki-boat8 e5 peh-siN3 ah, lin2 biat8-bo5 lah!
	Hou7 i e5 ta-pou-teng choe3 to5-chau2-e5,
	Cha-bou2-kiaN2 choe3 siu7-liah8-e5,
	Kau hou7 A-mou5-li7 ong5 Se-hong5.
30).	Goan2 sia7--in; Hi-sit8-pun2 kau3 Ti2-pun2 it-chin7 hui2 biat8,
	Goan2 hou7 toe7 pha-hng, tit8-kau3 Lo5-hoat,
	Chiu7-si7 kau3 Bi2-ti2-pa.
31). An2-ni, I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chiu7 khia7-khi2 ti7 A-mou5-li7 lang5 e5 toe7.  32). Mou5-se chhe lang5 khi3 thau-khoaN3 Nga2-sia7, chiu7 chhu2 in hiah e5 hiuN-sia7, koaN2-chhut khia7-khi2 hia e5 A-mou5-li7 lang5.
	33). I2-sek-liat8 oat tui3 Pa-san e5 lou7 khi3; Pa-san ong5 Gok8, kap i e5 cheng3 peh-siN3, long2 chhut-lai5 ti2-tek8 in, ti7 I2-tek-lai5 kap in kau-chian3.  34). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, M7-bian2 kiaN in, in-ui7 Goa2 i2-keng chiong i kap i e5 cheng3 peh-siN3, i e5 toe7, long2 kau ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2; li2 tioh8 khoan2-thai7 i, chhin-chhiuN7 li2 bat khoan2-thai7 tiam3 ti7 Hi-sit8-pun2 e5 A-mou5-li7 ong5 Se-hong5 chit8-iuN7.  35). In chiu7 phah i, kap i hiah e5 kiaN2, i2-kip8 i e5 cheng3 peh-siN3, bo5 ka7 i lau5 chit8-e5, chiu7 tit-tioh8 i e5 toe7.

[22]	I2-sek-liat8 lang5 khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Mou5-ap e5 piN5-iuN5, ti7 Iok-tan3 ho5-goa7, Ia5-li7-ko e5 tui3-bin7.
	2). Se-phoat e5 kiaN2 Pa-lek8 khoaN3-kiN3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tui3 A-mou5-li7 lang5 sou2 kiaN5 it-chhe3 e5 su7.  3). Mou5-ap chin kiaN hit e5 peh-siN3, in-ui7 in chin-choe7; Mou5-ap in-ui7 I2-sek-liat8 peh-siN3, sim chiu7 tioh8-kip.  4). Mou5-ap ka7 Bi2-tian5 e5 tiuN2-lo2 kong2, TaN chit-kun5 e5 lang5 beh it-chin7 chiah8 lan2 si3-ui5 sou2 u7 e5, chhin-chhiuN7 gu5 chiah8 chhan5--nih e5 chhau2 chit8-poaN; hit-si5 Se-phoat e5 kiaN2 Pa-lek8 choe3 Mou5-ap ong5.  5). I chhe su3-chia2 khi3 Toa7-ho5-piN e5 Pi5-toat8, kau3 Pi2-jiN2 e5 kiaN2 Pa-lan5 e5 pun2 sou2-chai7 kio3 i lai5, kong2, KhoaN3 ah, u7 chit8 e5 peh-siN3 tui3 Ai-kip8 chhut-lai5; khoaN3 ah, in jia-moa2 toe7-bin7, ia7 khia7-khi2 ti7 goa2 e5 tui3-bin7.  6). TaN chhiaN2 li2 lai5, ka7 goa2 chiu3-chou2 chit e5 peh-siN3, in-ui7 in pi2 goa2 khah-kiong5; kiam2-chhai2 goa2 oe7 phah lai5 khah-iaN5 in, koaN2 in chhut chit e5 sou2-chai7; in-ui7 goa2 chai li2 sou2 chiok-hok e5 , chiu7 tit-tioh8 hok-khi3, li2 sou2 chiu3-chou2 e5, chiu7 siu7 chiu3-chou2.  7). Mou5-ap tiuN2-lo2 kap Bi2-tian5 e5 tiuN2-lo2, chiu7 khi2-sin, chhiu2 toa3 pok-koa3 e5 le2, khi3 kau3 Pa-lan5 hia, chiong Pa-lek8 e5 oe7 ka7 i kong2.  8). I tui3 in kong2, Kim-mi5 lin2 hioh chia; chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3 goa2 e5, goa2 beh he5-hok lin2.  Mou5-ap e5 siu2-leng2 chiu7 hioh ti7 Pa-lan5 hia.  9). Siong7-te3 lim5-kau3 Pa-lan5, mng7 i kong2, Kap li2 toa3 hiah e5 lang5 si7 chi7-chui7?  10). Pa-lan5 in3 Siong7-te3 kong2, Si7 Mou5-ap ong5 Se-phoat e5 kiaN2 chhe lang5 kau3 goa2 chia, kong2,  11). KhoaN3 ah, u7 peh-siN3 tui3 Ai-kip8 lai5, jia-moa2 toe7-bin7; chhiaN2 li2 lai5 ka7 goa2 chiu3-chou2 in, kiam2-chhai2 goa2 oe7 thai5-iaN5 in, koaN2 in chhut-khi3.  12). Siong7-te3 tui3 Pa-lan5 kong2, Li2 m7-thang kap in khi3, ia7 m7-thang chiu3-chou2 chit e5 peh-siN3; in-ui7 in si7 tit-tioh8 hok-khi3-e5.  13). Pa-lan5 chheng-cha2 khi2-lai5, tui3 Pa-lek8 e5 siu2-leng2 kong2, Lin2 to3--khi3 lin2 e5 sou2-chai7, in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa m7-chun2 goa2 kap lin2 khi3.  14). Mou5-ap e5 siu2-leng2 chiu7 khi2-lai5, to3--khi3 Pa-lek8 hia, kong2, Pa-lan5 m7-kheng2 kap goan2 lai5.  15). Pa-lek8 koh chhe siu2-leng2, pi2 cheng5 khah-choe7, khah chun-kui3-e5.  16). In kau3 Pa-lan5 hia, tui3 i kong2, Se-phoat e5 kiaN2 Pa-lek8 an2-ni kong2, Kiu5 li2 m7-thang hou7 sim2-mih8 tai7-chi3 chou2-tong3 li2 bo5 lai5 goa2 chia.  17). In-ui7 goa2 beh hou7 li2 tit-tioh8 kek8-toa7 e5 chun-kui3; kiN3-na7 li2 tui3 goa2 kong2 sim2-mih8, goa2 beh chiau3 an2-ni kiaN5; sou2-i2 chhiaN2 li2 lai5, ka7 goa2 chiu3-chou2 chit e5 peh-siN3.  18). Pa-lan5 tui3 Pa-lek8 chiah e5 jin5-sin5 kong2, Pa-lek8 chiu7 na7 eng7 moa2-chhu3 e5 kim-gun5 hou7 goa2, goa2 ia7 m7-kaN2 poaN5-ke3 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 beng7-leng7, lai5 ke-kiam2 kiaN5.  19). ChhiaN2 lin2 kim-mi5 koh hioh chia, theng3-hau7 goa2 chai Ia5-ho5-hoa koh ka7 goa2 kong2 sim2-mih8.  20). Hit-mi5 Siong7-te3 lim5-kau3 Pa-lan5 hia kong2, Chiah e5 lang5 na7 lai5 kio3 li2, li2 chiu7 khi2-lai5 kap i khi3; chong2-si7 Goa2 sou2 beh ka7 li2 kong2 e5, li2 tioh8 chun-than3.
	21). Pa-lan5 cha2-khi2 khi2-lai5, pi7-pan7 lu5; kap Mou5-ap e5 siu2-leng2 saN-kap khi3.  22). Siong7-te3, in-ui7 i khi3, chiu7 siu7-khi3; Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 su3-chia2 khia7 ti7 lou7--nih lai5 ti2-tek8 i; i khia5 lu5, nng7 e5 lou5-pok8 kun-te3 i.  23). Lu5 khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 su3-chia2 khia7 ti7 lou7--nih, chhiu2--nih puih8 to; lu5 chiu7 tui3 lou7--nih siam2 jip8 hng5; Pa-lan5 chiu7 phah lu5 beh hou7 i kui goan5-lou7.  24). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 su3-chia2 chiu7 khia7 ti7 phu5-to5-hng5 e5 oeh8-lou7, chit-peng5 u7 chhiuN5, hit-peng5 ia7 u7 chhiuN5.  25). Lu5 khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 su3-chia2, chiu7 siam2-oa2 hit e5 chhiuN5, khoeh Pa-lan5 e5 kha ti7 chhiuN5--nih; Pa-lan5 chiu7 koh phah i.  26). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 su3-chia2 koh chin3-cheng5 khi3, khia7 ti7 oeh8-oeh8 e5 sou2-chai7, siang-peng5 bo5 lou7 thang oat.  27). Lu5 khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 su3-chia2, chiu7 phak ti7 Pa-lan5 e5 e7-toe2, Pa-lan5 hoat siu7-khi3, eng7 koaiN2-a2 phah lu5.  28). Ia5-ho5-hoa khui lu5 e5 chhui3, lu5 tui3 Pa-lan5 kong2, Goa2 tui3 li2 choe3 sim2-mih8, li2 keng2-jian5 phah goa2 chi2 saN-pai2 ah?  29). Pa-lan5 tui3 lu5 kong2, In-ui7 li2 hi3-lang7 goa2; goa2 hun7 chhiu2--nih bo5 to; u7, chiu7 ka7 li2 thai5-si2.  30). Lu5 tui3 Pa-lan5 kong2, Goa2 kiam2 m7-si7 li2 e5 lu5, li2 it-seng sou2 khia5-e5 mah? goa2 peng5-sou3 bat tui3 li2 an2-ni kiaN5 mah? Pa-lan5 kong2, Bo5.  31). Hit-si5 Ia5-ho5-hoa khui Pa-lan5 e5 bak8-chiu, i chiu7 khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 su3-chia2 khia7 ti7 lou7--nih, chhiu2 puih8 to; Pa-lan5 chiu7 aN3-thau5 phak ti7 toe7--nih.  32). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 su3-chia2 tui3 i kong2, Li2 siaN2-su7 chi2 saN-pai2 phah li2 e5 lu5 ah? KhoaN3 ah, goa2 chhut-lai5 ti2-tek8 li2, in-ui7 li2 ti7 goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 sou2 kiaN5 e5, si7 poe7-gek8.  33). Lu5 khoaN3-kiN3 goa2, chiu7 siam2-pi7 goa2 chi2 saN-pai2; siat-su2 lu5 bo5 siam2-pi7 goa2, goa2 i2-keng thai5-si2 li2, hou7 lu5 oah8-teh.  34). Pa-lan5 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 su3-chia2 kong2, Goa2 u7 hoan7-choe7 lah, goa2 m7-chai li2 khia7 ti7 lou7--nih chou2-tong3 goa2; li2 na7 bo5 hoaN-hi2 goa2 khi3, goa2 chiu7 to3-tng2--khi3.  35). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 su3-chia2 tui3 Pa-lan5 kong2, Li2 kap chiah e5 lang5 khi3; chong2-si7 li2 chi2-u7 thang kong2 goa2 sou2 beh tui3 li2 kong2-e5.  Pa-lan5 chiu7 kap Pa-lek8 e5 siu2-leng2 saN-kap khi3.
	36). Pa-lek8 thiaN-kiN3 Pa-lan5 lai5, chiu7 khi3 Mou5-ap siaN5 ngia5-chih i; chit e5 siaN5 si7 ti7 piN-kai3 e5 kek8-thau5, ti7 A-lun3 e5 piN-thau5.  37). Pa-lek8 tui3 Pa-lan5 kong2, Goa2 kiam2 m7-si7 chhiat-chhiat chhe lang5 kau3 li2 hia khi3 kio3 li2 mah? Li2 siaN2-su7 bo5 lai5 goa2 chia ah? goa2 kiam2 bo5 chin-chiaN3 oe7 hou7 li2 chun-kui3 mah?  38). Pa-lan5 in3 Pa-lek8 kong2, Goa2 taN lai5 kau3 li2 chia, goa2 kiam2 u7 koan5 oe7 kong2 sim2-mih8 ah? Siong7-te3 eng7 sim2-mih8 oe7 kau-tai3 goa2, goa2 chiu7 kong2 i.  39). Pa-lan5 kap Pa-lek8 saN-kap kiaN5, lai5 kau3 Ki-liat8-ou5-so2.  40). Pa-lek8 thai5 gu5-iuN5 hian3-che3, chiu7 sang3 hou7 Pa-lan5 i2-kip8 kap i ti7-teh e5 siu2-leng2.
	41). Kau3 keh cha2-khi2, Pa-lek8 chhoa7 Pa-lan5 kau3 Pa-lek8 e5 koaiN5-ui7; Pa-lan5 tui3 hia khoaN3 I2-sek-liat8 peh-siN3 kek8-thau5 e5 sou2-chai7.

[23]	Pa-lan5 tui3 Pa-lek8 kong2, Li2 ti7-chia ka7 goa2 khi2 chhit cho7 toaN5, ka7 goa2 pi7-pan7 chhit chiah gu5-kang2, chhit chiah iuN5-kang2.  2). Pa-lek8 chiau3 Pa-lan5 e5 oe7 lai5 kiaN5; Pa-lek8 kap Pa-lan5 ti7 tak8 cho7 e5 toaN5, hian3 chit8 chiah gu5-kang2, chit8 chiah iuN5-kang2.  3). Pa-lan5 tui3 Pa-lek8 kong2, Li2 khia7 ti7 li2 sio-che3 e5 piN-thau5, goa2 chhiaN2 chin3-cheng5 khi3, kiam2-chhai2 Ia5-ho5-hoa lai5 tu2-tioh8 goa2; I chi2-si7 goa2 sim2-mih8, goa2 beh ka7 li2 kong2.  Pa-lan5 chiu7 chiuN7--khi3 bo5 chhau2-bak8 e5 soaN.  4). Siong7-te3 tu2-tioh8 Pa-lan5, Pa-lan5 tui3 I kong2, Goa2 i2-keng pi7-pan7 chhit cho7 toaN5, ti7 tak8 cho7 toaN5 hian3 chit8 chiah gu5-kang2, chit8 chiah iuN5-kang2.  5). Ia5-ho5-hoa eng7 oe7 kau-tai3 Pa-lan5, koh ka7 i kong2, Li2 to3--khi3 Pa-lek8 hia, tioh8 an2-ni ka7 i kong2.  6). I chiu7 to3--khi3 Pa-lek8 hia; khoaN3-kiN3 i kap Mou5-ap e5 siu2-leng2, long2 khia7 ti7 i sio-che3 e5 piN-a2.  7). Pa-lan5 chiu7 the5-khi2 i e5 koa, kong2,
	Pa-lek8 chhoa7 goa2 tui3 A-lan5 lai5,
	Mou5-ap ong5 chhoa7 goa2 chhut tang-peng5 e5 soaN, kong2,
	Lai5 ah, ka7 goa2 chiu3-chou2 Nga2-kok,
	Lai5 ah, chiu3-me7 I2-sek-liat8.
8).	Siong7-te3 bo5 chiu3-chou2 e5, goa2 thai2 oe7 chiu3-chou2?
	Ia5-ho5-hoa bo5 chiu3-me7 e5, goa2 thai2 oe7 chiu3-me7?
9).	In-ui7 goa2 tui3 chiah e5 soaN-giam5 khoaN3 i,
	Koh tui3 soaN-be2-liu koan-khoaN3,
	KhoaN3 ah, chit e5 peh-siN3 beh ka-ki7 khia7-khi2.
	Bo5 liat8 ti7 chiah e5 kok e5 tiong-kan.
10).	Chi7-chui7 oe7 siau3 Nga2-kok e5 thou5-soa?
	Chi7-chui7 oe7 sng3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 si3-hun7-chit8?
	Goa2 goan7 chhin-chhiuN7 gi7-lang5 e5 si2 lai5 si2,
	Ia7 chhin-chhiuN7 i e5 kiat-kiok8 lai5 kiat-kiok8.
11). Pa-lek8 tui3 Pa-lan5 kong2, Li2 tui3 goa2 choe3-e5 si7 sim2-mih8 ah? Goa2 kio3 li2 lai5 chiu3-chou2 goa2 e5 tui3-tek8, khoaN3 ah, li2 long2 si7 ka7 in chiok-hok.  12). I in3 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 kau-tai3 goa2 e5 oe7, goa2 kiam2 m7-tioh8 kin2-sin7 lai5 kong2 mah?
	13). Pa-lek8 tui3 i kong2, Kiu5 li2 kap goa2 khi3 pat8-ui7, ti7-hia thang khoaN3-kiN3 in, li2 chi2-u7 oe7 khoaN3-kiN3 in e5 chit8 kak-thau5, boe7-oe7 long2-chong2 khoaN3-kiN3; ti7-hia tioh8 ka7 goa2 chiu3-chou2 in.  14). Tui3 hit-tiap8 chhoa7 i kau3 So2-hui e5 soaN-ia2, chiuN7 Pi5-su-ka e5 soaN-thau5, khi2 chhit cho7 toaN5, tak8 cho7 toaN5 hian3 chit8 chiah gu5-kang2, chit8 chiah iuN5-kang2.  15). Pa-lan5 tui3 Pa-lek8 kong2, Li2 toa3 chia, khia7 ti7 li2 sio-che3 e5 piN-a2, theng3-hau7 goa2 khi3 hia kiN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  16). Ia5-ho5-hoa tu2-tioh8 Pa-lan5, eng7 oe7 kau-tai3 i, koh kong2, Li2 to3--khi3 Pa-lek8 hia, tioh8 an2-ni kong2.  17). I chiu7 to3--khi3 Pa-lek8 hia, khoaN3-kiN3 i khia7 ti7 sio-che3 e5 piN-a2, Mou5-ap e5 siu2-leng2 ia7 kap i ti7-hia.  Pa-lek8 mng7 i kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2 sim2-mih8 oe7 ah?  18). Pa-lan5 chiu7 the5-khi2 i e5 koa, kong2, 
	Pa-lek8 ah, khi2-lai5 thiaN;
	Se-phoat e5 kiaN2, li2 aN3 hi7-khang lai5 thiaN goa2;
19).	Siong7-te3 m7-si7 chhin-chhiuN7 lang5, oe7 kong2 peh8-chhat8, 
	Ia7 m7-si7 lang5 e5 kiaN2, oe7 the3-hoe2;
	I i2-keng kong2, kiam2 bo5 kiaN5 mah?
	I kong2-chhut, kiam2 bo5 eng3-giam7 mah?
20).	KhoaN3 ah, goa2 hong7-beng7 chiok-hok,
	I sou2 eng3-un2 e5 hok-khi3, goa2 boe7 ka7 i peng2-to3-tng2.
21).	I bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 Nga2-kok u7 ke3-sit,
	Ti7 I2-sek-liat8 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 u7 kan-ok,
	Ia5-ho5-hoa i e5 Siong7-te3 kap i ti7-teh;
	Ti7 in tiong-kan u7 o-lo2 ong5 e5 siaN.
22).	Siong7-te3 chhoa7 in chhut Ai-kip8;
	In chhin-chhiuN7 u7 ia2-gu5 e5 lat8.
23).	Nga2-kok tiong koat-toan3 bo5 hoat-sut8,
	I2-sek-liat8 tiong ia7 bo5 chiam-pok;
	Kau3-si5 lun7-khi2 Nga2-kok kap I2-sek-liat8 beh kong2,
	Siong7-te3 kiaN5 hiah--nih toa7 e5 su7!
24).	KhoaN3 ah, chit e5 peh-siN3 khi2-lai5 chhin-chhiuN7 bu2 e5 sai,
	Theng2-sin chhin-chhiuN7 kang e5 sai;
	Iau2-be7 chiah8 sou2 lak8-tioh8 e5 mih8,
	Iau2-be7 lim siu7 ka7-si2-e5 e5 huih,
	Koat-toan3 bo5 to2--teh.
25). Pa-lek8 tui3 Pa-lan5 kong2, Li2 long2 m7-thang chiu3-chou2 in, ia7 m7-thang ka7 in chiok-hok.  26). Pa-lan5 in3 Pa-lek8 kong2, Goa2 kiam2 bo5 ka7 li2 kong2, KiN3-na7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 kong2 e5, goa2 beh chun-than3 mah?
	27). Pa-lek8 tui3 Pa-lan5 kong2, Lai5 ah, goa2 chhoa7 li2 khi3 pat8 sou2-chai7, kiam2-chhai2 Siong7-te3 hoaN-hi2 li2 ti7-hia ka7 goa2 chiu3-chou2 in.  28). Pa-lek8 chiu7 chhoa7 Pa-lan5 kau3 hit e5 khoaN3 loh8-ke7, oe7 khoaN3-kiN3 khong3-ia2 e5 Pi5-jiN2 e5 soaN-chiam.  29). Pa-lan5 tui3 Pa-lek8 kong2, Li2 ti7-chia ka7 goa2 khi2 chhit cho7 toaN5, koh ti7-chia ka7 goa2 pi7-pan7 chhit chiah gu5-kang2, chhit chiah iuN5-kang2.  30). Pa-lek8 chiu7 chiau3 Pa-lan5 e5 oe7 kiaN5, ti7 tak8 cho7 toaN5 hian3 chit8 chiah gu5-kang2, chit8 chiah iuN5-kang2.

[24]	Pa-lan5 khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa hoaN-hi2 su3-hok hou7 I2-sek-liat8, chiu7 bo5 chhin-chhiuN7 eng2-pai2 khi3 chhe7 hoat-sut8, si7 bin7 ng3 khong3-ia2.  2). Pa-lan5 kiah8-bak8, khoaN3-kiN3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chiau3 chi-phai3 khia7-khi2, Siong7-te3 e5 sin5 chiu7 lim5-kau3 i.  3). I chiu7 the5-khi2 i e5 koa, kong2,
	Pi2-jiN2 e5 kiaN2 Pa-lan5 kong2,
	Bak8-chiu hap8--teh e5 lang5 kong2;
4).	ThiaN-kiN3 Siong7-te3 e5 oe7,
	KhoaN3-kiN3 Choan5-leng5--e5 e5 iN7-siong7,
	Bak8-chiu thi2-khui to2-teh e5 lang5 kong2;
5).	Nga2-kok ah, li2 e5 pou3-piN5 chaiN2-iuN7 hiah sui2!
	I2-sek-liat8 ah, li2 e5 tiuN3-pang5 chaiN2-iuN7 hiah ho2-khoaN3!
6).	Chhin-chhiuN7 saN-lian5-soa3 e5 soaN-kok,
	Chhin-chhiuN7 ho5-piN e5 hng5,
	Chhin-chhiuN7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 chai e5 tim5-hiuN-chhiu7,
	Chhin-chhiuN7 chui2-piN e5 pek-hiuN-chhiu7.
7).	Chui2 beh tui3 i e5 thang2 lau5-chhut,
	Cheng2-chi2 beh ia7 ti7 choe7-choe7 chui2 e5 sou2-chai7,
	I e5 ong5 beh poaN5-ke3 A-kah,
	I e5 kok beh heng-khi2.
8).	Siong7-te3 chhoa7 i chhut Ai-kip8,
	I chhin-chhiuN7 u7 ia2-gu5 e5 lat8;
	I beh thun-chiah8 tui3-tek8 e5 kok,
	At-chih8 in e5 kut-thau5;
	Eng7 chiN3 sia7 in, kau3 thang3-ke3.
9). 	I thiN3-kha, koh to2-teh chhin-chhiuN7 kang e5 sai,
	Ia7 chhin-chhiuN7 bu2 e5 sai;
	Chi7-chui7 kaN2 jia2-tioh8 i?
	KiN3-na7 chiok-hok li2 e5, goan7 i siu7 chiok-hok,
	KiN3-na7 chiu3-chou2 li2 e5, goan7 i siu7 chiu3-chou2.
	10). Pa-lek8 toa7 siu7-khi3 Pa-lan5, chiu7 tah-chhiu2; Pa-lek8 koh ka7 Pa-lan5 kong2, Goa2 kio3 li2 lai5 chiu3-chou2 goa2 e5 tui3-tek8, li2 keng2-jian5 choan-choan chiok-hok in, kau3 chi2 saN-pai2.  11). TaN li2 chau2--khi3 pun2 sou2-chai7, goa2 pun2 siuN7 beh hou7 li2 tit-tioh8 toa7 chun-kui3, na7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa chou2-tong3, hou7 li2 bo5 tit-tioh8 chun-kui3.  12). Pa-lan5 tui3 Pa-lek8 kong2, Goa2 kiam2 bo5 tui3 li2 sou2 chhe kau3 goa2 hia e5 su3-chia2 kong2,  13). Pa-lek8 chiu7 na7 chiong i moa2-chhu3 e5 kim-gun5 hou7 goa2, goa2 ia7 boe7-tit poaN5-ke3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 beng7-leng7, pin5 ka-ki7 e5 sim lai5 choe3-ho2 choe3-phaiN2; Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 kong2--e5, goa2 chiu7 kong2 i.  14). KhoaN3 ah, taN goa2 beh to3--khi3 pun2-chok8; li2 lai5, goa2 ka7 li2 kong2, chiah e5 peh-siN3 jit8-au7 beh chaiN2-iuN7 khoan2-thai7 li2 e5 peh-siN3.  15). I chiu7 the5-khi2 i e5 koa, kong2,
	Pi2-jiN2 e5 kiaN2 Pa-lan5 kong2,
	Bak8-chiu hap8--teh e5 lang5 kong2;
16).	ThiaN-kiN3 Siong7-te3 e5 oe7,
	Tit-tioh8 chai Chi3-koaiN5--e5 e5 chai-bat,
	KhoaN3-kiN3 Choan5-leng5--e5 e5 iN7-siong7,
	Bak8-chiu thi2-khui, to2-teh e5 lang5 kong2:
17).	Goa2 khoaN3 i, chong2-si7 bo5 ti7 hian7-si5,
	Goa2 koan-khoaN3 i, chong2-si7 m7-si7 kun7-kun7;
	U7 chit8 liap8 chhiN beh tui3 Nga2-kok chhut,
	U7 chit8 e5 koan5-peng3, beh tui3 I2-sek-liat8 heng-khi2,
	Beh phah-phoa3 Mou5-ap e5 piN-kak,
	Hui2-hoai7 jiau2-loan7 e5 lang5.
18).	I2-tong beh choe3-giap8,
	Se-jiN2 ia7 beh choe3-giap8, hou7 i e5 tui3-tek8,
	I2-sek-liat8 beh kiaN5 tai7-chi3 iong2-kam2.
19).	U7 chit8-ui7 chiang2-koan5-e5 beh tui3 Nga2-kok chhut,
	I beh chau5-biat8 siaN5-tiong sou2 lau5 e5.
20). I koh khoaN3-kiN3 A-ma2-lek8, chiu7 the5-khi2 i e5 koa, kong2,
	A-ma2-lek8 pun2 choe3 chiah e5 kok e5 thau5,
	Chong2-si7 i e5 kiat-kiok8 beh eng2-eng2 biat8-bo5.
21). I koh khoaN3 Ki-ni5 lang5, chiu7 the5-khi2 i e5 koa, kong2,
	Li2 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7 si7 kian-kou3,
	Li2 choh-siu7 ti7 soaN-giam5;
22).	Chong2-si7 Ki-ni5 beh ti3-kau3 soe-bi5,
	Tit8-kau3 hou7 A-sut8 liah8 li2 khi3.
23). I koh the5-khi2 koa, kong2,
	Ai--ah, Siong7-te3 kiaN5 chit e5 su7 e5 si5,
	Chi7-chui7 oe7 tit-tioh8 oah8?
24).	Beh u7 chun5 tui3 Ki-the5 hia lai5,
	Khou2-chhou2 A-sut8, khou2-chhou2 Hi-pek;
	I ia7 beh eng2-eng2 biat8-bo5.
25). Pa-lan5 chiu7 khi2-lai5, to3--khi3 i pun2 sou2-chai7; Pa-lek8 ia7 kiaN5 i e5 lou7.

[25]	I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tiam3 ti7 Sip8-teng5, peh-siN3 chiu7 kap Mou5-ap e5 cha-bou2-gin2-a2 kiaN5 im5-loan7.  2). In hian3-che3 in e5 siong7-te3, chhiaN2 peh-siN3 lai5 hu3, peh-siN3 chiah8 in e5 che3-mih8, soa3 kui7-pai3 in e5 siong7-te3.  3). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kap Pa-lek8-pi2-jiN2 lian5-hap8; Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 tui3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 hoat siu7-khi3.  4). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Chiong peh-siN3 long2-chong2 e5 chok8-tiuN2, tng-thau5 peh8-jit8 tiau3-si2 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 toa7 siu7-khi3 thang tui3 I2-sek-liat8 siau-bo5.  5). Mou5-se chiu7 tui3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 sim2-phoaN3-koaN kong2, KiN3-na7 siok8 lin2 e5 lang5, u7 kap Pa-lek8-pi2-jiN2 lian5-hap8-e5, lin2 tioh8 thai5-si2 i.  6). Mou5-se kap I2-sek-liat8 hoe7-chiong3 tu2-a2 ti7 hoe7-bou7 mng5-khau2 teh-khau3 e5 si5, hut-jian5 u7 I2-sek-liat8 tiong chit8-lang5, tng in bak8-chiu cheng5 toa3 chit8 e5 Bi2-tian5 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 kau3 i e5 hiaN-ti7 hia.  7). Che3-si A-lun5 e5 sun, I2-li7-a-sat e5 kiaN2, Hui-ni5-hap khoaN3-kiN3, chiu7 tui3 hoe7-tiong khi2-lai5, chhiu2--nih kiah8 chhiuN;  8). te3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 jip8 teng5-a2-lai7, chhak8-si2 nng7-lang5, chiu7-si7 chhak8-thau3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kap hit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 pak-tou2; an2-ni, ti7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 tiong-kan un-ek8 chiu7 soah.  9). Hit-si5 tu2-tioh8 un-ek8 si2--e5, nng7-ban7 si3-chheng lang5.
	10). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2, 11). Che3-si A-lun5 e5 sun, I2-li7-a-sat e5 kiaN2, Hui-ni5-hap hou7 Goa2 sou2 hoat e5 siu7-khi3 siau-bo5 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5, in-ui7 i ti7 in tiong-kan, eng7 Goa2 e5 tou3-khi7 choe3 tou3-khi7, hou7 Goa2 ti7 tou3-khi7-tiong bo5 biat8-bo5 in.  12). Sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 kong2, KhoaN3 ah, Goa2 eng7 Goa2 peng5-an e5 iok siuN2-su3 i;  13). beh choe3 i kap i e5 hou7-e3 eng2-oan2 choe3 che3-si e5 chit e5 iok, in-ui7 i ui7-tioh8 i e5 Siong7-te3 u7 tou3-khi7 e5 sim, koh ui7-tioh8 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 siok8-choe7.  14). Hit e5 siu7-thai5 e5 I2-sek-liat8 lang5, chiu7-si7 kap Bi2-tian5 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 saN-kap siu7 chhak8-si2-e5, mia5-kio3 Sim-li7, si7 Sat-lou7 e5 kiaN2, si7 Se-bian7 chi-phai3-tiong chit8-chok8 e5 siu2-leng2.  15). Hit e5 siu7 chhak8-si2 Bi2-tian5 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 mia5-kio3 Ko-su-pi2, si7 Sou-jiN2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2; chit e5 Sou-jiN2 si7 Bi2-tian5 e5 peh-siN3 chit8-chok8 e5 thau5-lang5.
	16). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  17). Li2 tioh8 khun2-pek Bi2-tian5 lang5, koh phah in;  18). in-ui7 in eng7 khui2-khiat e5 ke3-bou5 khun2-pek lin2, ti7 Pi2-jiN2 e5 su7, kap in e5 chi2-be7, Bi2-tian5 siu2-leng2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, Ko-su-pi2 e5 su7, eng7 khui2-khiat e5 ke3-bou5 in2-iu2 lin2; chit e5 Ko-su-pi2, tng un-ek8 liu5-heng5 e5 jit8, in-ui7 Pi2-jiN2 e5 su7 i2-keng siu7 chhak8-si2.

[26]	Un-ek8 liau2-au7, Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kap che3-si A-lun5 e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-a-sat kong2,  2). Lin2 tioh8 chiong I2-sek-liat8 choan5-hoe7 e5 cheng3-lang5, chiau3 in e5 chong-chok8, kiN3-na7 I2-sek-liat8 tiong, tui3 ji7-chap8 he3 i2-chiuN7, oe7 chhut-khi3 kau-chian3 e5, tioh8 sng3 in e5 chong2-giah8.  3). Mou5-se kap che3-si I2-li7-a-sat, ti7 Mou5-ap e5 piN5-iuN5, Iok-tan3 ho5-piN, Ia5-li7-ko saN-tui3 e5 sou2-chai7, tui3 in kong2,  4). Tui3 ji7-chap8 he3 i2-chiuN7 sng3--i, chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se i2-kip8 chhut Ai-kip8 toe7 e5 I2-sek-liat8 lang5.
	5). I2-sek-liat8 e5 toa7-kiaN2 si7 Liu5-pian7; Liu5-pian7 chiah e5 kiaN2; siok8 Hap-lok8 e5, u7 Hap-lok8 chok8; siok8 Hoat-lou7 e5, u7 Hoat-lou7 chok8;  6). siok8 Hi-su-lun5 e5, u7 Hi-su-lun5 chok8; siok8 Ka-bi2 e5, u7 Ka-bi2 chok8.  7). Chiah-e5 chiu7-si7 Liu5-pian5 e5 tak8-chok8; ki5-tiong siu7-sng3-e5, kiong7 si3-ban7 saN-chheng chhit-pah saN-chap8 mia5.  8). Hoat-lou7 e5 kiaN2 si7 I2-li7-ap;  9). I2-li7-ap chiah e5 kiaN2 si7 Ni5-bou2-li7, Tai7-tan, A-pi2-lan5; chit e5 Tai7-tan, A-pi2-lan5, chiu7-si7 tui3 hoe7-tiong siu7-keng2-e5; Kho2-lah8 e5 tong2 kong-kek Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 si5, in ia7 kap in kong-kek Mou5-se A-lun5.  10). Hit-si5 toe7 khui-chhui3 thun in, kap Kho2-lah8; in hit-tong2 long2 si2; ia7 u7 he2 sio-si2 nng7-pah gou7-chap8 lang5, eng7 in choe3 kam3-kai3.  11). Chong2-si7 Kho2-lah8 chiah e5 kiaN2 bo5 si2.
	12). Se-bian7 chiah e5 kiaN2 chiau3 ke-chok8; siok8 Ni5-bou2-li7 e5, u7 Ni5-bou2-li7 chok8;  13). siok8 Nga2-bin2 e5, u7 Nga2-bin2 chok8; siok8 Nga2-kun e5, u7 Nga2-kun chok8; siok8 Sia7-lah8 e5, u7 Sia7-lah8 chok8; siok8 So3-lo5 e5, u7 So3-lo5 chok8.  14). Chiah-e5 si7 Se-bian7 e5 tak8-chok8, kiong7 nng7-ban7 nng7-chheng nng7-pah mia5.
	15). Ka-tek chiah e5 kiaN2, chiau3 ke-chok8; siok8 Se2-hun e5, u7 Se2-hun chok8; siok8 Hap-ki e5, u7 Hap-ki chok8; siok8 Su-ni5 e5, u7 Su-ni5 chok8;  16). siok8 A-su-ni5 e5, u7 A-su-ni5 chok8; siok8 I2-li7 e5, u7 I2-li7 chok8;  17). siok8 A-lut8 e5, u7 A-lut8 chok8; siok8 A-liat8-li7 e5, u7 A-liat8-li7 chok8.  18). Chiah-e5 si7 Ka-tek kiaN2-sun e5 tak8-chok8; in sou2 ke3-sng3 e5, kiong7 si3-ban7 lian5 gou7-pah mia5.
	19). Iu5-tai7 e5 kiaN2, JiN2 kap Go5-lam5; chit e5 JiN2 kap Go5-lam5 si2 ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7.  20). Iu5-tai7 ki5-u5 chiah e5 kiaN2, chiau3 in e5 ke-chok8; siok8 Si7-lah8 e5, u7 Si7-lah8 chok8; siok8 Hoat-lek8-su e5, u7 Hoat-lek8-su chok8; siok8 Sia7-lah8 e5, u7 Sia7-lah8 chok8.  21). Hoat-lek8-su e5 kiaN2; siok8 Hi-su-lun5 e5, u7 Hi-su-lun5 chok8; siok8 Hap-bou2-lek8 e5, u7 Hap-bou2-lek8 chok8.  22). Chiah-e5 si7 Iu5-tai7 e5 tak8-chok8; in ke3-sng3 e5, kiong7 chhit-ban7 lak8-chheng gou7-pah mia5.
	23). I2-sat-ka e5 kiaN2-sun, chiau3 in e5 chong-chok8; siok8 To5-lah8 e5, u7 To5-lah8 chok8; siok8 Phou2-oa2 e5, u7 Phou2-oa2 chok8;  24). siok8 Nga2-sut8 e5, u7 Nga2-sut8 chok8; siok8 Sin-lun5 e5, u7 Sin-lun5 chok8.  25). Chiah-e5 si7 I2-sat-ka e5 tak8-chok8; in ke3-sng3 e5, kiong7 lak8-ban7 si3-chheng saN-pah mia5.
	26). Se-pou3-lun5 e5 kiaN2-sun, chiau3 in e5 chong-chok8; siok8 Se-liat8 e5, u7 Se-liat8 chok8; siok8 I2-lun5 e5, u7 I2-lun5 chok8; siok8 Nga2-li7 e5, u7 Nga2-li7 chok8.  27). Chiah-e5 si7 Se-pou3-lun5 e5 tak8-chok8; in ke3-sng3 e5, kiong7 lak8-ban7 lian5 gou7-pah mia5.
	28). Iok-sek e5 kiaN2-sun, chiau3 in e5 chong-chok8, u7 Ma2-na2-se, I2-hoat-lian5.  29). Ma2-na2-se e5 kiaN2-sun; siok8 Ma2-kiat, u7 Ma2-kiat chok8; Ma2-kiat siN Ki-liat8; siok8 Ki-liat8 e5, u7 Ki-liat8 chok8.  30). Chiah-e5 si7 Ki-liat8 e5 kiaN2-sun; siok8 I-i2-sia7 e5, u7 I-i2-sia7 chok8; siok8 Hi-lek8 e5, u7 Hi-lek8 chok8;  31). siok8 A-su-liat8 e5, u7 A-su-liat8 chok8; siok8 Si7-kiam3 e5, u7 Si7-kiam3 chok8;  32). siok8 Si7-bi2-tai7 e5, u7 Si7-bi2-tai7 chok8; siok8 Hi-hut e5, u7 Hi-hut chok8;  33). Hi-hut e5 kiaN2 Se-lo5-hui-hap bo5 kiaN2, chi2-u7 cha-bou2-kiaN2; Se-lo5-hui-hap cha-bou2-kiaN2 e5 mia5, chiu7-si7 Ma2-lah8, Na2-a, Hat-lah8, Bit8-ka, Tek-sat.  34). chiah-e5 si7 Ma2-na2-se e5 tak8-chok8; in ke3-sng3-e5, kiong7 gou7-ban7 nng7-chheng chhit-pah mia5.
	35). Chiah-e5 si7 I2-hoat-lian5 e5 kiaN2-sun, chiau3 in e5 chong-chok8; siok8 Su-the5-lah8 e5, u7 Su-the5-lah8 chok8, siok8 Pi2-kiat e5, u7 Pi2-kiat chok8; siok8 Tha-han2 e5, u7 Tha-han2 chok8.  36). Chiah-e5 si7 Su-the5-lah8 e5 kiaN2-sun; siok8 I2-lan5 e5, u7 I2-lan5 chok8.  37). Chiah-e5 si7 I2-hoat-lian5 kiaN2-sun e5 tak8-chok8; in ke3-sng3-e5 kiong7 saN-ban7 nng7-chheng gou7-pah mia5.  Chiau3 in e5 chong-chok8, chiah-e5 si7 Iok-sek e5 kiaN2-sun.
	38). Pian7-nga2-bin2 e5 kiaN2-sun, chiau3 in chong-chok8; siok8 Pi2-lah8 e5, u7 Pi2-lah8 chok8; siok8 A-sit8-piat8 e5, u7 A-sit8-piat8 chok8; siok8 A-hi-lan5 e5, u7 A-hi-lan5 chok8;  39). siok8 Su-hoan2 e5, u7 Su-hoan2 chok8; siok8 Hou7-hoan2 e5, u7 Hou7-hoan2 chok8.  40). Pi2-lah8 e5 kiaN2-sun, si7 A-lek8, Nai2-ban7; siok8 A-lek8 e5, u7 A-lek8 chok8; siok8 Nai2-ban7 e5, u7 Nai2-ban7 chok8.  41). Chiau3 in e5 chong-chok8, chiah-e5 si7 Pian7-nga2-bin2 e5 kiaN2-sun; in ke3-sng3-e5, kiong7 si3-ban7 gou7-chheng lak8-pah mia5.
	42). Chiah-e5 si7 Tan3 e5 kiaN2-sun, chiau3 in e5 chong-chok8; siok8 Su-ham5 e5, u7 Su-ham5 chok8.  Chiau3 in e5 chong-chok8, chiah-e5 si7 Tan3 e5 tak8-chok8.  43). In ke3-sng3-e5, Su-ham5 sou2 u7 e5 tak8-chok8, kiong7 u7 lak8-ban7 si3-chheng si3-pah mia5.
	44). A-siat e5 kiaN2-sun, chiau3 in e5 chong-chok8; siok8 Im-na2 e5, u7 Im-na2 chok8; siok8 Ek8-si-ui2 e5, u7 Ek8-si-ui2 chok8; siok8 Pi2-li7-a e5, u7 Pi2-li7-a chok8.  45). Pi2-li7-a e5 kiaN2-sun, siok8 Hi-piat e5, u7 Hi-piat chok8; siok8 Ma2-kiat e5, u7 Ma2-kiat chok8.  46). A-siat e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 mia5 kio3 Se-lah8.  47). Chiah-e5 si7 A-siat kiaN2-sun e5 tak8-chok8; in ke3-sng3-e5, kiong7 gou7-ban7 saN-chheng si3-pah mia5.
	48). Na2-hut-tha-li7 e5 kiaN2-sun, chiau3 in e5 chong-chok8; siok8 Nga2-siat e5, u7 Nga2-siat chok8; siok8 Kou-ni5 e5, u7 Kou-ni5 chok8;  49). siok8 Ia5-sek e5, u7 Ia5-sek chok8; siok8 Si7-leng2 e5, u7 Si7-leng2 chok8.  50). Chiau3 in e5 chong-chok8, chiah-e5 si7 Na2-hut-tha-li7 e5 tak8-chok8; in ke3-sng3-e5, kiong7 si3-ban7 gou7-chheng si3-pah mia5.
	51). Chiah-e5 long2 si7 I2-sek-liat8 kiaN2-sun, in ke3-sng3-e5, kiong7 u7 lak8-chap8-ban7 lian5 chit8-chheng chhit-pah saN-chap8 mia5.
	52). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  53). Hit e5 toe7 tioh8 pun hou7 chiah e5 lang5 choe3 san2-giap8, chiau3 in e5 mia5-giah8.  54). Lang5 choe7-e5, tioh8 pun hou7 in khah-choe7 giap8, lang5 chio2-e5, tioh8 pun hou7 in khah-chio2; tioh8 chiau3 i ke3-sng3 e5 lang5-giah8, eng7 giap8 pun hou7 tak8-lang5.  55). Chong2-si7 hit e5 toe7 tioh8 liam-khau lai5 pun i, tak8-lang5 chiau3 i chou2-chong chiah e5 chi-phai3 e5 mia5, lai5 seng5-chiap chiah e5 giap8.  56). Tioh8 chiau3 sou2 liam e5 khau, khoaN3 lang5-giah8 choe7, lang5-giah8 chio2, eng7 san2-giap8 pun hou7 in.
	57). Chiah-e5 chiu7-si7 Li7-bi7 lang5, chiau3 in e5 chong-chok8 ke3-sng3-e5; siok8 Kek-sun7 e5, u7 Kek-sun7 chok8; siok8 Ko-hat e5, u7 Ko-hat chok8; siok8 Bi2-lah8-li7 e5, u7 Bi2-lah8-li7 chok8.  58). Chiah-e5 si7 Li7-bi7 e5 tak8-chok8; u7 Lip8-ni5 chok8, Hi-pek-lun5 chok8, Ma2-li7 chok8, Bou2-si7 chok8, Kho2-lah8 chok8.  Ko-hat siN Am3-lan5.  59). Am3-lan5 e5 bou2 mia5-kio3 Iok-ki5-piat8, si7 Li7-bi7 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2; i e5 lau7-bu2 ti7 Ai-kip8 tui3 Li7-bi7 siN e5; i tui3 Am3-lan5 siN A-lun5, Mou5-se, kap in e5 toa7-chi2 Bi2-li7-am3.  60). Tui3 A-lun5 siN Na2-tap, A-pi2-hou7, I2-li7-a-sat, I2-tha-ma2.  61). Na2-tap A-pi2-hou7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 hian3 pat8-ho7 he2 e5 si5, chiu7 si2.  62). In tiong-kan chit8-geh8-jit8 i2-goa7, ke3-sng3 e5 ta-pou-teng, kiong7 nng7-ban7 saN-chheng; in-ui7 in ti7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tiong bo5 sng3 chai7-lai7, in-ui7 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tiong bo5 eng7 san2-giap8 hou7 in.
	63). Chiah-e5 chiu7-si7 hou7 Mou5-se kap che3-si I2-li7-a-sat sou2 sng3-ke3 e5; in ti7 Mou5-ap piN5-iuN5, kap Ia5-li7-ko saN-tui3 e5 Iok-tan3 ho5-piN, tiam2-sng3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5.  64). Cheng5 Mou5-se kap che3-si A-lun5 ti7 Se-nai2 e5 khong3-ia2 sng3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5, hit-si5 sou2 sng3-e5, taN bo5 chit8-e5 ti7-teh.  65). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lun7-kau3 in bat kong2, In tek-khak tioh8 si2 ti7 khong3-ia2; sou2-i2 tu5 Ia5-hu-ni5 e5 kiaN2 Ka-lek8, kap Lun3 e5 kiaN2 Iok-su-a i2-goa7, hiah e5 lang5 bo5 lau5 chit8-lang5 ti7-teh.

[27]	Siok8 Iok-sek e5 kiaN2 Ma2-na2-se e5 chok8, u7 Ma2-na2-se e5 goan5-sun, Ma2-kiat e5 cheng-sun, Ki-liat8 e5 sun, Hi-hut e5 kiaN2, Se-lo5-hui-hap e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, mia5-kio3 Ma2-lah8, Na2-a, Hat-lah8, Bit8-ka, Tek-sat;  2). in chin3-cheng5 lai5, khia7 ti7 hoe7-bou7 mng5-khau2, ti7 Mou5-se kap che3-si {A-lun5}, I2-li7-a-sat, i2-kip8 cheng3 siu2-leng2, kap hoe7-chiong3 e5 bin7-cheng5, kong2,  3). Goan2 lau7-pe7 si2 ti7 khong3-ia2, i m7-si7 ti7 Kho2-lah8 e5 tong2-lai7, tang5-tong2 chu7-chip8 kong-kek Ia5-ho5-hoa; si7 ti7 ka-ki7 e5 choe7-tiong si2; i ia7 bo5 kiaN2.  4). SiaN2-su7 in-ui7 goan2 lau7-pe7 bo5 kiaN2, chiu7 chiong i e5 mia5 tui3 i e5 chok8-tiong tu5-khi3 ah? ChhiaN2 ti7 goan2 lau7-pe7 e5 hiaN-ti7 tiong pun giap8 hou7 goan2.  5). Mou5-se chiu7 chiong in e5 an3-kiaN7 pai5-liat8 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5.  6). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  7). Se-lo5-hui-hap e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 sou2-kong2-e5 u7 cheng5-li2; li2 tek-khak tioh8 ti7 in lau7-pe7 e5 hiaN-ti7 tiong, pun toe7 hou7 in choe3-giap8, tioh8 chiong in lau7-pe7 e5 san2-giap8 kui hou7 in.  8). Li2 ia7 tioh8 hoan-hu3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kong2, Lang5 na7 si2 bo5 kiaN2, chiu7 tioh8 chiong i e5 san2-giap8 kui hou7 i e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2.  9). I na7 bo5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, chiu7 tioh8 chiong i e5 giap8 hou7 i e5 hiaN-ti7.  10). I na7 bo5 hiaN-ti7, chiu7 tioh8 chiong i e5 giap8 hou7 i e5 lau7-pe7 e5 hiaN-ti7.  11). I e5 lau7-pe7 na7 bo5 hiaN-ti7, chiu7 tioh8 chiong i e5 giap8 hou7 i e5 chok8-tiong chi3-chhin e5, i chiu7 tit-tioh8 choe3-giap8; che beh choe3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 toan3 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 le7; si7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 hoan-hu3 Mou5-se e5.
	12). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 chiuN7 chit e5 A-pa-lim5 e5 soaN, khoaN3 Goa2 siuN2-su3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 toe7.  13). KhoaN3 liau2-au7 li2 ia7 beh to3-chou2; chhin-chhiuN7 li2 e5 hiaN A-lun5 to3--khi3 chit8-iuN7.  14). In-ui7 lin2 ti7 Sim5 e5 khong3-ia2, tng hoe7-chiong3 ke3-kau3 e5 si5, ui5-poe7 Goa2 e5 oe7, bo5 ti7 chheng3-chhut chui2 e5 sou2-chai7, hoe7-chiong3 e5 bin7-cheng5, chun Goa2 choe3-seng3. (Chit e5 chui2 chiu7-si7 ti7 Sim5 e5 khong3-ia2, Ka-te-su e5 Bi2-li7-pa e5 chui2.)  15). Mou5-se tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, SiuN2-su3 oah8-mia7 hou7 kiN3-na7 u7 jiok8-the2--e5 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah,  16). goan7 Li2 siat-lip8 chit8-lang5 lai5 ti7-li2 hoe7-chiong3,  17). thang ti7 in e5 bin7-cheng5 chhut-khi3, ia7 ti7 in e5 bin7-cheng5 jip8-lai5, thang chhoa7 in chhut-khi3, ia7 chhoa7 in jip8-lai5, bian2-tit Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 hoe7-chiong3 chhin-chhiuN7 bo5 bok8-chia2 e5 iuN5-kun5 chit8-poaN.  18). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Lun3 e5 kiaN2 Iok-su-a, i e5 sim-lai7 u7 seng3-sin5, li2 chhoa7 i lai5, hoaN7-chhiu2 ti7 i e5 teng2-bin7;  19). hou7 i khia7 ti7 che3-si I2-li7-a-sat kap choan5-hoe7 e5 bin7-cheng5, eng7 chit-jim7 beng7-leng7 i.  20). Koh tui3 li2 e5 eng5-kng pun hou7 i, hou7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 choan5-hoe7 long2 thiaN-than3 i.  21). I tioh8 khia7 ti7 che3-si I2-li7-a-sat e5 bin7-cheng5, I2-li7-a-sat tioh8 chiau3 OU-leng5 e5 phoaN3-toan3, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, thoe3 i kiu5-mng7; i kap I2-sek-liat8 choan5-hoe7 e5 cheng3-lang5 long2 tioh8 chiau3 i e5 beng7-leng7 lai5 chhut, chiau3 i e5 beng7-leng7 lai5 jip8.  22). Mou5-se chiu7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beng7-leng7 i-e5 lai5 kiaN5; i chhoa7 Iok-su-a lai5, hou7 i khia7 ti7 che3-si I2-li7-a-sat kap choan5-hoe7 e5 bin7-cheng5,  23). hoaN7-chhiu2 ti7 i e5 teng2-bin7, eng7 beng7-leng7 kau-thok i; si7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa thok Mou5-se sou2 kong2 e5 oe7.

[28]	Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  2). Li2 tioh8 beng7-leng7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kong2, Goa2 e5 le2-mih8, chiu7-si7 hian3-hou7 Goa2 choe3 phang-phang chiah e5 he2-che3 e5 chiah8-mih8, lin2 tioh8 chiau3 jit8-ki5 kin2-sin7 hian3 hou7 Goa2.  3). Koh tioh8 ka7 in kong2, Lin2 tioh8 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 he2-che3, chiu7-si7 bo5 ha5-chhu5 be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2, tak8-jit8 nng7-chiah, choe3 ku2-tng5 hian3 e5 sio-che3.  4). Cha2-khi2-si5 tioh8 hian3 iuN5-a2 chit8-chiah, hong5-hun e5 si5 tioh8 hian3 iuN5-a2 chit8-chiah.  5). Koh tioh8 hian3 iu3-mi7-hun2 i-hoat chap8-hun7-chit8, kap tiau-ho5 khoeh-ho2 e5 iu5 chit8-him si3-hun7-chit8 choe3 sou3-che3.  6). Che si7 ti7 Se-nai2 soaN sou2 tiaN7-tioh8 choe3 siong5-siong5 hian3 e5 sio-che3, chiu7-si7 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 phang-phang e5 he2-che3.  7). Ui7-tioh8 chi2 chit8 chiah iuN5-a2, tioh8 soa3 hian3 koan3-tian7 e5 chiu2, chit8-him si3-hun7 e5 chit8-hun7; ti7 seng3-sou2 tiong, li2 tioh8 chiong kau7 e5 chiu2 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 koan3-tian7.  8). E5-hng si5, tioh8 hian3 te7-ji7 chiah iuN5-a2, chhin-chhiuN7 cha2-khi2-si5 e5 sou3-che3, ia7 chhin-chhiuN7 i e5 koan3-tian7, hian3 i hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 phang-phang e5 he2-che3.
	9). Koh ti7 an-hioh-jit8 tioh8 hian3 nng7-chiah bo5 ha5-chhu5 be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2, ia7 eng7 tiau-ho5 iu5 e5 iu3-mi7-hun2 i-hoat chap8-hun7 e5 nng7-hun7, choe3 sou3-che3, kap i e5 koan3-tian7.  10). Che si7 tak8 e5 an-hioh-jit8 e5 sio-che3, hit e5 siong5-siong5 hian3 e5 sio-che3, kap i e5 koan3-tian7 i2-goa7.
	11). Tak8-geh8 e5 chhoe-it, lin2 tioh8 hian3 sio-che3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, chiu7-si7 gu5-kang2-a2 nng7-chiah8, mi5-iuN5-kang2 chit8-chiah, bo5 ha5-chhu5 be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2 chhit-chiah.  12). Ui7 tak8 chiah gu5-kang2-a2, tioh8 eng7 tiau-ho5 iu5 e5 iu3-mi7-hun2 i-hoat chap8-hun7 e5 saN-hun7, choe3 sou3-che3; ui7 hit chiah iuN5-kang2, ia7 tioh8 eng7 tiau-ho5 iu5 e5 iu3-mi7-hun2 i-hoat chap8-hun7 e5 nng7-hun7, choe3 sou3-che3.  13). Ui7-tioh8 tak8 chiah iuN5-a2 tioh8 eng7 tiau-ho5 iu5 e5 iu3-mi7-hun2 chap8-hun7 e5 chit8-hun7, choe3 sou3-che3, kap phang-phang e5 sio-che3; si7 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 he2-che3.  14). I e5 koan3-tian7 tioh8 eng7 chiu2, ui7-tioh8 chit8 chiah gu5-kang2-a2 eng7 poaN3-him, ui7-tioh8 chit8 chiah iuN5-kang2 eng7 chit8-him e5 saN-hun7-chit8, ui7-tioh8 chit8 chiah iuN5-a2 chiu7 eng7 chit8-him e5 si3-hun7-chit8; che si7 tak8-geh8 e5 sio-che3, chit8-ni5 e5 tiong-kan, tak8-geh8 tioh8 an2-ni.  15). Koh tioh8 eng7 chit8 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2 choe3 siok8-choe7-che3, hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa; tioh8 ti7 siong5-siong5 hian3 e5 sio-che3, kap i e5 koan3-tian7, i2-goa7 lai5 hian3 i.
	16). ChiaN-geh8 chap8-si3 jit8 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 poaN5-ke3-choeh.  17). Chit-geh8 chap8-gou7 jit8 si7 choeh-ian5; tioh8 chiah8 bo5-kaN3-piaN2 chhit-jit8 ku2.  18). Ti7 i e5 thau5-chit8 jit8 tioh8 u7 seng3-hoe7, long2 m7-thang choe3 lo5-tong7 e5 kang.  19). Li2 tioh8 hian3 he2-che3 choe3 sio-che3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, chiu7-si7 gu5-kang2-a2 nng7-chiah, mi5-iuN5-kang2 chit8-chiah, be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2 chhit-chiah; lin2 long2 tioh8 eng7 bo5 ha5-chhu5 e5.  20). In e5 sou3-che3, eng7 tiau-ho5 iu5 e5 iu3-mi7-hun2, ui7-tioh8 chit8 chiah gu5-kang2 hian3 chap8-hun7-saN, ui7-tioh8 chit8 chiah iuN5-kang2 hian3 chap8-hun7-nng7.  21). Ui7-tioh8 hi2 chhit chiah iuN5-a2, tak8 chiah tioh8 hian3 chap8-hun7-chit8.  22). Koh hian3 chit8 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2 choe3 siok8-choe7-che3, ka7 lin2 siok8-choe7.  23). Lin2 hian3 chiah-e5, tioh8 ti7 cha2-khi2-si5 e5 sio-che3, chiu7-si7 siong5-siong5 hian3 e5 sio-che3 i2-goa7.  24). Lian5-lian5 chhit-jit8 ku2, tak8-jit8 chiau3 chit e5 le7, eng7 phang-phang e5 he2-che3 e5 chiah8-mih8, hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa; tioh8 ti7 siong5-siong5 hian3 e5 sio-che3, kap i e5 koan3-tian7, i2-goa7 lai5 hian3.  25). Te7-chhit jit8 lin2 tioh8 u7 seng3-hoe7, long2 m7-thang choe3 sim2-mih8 lo5-tong7 e5 kang5.
	26). Chhit e5 chhit jit8 choeh, khi2-thau5-sek8 e5 thou2-san2, lin2 hian3 sin e5 sou3-che3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 jit8, tioh8 u7 seng3-hoe7, long2 m7-thang choe3 lo5-tong7 e5 kang.  27). Lin2 tioh8 hian3 phang-phang e5 sio-che3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, chiu7-si7 gu5-kang2-a2 nng7-chiah, mi5-iuN5-kang2-a2 chit8-chiah, be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2 chhit-chiah.  28). In e5 sou3-che3, eng7 tiau-ho5 iu5 e5 iu3-mi7-hun2, ui7-tioh8 chit8 chiah gu5-kang2 hian3 chap8-hun7-saN, ui7-tioh8 chit8 chiah iuN5-kang2 hian3 chap8-hun7-nng7.  29). Ui7-tioh8 hi2 chhit chiah iuN5-a2, tak8-chiah tioh8 hian3 chap8-hun7-chit8.  30). Koh hian3 chit8 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2, ka7 lin2 siok8-choe7.  31). Lin2 tioh8 hian3 chiah-e5, kap i e5 koan3-tian7, ti7 siong5-siong5 hian3 e5 sio-che3 kap i e5 sou3-che3 i2-goa7, lin2 long2 tioh8 eng7 bo5 ha5-chhu5-e5.

[29]	Chhit-geh8 chhoe-it lin2 tioh8 u7 seng3-hoe7, long2 m7-thang choe3 lo5-tong7 e5 kang; che si7 lin2 pun5 sau3-kak e5 jit8.  2). Lin2 tioh8 hian3 phang-phang e5 sio-che3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, chiu7-si7 gu5-kang2-a2 chit8-chiah, mi5-iuN5-kang2 chit8-chiah, be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2 chhit-chiah, long2 tioh8 bo5 ha5-chhu5-e5.  3). In e5 sou3-che3, eng7 tiau-ho5 iu5 e5 iu3-mi7-hun2, ui7-tioh8 chit8 chiah gu5-kang2 hian3 i-hoat chap8-hun7-saN, ui7-tioh8 chit8-chiah iuN5-kang2 hian3 chap8-hun7-nng7.  4). Ui7-tioh8 hi2 chhit chiah iuN5-a2, tak8-chiah tioh8 hian3 chap8-hun7-chit8.  5). Koh hian3 chit8 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2 choe3 siok8-choe7-che3, ka7 lin2 siok8-choe7.  6). Chiah-e5 si7 tak8-geh8 chhoe-it e5 sio-che3, kap i e5 sou3-che3, i2-kip8 siong5-siong5 hian3 e5 sio-che3, kap in e5 sou3-che3, i2-kip8 i e5 koan3-tian7, kok chiau3 i e5 le7 i2-goa7, long2 choe3 phang-phang e5 he2-che3 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
	7). Chhit-geh8 chhoe-chap8 jit8, lin2 tioh8 u7 seng3-hoe7, tioh8 khek-khou2 ka-ki7 e5 sim, long2 m7-thang choe3-kang.  8). Lin2 tioh8 hian3 phang-phang e5 sio-che3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, chiu7-si7 gu5-kang2-a2 chit8-chiah, mi5-iuN5-kang2 chit8-chiah, be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-kang2-a2 chhit-chiah, long2 tioh8 bo5 ha5-chhu5-e5.  9). In e5 sou3-che3, eng7 tiau-ho5 iu5 e5 iu3-mi7-hun2, ui7-tioh8 chit8 chiah gu5-kang2 hian3 chap8-hun7-saN, ui7-tioh8 chit8 chiah iuN5-kang2 hian3 chap8-hun7-nng7;  10). ui7-tioh8 hi2 chhit-chiah iuN5-a2, tak8-chiah tioh8 hian3 chap8-hun7-chit8.  11). Koh hian3 chit8 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2 choe3 siok8-choe7-che3; che si7 ti7 siok8-choe7-che3, kap siong5-siong5 hian3 e5 sio-che3, kap in e5 sou3-che3, i2-kip8 in e5 koan3-tian7 i2-goa7.
	12). Chhit-geh8 chap8-gou7 jit8, lin2 tioh8 u7 seng3-hoe7, long2 m7-thang choe3 lo5-tong7 e5 kang; tioh8 chhit-jit8 ku2 siu2-choeh hok8-sai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  13). Lin2 tioh8 hian3 sio-che3 choe3 phang-phang e5 he2-che3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, chiu7-si7 soe3-chiah e5 gu5-kang2-a2 chap8-saN chiah, mi5-iuN5-kang2 nng7-chiah, be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-a2 chap8-si3 chiah, long2 tioh8 bo5 ha5-chhu5-e5.  14). In e5 sou3-che3 eng7 tiau-ho5 iu5 e5 iu3-mi7-hun2, ui7-tioh8 chi2 chap8-saN chiah gu5-kang2, tak8 chiah gu5-kang2 hian3 chap8-hun7-saN, ui7-tioh8 nng7 chiah mi5-iuN5-kang2, tak8 chiah mi5-iuN5-kang2 hian3 chap8-hun7-nng7,  15). ui7-tioh8 hi2 chap8-si3 chiah iuN5-a2, tak8 chiah iuN5-a2 hian3 chap8-hun7-chit8.  16). Ia7 hian3 chit8 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2 choe3 siok8-choe7-che3; che si7 ti7 siong5-siong5 hian3 e5 sio-che3, kap i e5 sou3-che3, kap i e5 koan3-tian7 i2-goa7.
	17). Te7-ji7 jit8 tioh8 hian3 soe3-chiah gu5-kang2-a2 chap8-ji7 chiah, mi5-iuN5-kang2 nng7-chiah, be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-a2 chap8-si3-chiah, long2 tioh8 bo5 ha5-chhu5-e5;  18). ia7 ui7-tioh8 gu5-kang2, iuN5-kang2, kap iuN5-a2, soa3 hian3 i e5 sou3-che3, i e5 koan3-tian7, long2 chiau3 in e5 siau3-giah8, chiau3 hit e5 le7;  19). ia7 hian3 chit8 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2 choe3 siok8-choe7-che3; che si7 ti7 siong5-siong5 hian3 e5 sio-che3, kap i e5 sou3-che3, kap i e5 koan3-tian7 i2-goa7.
	20). Te7-saN jit8 tioh8 hian3 gu5-kang2-a2 chap8-it-chiah, mi5-iuN5-kang2 nng7-chiah, be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-a2 chap8-si3-chiah, long2 tioh8 bo5 ha5-chhu5-e5;  21). ia7 ui7-tioh8 gu5-kang2, iuN5-kang2, kap iuN5-a2, soa3 hian3 i e5 sou3-che3, i e5 koan3-tian7, long2 chiau3 in e5 siau3-giah8, chiau3 hit e5 le7;  22). ia7 hian3 chit8 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2 choe3 siok8-choe7-che3; che si7 ti7 siong5-siong5 hian3 e5 sio-che3, kap i e5 sou3-che3, kap i e5 koan3-tian7 i2-goa7.
	23). Te7-si3 jit8 tioh8 hian3 gu5-kang2-a2 chap8-chiah, mi5-iuN5-kang2 nng7-chiah, be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-a2 chap8-si3-chiah, long2 tioh8 bo5 ha5-chhu5-e5;  24). ia7 ui7-tioh8 gu5-kang2, iuN5-kang2, kap iuN5-a2, soa3 hian3 i e5 sou3-che3, i e5 koan3-tian7, long2 chiau3 in e5 siau3-giah8, chiau3 hit e5 le7;  25). ia7 hian3 chit8 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2 choe3 siok8-choe7-che3; che si7 ti7 siong5-siong5 hian3 e5 sio-che3, kap i e5 sou3-che3, kap i e5 koan3-tian7 i2-goa7.
	26). Te7-gou7 jit8 tioh8 hian3 gu5-kang2-a2 kau2-chiah, mi5-iuN5-kang2 nng7-chiah, be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-a2 chap8-si3-chiah, long2 tioh8 bo5 ha5-chhu5-e5;  27). ia7 ui7-tioh8 gu5-kang2, iuN5-kang2, kap iuN5-a2, soa3 hian3 i e5 sou3-che3, i e5 koan3-tian7, long2 chiau3 in e5 siau3-giah8, chiau3 hit e5 le7;  28). ia7 hian3 chit8 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2 choe3 siok8-choe7-che3; che si7 ti7 siong5-siong5 hian3 e5 sio-che3, kap i e5 sou3-che3, kap i e5 koan3-tian7 i2-goa7.
	29). Te7-lak8 jit8 tioh8 hian3 gu5-kang2-a2 poeh-chiah, mi5-iuN5-kang2 nng7-chiah, be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-a2 chap8-si3-chiah, long2 tioh8 bo5 ha5-chhu5-e5;  30). ia7 ui7-tioh8 gu5-kang2, iuN5-kang2, kap iuN5-a2, soa3 hian3 i e5 sou3-che3, i e5 koan3-tian7, long2 chiau3 in e5 siau3-giah8, chiau3 hit e5 le7;  31). ia7 hian3 chit8 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2 choe3 siok8-choe7-che3; che si7 ti7 siong5-siong5 hian3 e5 sio-che3, kap i e5 sou3-che3, kap i e5 koan3-tian7 i2-goa7.
	32). Te7-chhit jit8 tioh8 hian3 gu5-kang2-a2 chhit-chiah, mi5-iuN5-kang2 nng7-chiah, be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-a2 chap8-si3 chiah, long2 tioh8 bo5 ha5-chhu5-e5;  33). ia7 ui7-tioh8 gu5-kang2, iuN5-kang2, kap iuN5-a2, soa3 hian3 i e5 sou3-che3, i e5 koan3-tian7, long2 chiau3 in e5 siau3-giah8, chiau3 hit e5 le7;  34). ia7 hian3 chit8 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2 choe3 siok8-choe7-che3; che si7 ti7 siong5-siong5 hian3 e5 sio-che3 kap i e5 sou3-che3, kap i e5 koan3-tian7 i2-goa7.
	35). Te7-poeh jit8 lin2 tioh8 u7 giam5-siok-hoe7, long2 m7-thang choe3 lo5-tong7 e5 kang.  36). Lin2 tioh8 hian3 sio-che3 choe3 phang-phang e5 he2-che3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, chiu7-si7 gu5-kang2 chit8-chiah, mi5-iuN5-kang2 chit8-chiah, be7-moa2-ni5 e5 iuN5-a2 chhit-chiah, bo5 ha5-chhu5-e5;  37). ia7 ui7-tioh8 gu5-kang2, iuN5-kang2, kap iuN5-a2, soa3 hian3 i e5 sou3-che3, i e5 koan3-tian7, long2 chiau3 in e5 siau3-giah8, chiau3 hit e5 le7;  38). ia7 hian3 chit8 chiah kang e5 soaN-iuN5 choe3 siok8-choe7-che3; che si7 ti7 siong5-siong5 hian3 e5 sio-che3 kap i e5 sou3-che3, kap i e5 koan3-tian7 i2-goa7.
	39). Ti7 lin2 chiah e5 choeh-ki5, tioh8 eng7 chiah-e5 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, long2 ti7 sou2 he7 e5 goan7, kap kam-sim sou2 hian3-e5 i2-goa7, choe3 lin2 e5 sio-che3, sou3-che3, koan3-tian7, kap peng5-an-che3.  40). Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beng7-leng7 Mou5-se e5, Mou5-se chiu7 chiau3 an2-ni long2 ka7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kong2.

[30]	Mou5-se hoan-hu3 I2-sek-liat8 tak8 chi-phai3 e5 thau5-lang5, ka7 in kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beng7-leng7-e5 si7 an2-ni.  2). Lang5 na7 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa he7-goan7, a2-si7 chiu3-choa7, eng7 chit8 e5 iok ka-ki7 iok-sok, chiu7 m7-thang thun-chiah8 i e5 oe7, tioh8 chiau3 i e5 chhui3 sou2 kong2-chhut-e5, it-chin7 kiaN5 i.  3). Cha-bou2-gin2-a2 siau3-lian5 iau2 ti7 lau7-pe7 e5 ke e5 si5, na7 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa he7-goan7, eng7 iok lai5 ka-ki7 iok-sok,  4). i e5 lau7-pe7 thiaN-kiN3 i sou2 he7 e5 goan7, kap iok-sok ka-ki7 e5 iok, i e5 lau7-pe7 na7 cheng7-cheng7 bo5 chhap i, i sou2 he7 chiah e5 goan7 tek-khak seng5-lip8, i sou2 ka-ki7 iok-sok e5 iok, ia7 tek-khak seng5-lip8.  5). Chong2-si7 lau7-pe7 thiaN-kiN3 e5 jit8, bo5 un2-chun2 i, i sou2 he7 chiah e5 goan7 kap ka-ki7 iok-sok hiah e5 iok, long2 bo5 seng5-lip8; Ia5-ho5-hoa ia7 beh sia3-bian2 i, in-ui7 i e5 lau7-pe7 bo5 un2-chun2.  6). I chhut-ke3 e5 si5, na7 i2-keng u7 he7-goan7, a2-si7 i e5 chhui3 sui5-pian7 kong2-chhut iok-sok ka-ki7 e5 oe7 ti7 i e5 sin-chiuN7;  7). i e5 tiong7-hu na7 thiaN-kiN3, ia7 ti7 thiaN-kiN3 e5 jit8 cheng7-cheng7 bo5 chhap i, chiu7 i sou2 he7 chiah e5 goan7, tek-khak seng5-lip8; i ka-ki7 iok-sok e5 iok, ia7 tek-khak seng5-lip8.  8). Chong2-si7 i e5 tiong7-hu thiaN-kiN3 e5 jit8, bo5 un2-chun2 i, chiu7 hoe3-bo5 i sou2 he7 e5 goan7, kap i e5 chhui3 sui5-pian7 kong2-chhut iok-sok ka-ki7 e5 oe7, Ia5-ho5-hoa ia7 beh sia3-bian2 i.  9). Chiu2-koaN2 hu7-jin5-lang5, a2-si7 siu7 li7-chhut e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, sou2 he7 e5 goan7, kap i ka-ki7 iok-sok e5 oe7, long2 beh seng5-lip8 ti7 i e5 sin-chiuN7.  10). Hu7-jin5-lang5 na7 ti7 tiong7-hu e5 chhu3 he7-goan7, a2-si7 chiu3-choa7, eng7 iok lai5 iok-sok ka-ki7,  11). tiong7-hu thiaN-kiN3, cheng7-cheng7 bo5 chhap i, ia7 bo5 m7 un2-chun2, i sou2 he7 chiah e5 goan7 long2 beh seng5-lip8, ia7 i iok-sok ka-ki7 e5 iok ia7 beh seng5-lip8.  12). Chong2-si7 tiong7-hu thiaN-kiN3 e5 jit8, na7 ka7 i hoe3-bo5, kiN3-na7 i e5 chhui3 sou2 chhut e5, hek8-si7 sou2 he7 e5 goan7, a2-si7 ka-ki7 iok-e5, chiu7 long2 boe7 seng5-lip8; in-ui7 i e5 tiong7-hu i2-keng hoe3-bo5 i; Ia5-ho5-hoa ia7 beh sia3-bian2 i.  13). KiN3-na7 sou2 he7 e5 goan7, kap iok-sok e5 chiu3-choa7, lai5 khek-khou2 ka-ki7, i e5 tiong7-hu thang seng5-lip8 i, i e5 tiong7-hu ia7 thang hoe3-bo5 i.  14). Chong2-si7 i e5 tiong7-hu jit8-jit8 cheng7-cheng7 bo5 chhap i, chiu7 seng5-lip8 i sou2 he7 hiah e5 goan7, kap iok-sok i e5 oe7, in-ui7 i e5 tiong7-hu thiaN-kiN3 e5 jit8 cheng7-cheng5 bo5 chhap i, i chiu7 seng5-lip8 i.  15). Chong2-si7 tiong7-hu thiaN-kiN3 liau2-au7 hoe3-bo5 i, chiu7 i tioh8 tam-tng hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 choe7.  16). Chiah-e5 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beng7-leng7 Mou5-se e5, lun7-khi2 tiong7-hu tui3 ti7 hu7-jin5-lang5, lau7-pe7 tui3 ti7 siau3-lian5 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 toa3 ti7 ke-lai7 e5 kui-le7.

[31]	Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  2). Li2 tioh8 kong-kek Bi2-tian5 lang5, thoe3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 po3-siu5; au7-lai7 li2 beh to3-chou2.  3). Mou5-se hoan-hu3 peh-siN3 kong2, Tioh8 tui3 lin2 tiong-kan pi7-pan7 lang5 toa3 ke-si chhut-khi3 kong-kek Bi2-tian5, thang ti7 Bi2-tian5 lang5 e5 sin-chiuN7 ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa po3-siu5.  4). Tioh8 tui3 I2-sek-liat8 cheng3 chi-phai3 e5 tiong-kan, tak8 chi-phai3 tioh8 chhe chit8-chheng lang5 khi3 kau-chian3.  5). Chiu7 tui3 I2-sek-liat8 chiah e5 chok8-tiong, tak8 chi-phai3 chhut chit8-chheng lang5, kiong7 chit8-ban7 nng7-chheng lang5, toa3 ke-si pi7-pan7 kau-chian3.  6). Mou5-se chiu7 chhe mui2 chi-phai3 chit8-chheng lang5 khi3 kau-chian3; in kap che3-si I2-li7-a-sat e5 kiaN2 Hui-ni5-hap khi3 kau-chian3; Hui-ni5-hap chhiu2 theh8 seng3-sou2 e5 khi3-ku7, kap pun5 toa7-siaN e5 ho7-thau5.  7). In chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beng7-leng7 Mou5-se e5, kap Bi2-tian5 lang5 kau-chian3; it-chin7 thai5-si2 in e5 ta-pou-teng.  8). Ti7 sou2 thai5-si2 e5 lang5 e5 tiong-kan, ia7 thai5-si2 Bi2-tian5 chiah e5 ong5, chiu7-si7 I2-bi2, Li7-kim, Sou-jiN2, Hou7-jiN2, Li7-pa, Bi2-tian5 gou7 e5 ong5; koh eng7 to thai5-si2 Pi2-jiN2 e5 kiaN2 Pa-lan5.  9). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 liah8 Bi2-tian5 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, kap in e5 gin2-a2, ia7 chiong in it-chhe3 e5 cheng-siN, it-chhe3 iuN5-kun5, kap it-chhe3 e5 chai5-but8 long2 chhiuN2 lai5, choe3 chhiuN2-mih8.  10). Koh eng7 he2 sio in sou2 khia7-khi2 e5 toe7, hiah e5 siaN5, kap in sou2 u7 e5 iaN5-poaN5;  11). chiong it-chhe3 sou2 chhiuN2 e5, sou2 liah8 e5, lang5 kap cheng-siN, long2 toa3-lai5.  12). Chiong sou2 liah8 e5 lang5, i2-kip8 sou2 chhiuN2 sou2 theh8 e5 mih8, long2 toa3 kau3 Mou5-ap e5 piN5-iuN5, ti7 Iok-tan3 ho5-piN, kap Ia5-li7-ko saN-tui3 e5 iaN5-poaN5, kau hou7 Mou5-se, kap che3-si I2-li7-a-sat, kap I2-sek-liat8 e5 hoe7-chiong3.
	13). Mou5-se kap che3-si I2-li7-a-sat kap hoe7-chiong3 long2-chong2 e5 siu2-leng2, chhut-khi3 iaN5-goa7 ngia5-chih in.  14). Mou5-se siu7-khi3 hiah e5 tui3 kau-chian3 to3--lai5 e5 kun-tiuN2, chhian-chong2, peh-chong2.  15). Mou5-se tui3 in kong2, Lin2 lau5 chiah e5 hu7-lu2 iau2 oah8-teh mah?  16). KhoaN3 ah, in than3 Pa-lan5 e5 ke3-bou5, hou7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 ti7 Pi2-jiN2 e5 su7 tek-choe7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, ti3-kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 hoe7-chiong3 tu2-tioh8 un-ek8.  17). TaN tioh8 thai5-si2 soe3-kiaN2-tiong long2-chong2 e5 ta-pou-gin2-a2, ia7 thai5-si2 hiah e5 i2-keng kap ta-pou-lang5 tang5-pang5 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5.  18). Chong2-si7 hiah e5 be7 kap ta-pou-lang5 tang5-pang5 e5 cha-bou2-gin2-a2, lin2 thang ui7 ka-ki7 lau5 in e5 oah8-mia7.  19). Lin2 tioh8 chat-iaN5 ti7 iaN5-goa7 chhit-jit8 ku2; kiN3-na7 thai5 lang5 e5, kiN3-na7 bong-tioh8 siu7-thai5-e5, tioh8 ti7 te7-saN jit8, te7-chhit jit8 chheng-khi3 ka-ki7, ia7 tioh8 chheng-khi3 lin2 sou2 liah8--lai5 e5 lang5.  20). Lun7-kau3 sou2 u7 e5 i-hok8, a2-si7 phe5-choe3-e5, a2-si7 soaN-iuN5-mng5 chit-e5, a2-si7 chha5-choe3 e5 mih8, long2 tioh8 chheng-khi3 i.  21). Che3-si I2-li7-a-sat tui3 kau-chian3 to3-lai5 e5 kun-tui7 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beng7-leng7 Mou5-se lut8-hoat e5 tiau5-le7 chiu7-si7 an2-ni;  22). chong2-si7 kim, gun5, tang5, thih, siah, ian5,  23). kiN3-na7 oe7 tong3-tit he2 e5 mih8, lin2 tioh8 hou7 i keng-ke3 he2, chiu7 chiaN5-choe3 chheng-khi3; chong2-si7 tioh8 koh eng7 tu5-khi3 u3-oe3 e5 chui2 chheng-khi3 i; kiN3-na7 boe7 tong3-tit he2 e5 mih8, lin2 tioh8 hou7 i keng-ke3 chui2.  24). Te7-chhit jit8 tioh8 soe2 lin2 e5 saN, lin2 chiu7 chheng-khi3; chiah thang jip8 iaN5.
	25). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  26). Li2 kap che3-si I2-li7-a-sat, kap hoe7-chiong3 chiah e5 chok8-tiuN2, tioh8 sng3 sou2 chhiuN2-liah8-e5, bo5-lun7 lang5 kap cheng-siN e5 siau3-giah8.  27). Sou2 chhiuN2-lai5-e5 tioh8 pun choe3 nng7-hun7, chit8-hun7 hou7 chhut-khi3 kau-chian3 e5 cheng-peng, chit8-hun7 hou7 choan5-hoe7 e5 cheng3-lang5.  28).
