Tioh8 tui3 chhut-chian3 e5 peng-teng thiu-mih8 lai5 chin3-kong3 Ia5-ho5-hoa; kiN3-na7 lang5, gu5, lu5, iuN5-kun5, mui2 gou7-pah thiu chit8.  29). Tui3 in hit-poaN3 e5 tiong-kan, tioh8 thiu-chhut--i lai5 hou7 che3-si I2-li7-a-sat, choe3 ku2-che3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  30). Tui3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 hi2 chit8-poaN3 e5 tiong-kan, chiu7-si7 tui3 lang5, gu5, lu5, iuN5-kun5, long2-chong2 e5 cheng-siN, mui2 gou7-chap8 thiu chit8, kau-hou7 kou3-siu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa hoe7-bou7 e5 chek-seng5 e5 Li7-bi7 lang5.  31). Mou5-se chiu7 kap che3-si I2-li7-a-sat, chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beng7-leng7 Mou5-se e5 lai5 kiaN5.  32). Sou2 chhiuN2 e5 mih8, chiu7-si7 peng-teng sou2 chhiuN2 eng7-chhun-e5, iuN5, lak8-chap8-chhit ban7 gou7-chheng chiah;  33). gu5, chhit-ban7 nng7-chheng chiah;  34). lu5, lak8-ban7 chit8-chheng chiah;  35). lang5, saN-ban7 nng7-chheng, chiu7-si7 m7-bat kap ta-pou-lang5 tang5-pang5 e5 cha-bou2-gin2-a2.  36). Chhut-khi3 kau-chian3 e5 lang5 e5 hun7-giah8, chiu7-si7 in sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 hit-poaN3, kiong7 u7 iuN5, saN-chap8-saN ban7 chhit-chheng gou7-pah chiah.  37). Tui3 in tiong-kan thiu lai5 chin3-kong3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 iuN5, lak8-pah chhit-chap8-gou7 chiah.  38). Gu5, saN-ban7 lak8-chheng chiah; tui3 in tiong-kan thiu lai5 chin3-kong3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5, chhit-chap8-ji7 chiah.  39). Lu5, saN-ban7 lian5 gou7-pah chiah; tui3 hit tiong-kan thiu lai5 chin3-kong3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5, si7 lak8-chap8-it chiah.  40). Lang5 chit8-ban7 lak8-chheng; tui3 hit tiong-kan thiu lai5 chin3-kong3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5, si7 saN-chap8-ji7 e5.  41). Mou5-se chiong chin3-kong3 e5 mih8, chiu7-si7 kui hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 ku2-che3, kau hou7 che3-si I2-li7-a-sat; si7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beng7-leng7 Mou5-se e5.
	42). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 sou2 tit-tioh8 hit-chit8-poaN3, chiu7-si7 Mou5-se tui3 kau-chian3 e5 lang5 pun lai5 hou7 in e5,  43). (hoe7-chiong3 hit-chit8-poaN3 u7 iuN5, saN-chap8-saN ban7 chhit-chheng gou7-pah chiah;  44). gu5, saN-ban7 lak8-chheng chiah;  45). lu5, saN-ban7 lian5 gou7-pah chiah;  46). lang5, chit8-ban7 lak8-chheng e5,)  47). tui3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 chit8-poaN3, bo5-lun7 si7 lang5, si7 cheng-siN, Mou5-se mui2 gou7-chap8 thiu chit8, kau-hou7 kou3-siu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa hoe7-bou7 e5 chek-seng5 e5 Li7-bi7 lang5; si7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beng7-leng7 Mou5-se e5.  48). Koan2-li2 kun-tui7 chiah e5 koaN, chiu7-si7 chhian-chong2 peh-chong2, long2 lai5 chiu7-kun7 Mou5-se,  49). tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Lou5-pok8 sou2 koan2 e5 peng, i2-keng tiam2-sng3 chong2-giah8, goan2 tiong-kan bo5 kiam2-chio2 chit8-lang5.  50). TaN goan2 chiong tak8-lang5 sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 kim-khi3, lian7-a2, chhiu2-khoan5, phah in3-a2 e5 chhiu2-chi2, hi7-kau, koa3 am7-kun2 e5 chu-lian7-a2, long2 toa3-lai5 choe3 le2-mih8 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, thang ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, ui7-tioh8 goan2 pun2-sin siok8-choe7.  51). Mou5-se kap che3-si I2-li7-a-sat, chiu7 siu in e5 kim, chiu7-si7 tak8-iuN7 phah ho2 e5 chhiu2-sek.  52). Chhian-chong2 peh-chong2 sou2 hian3-hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 kim, kiong7 u7 chit8-ban7 lak8-chheng chhit-pah gou7-chap8 sia3-khek-lek8.  53). In-ui7 tak8 e5 peng-teng long2 u7 ui7-tioh8 ka-ki7 chhiuN2 chai5-but8.  54). Mou5-se kap che3-si I2-li7-a-sat siu chhian-chong2 peh-chong2 e5 kim, chiu7 toa3-jip8 hoe7-bou7, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 choe3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 ki3-liam7.

[32]	Liu5-pian7 e5 kiaN2-sun, kap Ka-tek e5 kiaN2-sun, in e5 cheng-siN kek8-ki5 choe7; in khoaN3-kiN3 Nga2-sia7 e5 toe7, kap Ki-liat8 e5 toe7, si7 thang chhi7 cheng-siN e5 sou2-chai7.  2). Ka-tek e5 kiaN2-sun, kap Liu5-pian7 e5 kiaN2-sun, chiu7 lai5 kiN3 Mou5-se, kap che3-si I2-li7-a-sat, i2-kip8 hoe7-chiong3 e5 siu2-leng2, ka7 in kong2,  3). A-tai7-liok8, Ti2-pun2, Nga2-sia7, Leng5-lah8, Hi-sit8-pun2, I2-li7-a-li7, Si7-pan, Ni5-pho, Pi2-un2,  4). chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 I2-sek-liat8 hoe7-chiong3 e5 bin7-cheng5 sou2 kong-chhu2 e5 toe7, si7 thang chhi7 cheng-siN e5 toe7, li2 e5 lou5-pok8 ia7 u7 cheng-siN.  5). Koh kong2, Goan2 na7 tit-tioh8 un-tian2 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5, kiu5 li2 eng7 chit e5 toe7 hou7 li2 e5 lou5-pok8 choe3-giap8, boh8-tit chhoa7 goan2 ke3 Iok-tan3 ho5.  6). Mou5-se tui3 Ka-tek e5 kiaN2-sun kap Liu5-pian7 e5 kiaN2-sun kong2, Chong2 bo5 lin2 e5 hiaN-ti7 khi3 cheng-chian3, ia7 lin2 che7 ti7-chia mah?  7). Lin2 siaN2-su7 hou7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 loe2-chi3, bo5 ai3 ke3-khi3 jip8 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 siuN2-su3 in hit e5 toe7 ah?  8). Goa2 cheng5 tui3 Ka-te-su Pa-ni5-a chhe lin2 e5 lau7-pe7 khi3 thau-khoaN3 hit e5 toe7, in ia7 si7 an2-ni kiaN5.  9). In-ui7 in chiuN7-khi3 I2-sit8-kok e5 soaN-kok, khi3 khoaN3 hit e5 toe7 e5 si5, u7 hou7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 loe2-chi3, m7 ai3 jip8 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 siuN2-su3 in e5 toe7.  10). Tng-jit8 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 siu7-khi3 hoat-chhut, chiu7 chiu3-choa7 kong2,  11). KiN3-na7 tui3 Ai-kip8 chiuN7-lai5 ji7-chap8 he3 i2-siong7 e5 lang5, koat-toan3 boe7 tit-tioh8 khoaN3-kiN3 Goa2 tui3 A-pek-lah8-han2, I2-sat, Nga2-kok, chiu3-choa7 eng3-un2 e5 toe7; in-ui7 in bo5 choan-sim kun-te3 Goa2.  12). Tok8-tok8 Ki-ni5-se2 chok8, Ia5-hu-ni5 e5 kiaN2 Ka-lek8, kap Lun3 e5 kiaN2 Iok-su-a, thang khoaN3-kiN3, in-ui7 in choan-sim te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  13). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 hoat siu7-khi3, hou7 in ti7 khong3-ia2 phiau-liu5 si3-chap8 ni5, theng3-hau7 hit-tai7 kiaN5-phaiN2 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa bin7-cheng5 e5 lang5 long2 siau-biat8.  14). KhoaN3 ah, lin2 khi2-lai5 soa3-chiap lin2 e5 lau7-pe7, ke-thiN choe7-jin5 e5 siau3-giah8, hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa it-hoat siu7-khi3 I2-sek-liat8.  15). Lin2 na7 oat-to3-tng2 bo5 te3 I, I beh koh pang3-sak in ti7 khong3-ia2, lin2 chiu7-si7 biat8-bo5 chiah e5 cheng3 peh-siN3.
	16). In oa2-kun7 Mou5-se kong2, Goan2 beh ti7-chia ui7 goan2 e5 cheng-siN chhong3 tiau5, ui7 goan2 e5 gin2-a2 khi2 siaN5;  17). chong2-si7 goan2 pun2-sin beh toa3 kun-khi3, kiaN5 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 thau5-cheng5, theng3-hau7 goan2 chhoa7 in kau3 in e5 toe7-hng; tok8-tok8 goan2 e5 gin2-na2, in-ui7 chit e5 toe7 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 e5 ian5-kou3, beh tiam3 ti7 kian-kou3 e5 siaN5-lai7.  18). Goan2 m7 to3--khi3 goan2 chhu3, theng3-hau7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tak8-e5 tit-tioh8 i e5 giap8.  19). Goan2 bo5 beh kap in ti7 Iok-tan3 ho5 hit-peng5 koh khi3 e5 toe7 tit-tioh8 giap8; in-ui7 goan2 e5 giap8 si7 chai7 ti7 Iok-tan3 ho5 tang--si3 chit-peng5.
	20). Mou5-se tui3 in kong2, Lin2 na7 beh an2-ni kiaN5, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 toa3 kun-khi3 chhut-khi3 kau-chian3;  21). lin2 sou2 u7 toa3 kun-khi3 e5 lang5, na7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 ke3 Iok-tan3 ho5, theng3-hau7 I tui3 I e5 bin7-cheng5 koaN2-chhut I e5 tui3-tek8;  22). hit e5 toe7 i2-keng hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa khah-iaN5, jian5-au7 lin2 thang to3--lai5; ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kap I2-sek-liat8 e5 bin7-cheng5, lin2 chiu7 bo5 choe7, chit e5 toe7 beh ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 hou7 lin2 choe3-giap8.  23). Siat-su2 lin2 bo5 an2-ni kiaN5, chiu7-si7 tek-choe7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, tioh8 chai lin2 e5 choe7 beh tui-jip lin2.  24). TaN tioh8 ka7 lin2 e5 gin2-na2 khi2 siaN5, ka7 lin2 e5 iuN5-kun5 chhong3 tiau5, chiau3 lin2 e5 chhui3 sou2 kong2 e5, khi3 kiaN5.
	25). Ka-tek e5 kiaN2-sun kap Liu5-pian7 e5 kiaN2-sun tui3 Mou5-se kong2, Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 beh chiau3 goa2 e5 chu2 sou2 hoan-hu3-e5 khi3 kiaN5.  26). Goan2 e5 gin2-a2, goan2 e5 bou2, goan2 e5 iuN5-kun5, goan2 e5 cheng-siN, long2 beh lau5 ti7 Ki-liat8 chiah e5 siaN5.  27). Chong2-si7 li2 e5 lou5-pok8, kiN3-na7 toa3 kun-khi3 e5, long2 beh chiau3 goa2 e5 chu2 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 ke3-khi3 kau-chian3.
	28). Mou5-se chiu7 ui7-tioh8 in hoan-hu3 che3-si I2-li7-a-sat, kap Lun3 e5 kiaN2 Iok-su-a, kap I2-sek-liat8 cheng3 chi-phai3 e5 chok8-tiuN2.  29). Mou5-se tui3 in kong2, Ka-tek e5 kiaN2-sun kap Liu5-pian7 e5 kiaN2-sun, na7 kap lin2 ke3 Iok-tan3 ho5, tak8-lang5 kiah8 ke-si ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 khi3 kau-chian3, hit e5 toe7 hou7 lin2 khah-iaN5, lin2 chiu7 tioh8 eng7 Ki-liat8 toe7 hou7 in choe3 giap8.  30). Siat-su2 in m7 toa3 kun-khi3 kap lin2 ke3-khi3, in chiu7 ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7 tui3 lin2 tiong-kan tit-tioh8 giap8.  31). Ka-tek e5 kiaN2-sun kap Liu5-pian7 e5 kiaN2-sun in3 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 goan2 sou2 kong2-e5, Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 chiu7 an2-ni kiaN5.  32). Goan2 beh toa3 kun-khi3, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 ke3-khi3 jip8 Ka-lam5 toe7; tok8-tok8 Iok-tan3 ho5-goa7, goan2 sou2 tit-tioh8 choe3 giap8 e5 toe7, iu5-goan5 kui goan2.  33). Mou5-se chiu7 eng7 A-mou5-li7 ong5 Se-hong5 e5 kok, kap Pa-san ong5 Gok8 e5 kok, hit e5 toe7 kap i keng2-lai7 chiah e5 siaN5, chiu7-si7 si3-chiu-ui5 chiah e5 siaN5, long2 hou7 Ka-tek e5 kiaN2-sun, kap Liu5-pian7 e5 kiaN2-sun, i2-kip8 Iok-sek e5 kiaN2 Ma2-na2-se e5 poaN3-chi-phai3.  34). Ka-tek e5 kiaN2-sun khi2 Ti2-pun2, A-tha-liok8, A-lo5-jiN2,  35). A-tha-liok8-sok-hoan2, Nga2-sia7, Iok-pi2-hap,  36). Pek-leng5-lah8, Pek-hap-lan5; long2 si7 kian-kou3 e5 siaN5; in koh khi2 iuN5-tiau5.  37). Liu5-pian7 e5 kiaN2-sun khi2 Hi-sit8-pun2, I2-li7-a-li7, Ki-liat8-teng5,  38). Ni5-phou, Pa-lek8-bian2, (i2-keng oaN7 in e5 mia5,) koh khi2 Se-pi2-ma2; in sou2 khi2 chiah e5 siaN5 eng7 sin e5 mia5 ho7 i.  39). Ma2-na2-se e5 kiaN2 Ma2-kiat, i e5 kiaN2-sun khi3 Ki-liat8, chiam3 hit e5 toe7, koaN2-chhut hit sou2-chai7 e5 A-mou5-li7 lang5.  40). Mou5-se chiong Ki-liat8 hou7 Ma2-na2-se e5 kiaN2 Ma2-kiat; i chiu7 khia7 ti7-hia.  41). Ma2-na2-se e5 kiaN2 Gai7-jiN2 khi3 chiam3 hiah e5 hiuN-sia7, chiu7 chheng i choe3 Hap-ui2-tek8-gai7-jiN2.  42). Lo5-pa khi3 chiam3 Ki-lap8, kap Ki-lap8 chiah e5 hiuN-sia7; chiu7 chiau3 ka-ki7 e5 mia5 chheng i choe3 Lo5-pa.

[33]	I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chiau3 kun-tui7, ti7 Mou5-se A-lun5 e5 chhiu2-e7, chhut Ai-kip8 toe7 sou2 kiaN5 e5 lou7-cham7, ki3 ti7 e7-bin7.  2). Mou5-se chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 beng7-leng7 ki3-chai3 in khi2-sin kiaN5 e5 lou7-cham7; in khi2-sin kiaN5 e5 lou7-cham7 chiu7-si7 an2-ni.  3). ChiaN-geh8-kan, ti7 chiaN-geh8 chap8-gou7 jit8, chiu7-si7 poaN5-ke3-choeh e5 te7-ji7 jit8, I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tui3 Lan5-sek khi2-sin, ti7 Ai-kip8 cheng3-lang5 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5 , kho3 toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 chhiu2 chhut-khi3.  4). Hit-si5 Ai-kip8 lang5 teh bai5-chong3 in long2-chong2 e5 toa7-kiaN2, chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 in tiong-kan sou2 phah-si2--e5; Ia5-ho5-hoa ia7 khian3-chek in hiah e5 siong7-te3.  5). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tui3 Lan5-sek khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Sou-kat.  6). Tui3 Sou-kat khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 kun7 khong3-ia2 e5 I2-thong2.  7). Tui3 I2-thong2 khi2-sin, oat8-tng2 kau3 Pi2-hap-hi-liok8, chiu7-si7 ti7 Pa-lek8-se2-hun e5 tui3-bin7, chiu7 chat-iaN5 ti7 Bit8-toat8 e5 thau5-cheng5.  8). Tui3 Hap-hi-liok8 tui3-bin7 khi2-sin, keng-ke3 hai2-tiong kau3 khong3-ia2; koh ti7 I2-thong2 e5 khong3-ia2 kiaN5 saN-jit8 e5 lou7-cham7, chiu7 chat-iaN5 ti7 Ma2-lah8.  9). In tui3 Ma2-lah8 khi2-sin, lai5 kau3 I2-lim5; I2-lim5 u7 chap8-ji7 tiau5 chui2-choaN5, chhit-chap8 chang5 cho2-chhiu7; chiu7 ti7-hia chat-iaN5.  10). Tui3 I2-lim5 khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Ang5-hai2 kiN5.  11). Tui3 Ang5-hai2 kiN5 khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Sin3 e5 khong3-ia2.  12). Tui3 Sin3 e5 khong3-ia2 khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Thoat-ka.  13). Tui3 Thoat-ka khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 A-liok8.  14). Tui3 A-liok8 khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Li7-hui-teng3; ti7-hia bo5 chui2 thang hou7 peh-siN3 lim.  15). Tui3 Li7-hui-teng3 khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Se-nai2 e5 khong3-ia2.  16). Tui3 Se-nai2 e5 khong3-ia2 khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Ki-phok-lo5-hap-tha-oa2.  17). Tui3 Ki-phok-lo5-hap-tha-oa2 khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Hap-se2-liok8.  18). tui3 Hap-se2-liok8 khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Li7-the5-ma2.  19). Tui3 Li7-the5-ma2 khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Lim5-bun5-phaN3-liat8.  20). Tui3 Lim5-bun5-phaN3-liat8 khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Lip8-na2.  21). Tui3 Lip8-na2 khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Lek8-sat.  22). Tui3 Lek8-sat khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Ki-hi-lah8-tha.  23). Tui3 Ki-hi-lah8-tha khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Sa-hui2 soaN.  24). Tui3 Sa-hui2 soaN khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Hap-lah8-tai7.  25). Tui3 Hap-lah8-tai7 khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Ma2-kiat-hi-liok8.  26). Tui3 Ma2-kiat-hi-liok8 khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Tha-hap.  27). Tui3 Tha-hap khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Tha-lah8.  28). Tui3 Tha-lah8 khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Bit8-ka.  29). Tui3 Bit8-ka khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Hap-mou5-na2.  30). Tui3 Hap-mou5-na2 khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Mou5-se-liok8.  31). Tui3 Mou5-se-liok8 khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Pi2-ni5-a-kan.  32). Tui3 Pi2-ni5-a-kan khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Hat-hap-kip8-kah.  33). Tui3 Hat-hap-kip8-kah khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Iok-pa-tha.  34). Tui3 Iok-pa-tha khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 A-phok-na2.  35). Tui3 A-phok-na2 khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 I2-sun5-ka-piat8.  36). Tui3 I2-sun5-ka-piat8 khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Sim5 e5 khong3-ia2, chiu7-si7 Ka-te-su.  37). Tui3 Ka-te-su khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Ho5-jiN2 soaN, I2-tong toe7 e5 piN-kai3.
	38). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chhut Ai-kip8 toe7 e5 si3-chap8 ni5, gou7-geh8 chhoe-it jit8, che3-si A-lun5 chun-than3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 beng7-leng7, chiuN7 Ho5-jiN2 soaN, chiu7 si2 ti7-hia.  39). A-lun5 si2 ti7 Ho5-jiN2 soaN e5 si5, chit8-pah ji7-chap8-saN he3.
	40). Khia7-khi2 ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7 lam5-hng e5 Ka-lam5 lang5 A-lah8-tek ong5 thiaN-kiN3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 lai5 lah.
	41). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tui3 Ho5-jiN2 soaN khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Sat-mou5-na2.  42). Tui3 Sat-mou5-na2 khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Phou2-lun3.  43). Tui3 Phou2-lun3 khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 O-pek.  44). Tui3 O-pek khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 I2-ia5-a-pa-lim5, Mou5-ap e5 piN-kai3.  45). Tui3 I2-in3 khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Ti2-pun2-ka-tek.  46). Tui3 Ti2-pun2-ka-tek khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 A-bun5-te-pi2-lah8-thai3-im.  47). Tui3 A-bun5-te-pi2-lah8-thai3-im khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Ni5-pho tui3-bin7 e5 A-pa-lim5 soaN.  48). Tui3 A-pa-lim5 soaN khi2-sin, chat-iaN5 ti7 Mou5-ap e5 piN5-iuN5, Iok-tan3 ho5-piN, Ia5-li7-ko tui3-bin7.  49). In chat-iaN5 ti7 Iok-tan3 e5 ho5-piN, tui3 Pek-ia5-se-boat8 kau3 A-pek-sip8-teng5, ti7 Mou5-ap piN5-iuN5.
	50). Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 Mou5-ap piN5-iuN5, Iok-tan3 ho5-piN, Ia5-li7-ko tui3-bin7, hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  51). Li2 tioh8 hoan-hu3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 ka7 in kong2, Lin2 ke3 Iok-tan3 ho5 jip8 Ka-lam5 toe7 e5 si5,  52). chiu7 tioh8 tui3 lin2 bin7-cheng5 koaN2-chhut hia sou2 u7 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3, hui2-biat8 in it-chhe3 phah-chiaN5 e5 chioh8-siong7, koh hui2-biat8 in it-chhe3 iuN5-chu3 e5 ngou2-siong7, koh thiah-hui2 in it-chhe3 e5 soaN-thau5-toaN5.  53). Lin2 tioh8 chiam3 hit sou2-chai7, ia7 tioh8 khia7-khi2 ti7-hia, in-ui7 Goa2 chiong hit sou2-chai7 siuN2-su3 lin2 choe3-giap8.  54). Lin2 tioh8 chiau3 tak8-ke liam-khau seng5-chiap hit e5 toe7; lang5 choe7-e5, tioh8 pun san2-giap8 khah-choe7 hou7 in, lang5 chio2-e5 tioh8 pun san2-giap8 khah-chio2 hou7 in; khoaN3 lang5 liam-tioh8 sim2-mih8 sou2-chai7, hit sou2-chai7 chiu7 kui i; chiau3 lin2 chou2-kong e5 chi-phai3 lin2 tioh8 seng5-chiap i.  55). Siat-su2 lin2 bo5 koaN2-chhut hit sou2-chai7 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3, chiu7 lin2 sou2 iong5-un2 i tiam3-teh e5 peh-siN3, beh choe3 lin2 bak8-chiu-tiong e5 chhi3, hiap8-e7 e5 chhau2-chhi3; in ia7 beh ti7 lin2 sou2 khia7-khi2 e5 toe7 khun2-pek lin2.  56). Koh Goa2 beh khoan2-thai7 lin2, chhin-chhiuN7 Goa2 bat siuN7 beh khoan2-thai7 in e5.

[34]	Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  2). Li2 tioh8 beng7-leng7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 ka7 in kong2, Lin2 kau3 Ka-lam5 toe7 e5 si5, chiu7-si7 kui hou7 lin2 choe3-giap8 e5 Ka-lam5, chiau3 i si3-keng2 e5 toe7;  3). lin2 e5 lam5-hng tioh8 tui3 Sim5 e5 khong3-ia2 ian5 I2-tong e5 piN-kai3, lin2 e5 lam5-kai3 tioh8 tui3 Iam5-hai2 tang--si3 e5 kek8-thau5.  4). Lin2 e5 kai3 tioh8 kau3 A-khek-lah8-piN e5 soaN-phiaN5 e5 lam5--si3, soa3-kau3 Sim5, tit8-tit8 thang3-kau3 Ka-te-su-pa-ni5-a e5 lam5-peng5; koh thang3-kau3 Hap-sat-a-tat8, soa3-kau3 Ap-bun5.  5). Chit e5 keng2-kai3 tioh8 tui3 Ap-bun5 oat-kau3 Ai-kip8 e5 khoe, thang3-kau3 hai2 ui5-chi2.  6). Sai-peng5 tioh8 eng7 toa7-hai2 choe3 kai3; che chiu7-si7 lin2 sai--si3 e5 kai3.  7). Lin2 pak--si3 e5 kai3 tioh8 tui3 toa7-hai2, uih8-kau3 Ho5-jiN2 soaN.  8). Tui3 Ho5-jiN2 soaN uih8-kau3 Hap-ma2 e5 lou7-khau2, thang3-kau3 Se-tat8-tat8.  9). Koh thang3-kau3 Se-hui2-lun5, tit8-kau3 Hap-sat-i2-lan5 ui5-chi2, che beh choe3 lin2 pak--si3 e5 kai3.  10). Lin2 tioh8 tui3 Hap-sat-i2-lan5, uih8-kau3 Si7-hoan choe3 lin2 tang--si3 e5 kai3.  11). Chit e5 kai3 tioh8 tui3 Si7-hoan loh8-khi3 kau3 A-ian5 tang--si3 e5 Li7-pi2-lah8, koh loh8-khi3 kau3 Ki-ni5-liat8 ou5 e5 tang--si3.  12). Chit e5 kai3 tioh8 loh8-khi3 kau3 Iok-tan3 ho5, thang3-kau3 Iam5-hai2 ui5-chi2; chit si3-ui5 e5 kai3-lai7 beh choe3 lin2 e5 toe7.
	13). Mou5-se beng7-leng7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kong2, Che si7 chiau3 lin2 sou2 liam-khau choe3 teh-beh soa3-chiap giap8 e5 toe7, Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beng7-leng7 hou7 kau2 e5 chi-phai3 koh poaN3-chi-phai3 e5.  14). In-ui7 Liu5-pian7 kiaN2-sun e5 chi-phai3 chiau3 in e5 chong-chok8, koh Ka-tek kiaN2-sun e5 chi-phai3 chiau3 in e5 chong-chok8, i2-keng tit-tioh8 san2-giap8; Ma2-na2-se poaN3-chi-phai3 ia7 tit-tioh8;  15). chi2 nng7 chi-phai3, koh poaN3-chi-phai3, i2-keng ti7 Iok-tan3 goa7, Ia5-li7-ko e5 tang--si3, ng3 jit8 chhut e5 sou2-chai7 tit-tioh8 giap8.
	16). Ia5-ho5-hoa koh hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  17). Beh ka7 lin2 pun toe7 choe3-giap8 e5 lang5 e5 mia5-ji7 ki3 ti7 e7-toe2; si7 che3-si I2-li7-a-sat, kap Lun3 e5 kiaN2 Iok-su-a.  18). Lin2 tioh8 tui3 tak8 chi-phai3 keng2 chit e5 siu2-leng2, pun hit e5 toe7 choe3-giap8.  19). Chiah e5 lang5 e5 mia5 ki3 ti7 e7-toe2; Iu5-tai7 e5 chi-phai3, u7 Ia5-hu-ni5 e5 kiaN2 Ka-lek8.  20). Se-bian7 kiaN2-sun e5 chi-phai3, u7 A-bi2-hut e5 kiaN2 Si7-bou2-li7.  21). Pian7-nga2-bin2 e5 chi-phai3, u7 Ki-su-lun5 e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-tat8.  22). Tan3 e5 kiaN2-sun e5 chi-phai3, u7 siu2-leng2, Iok-li7 e5 kiaN2 Pou3-ki.  23). Iok-sek e5 kiaN2-sun, Ma2-na2-se kiaN2-sun e5 chi-phai3, u7 siu2-leng2, I2-hut e5 kiaN2 Han3-liap;  24). I2-hoat-lian5 kiaN2-sun e5 chi-phai3, u7 siu2-leng2, Lip8-hut-tan3 e5 kiaN2 Ki-bou2-li7.  25). Se-pou3-lun5 kiaN2-sun e5 chi-phai3, u7 siu2-leng2, PhaN3-lap8 e5 kiaN2 I-li7-sat-hoan.  26). I2-sat-ka kiaN2-sun e5 chi-phai3, u7 siu2-leng2, A-san3 e5 kiaN2 PhaN3-thiah.  27). A-siat kiaN2-sun e5 chi-phai3, u7 siu2-leng2, Si7-lo5-bi2 e5 kiaN2 A-hi-hut.  28). Na2-hut-tha-li7 kiaN2-sun e5 chi-phai3, u7 siu2-leng2, A-bi2-hut e5 kiaN2 Pi2-tai7-hek.  29). Chiah e5 lang5 chiu7-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beng7-leng7 ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7 chiong san2-giap8 pun hou7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5.

[35]	Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 Mou5-ap e5 piN5-iuN5, Iok-tan3 ho5-piN, Ia5-li7-ko tui3-bin7, hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  2). Li2 beng7-leng7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5, tioh8 tui3 in sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 giap8, eng7 siaN5 hou7 Li7-bi7 lang5 khia7-khi2; ia7 tioh8 eng7 siaN5 si3-ui5 e5 kau-ia2 hou7 Li7-bi7 lang5.  3). SiaN5 beh hou7 in khia7-khi2; kau-ia2 beh choe3 in e5 gu5, iuN5, chai5-but8, kap tak8-iuN7 cheng-siN e5 lou7-eng7.  4). Lin2 sou2 hou7 Li7-bi7 lang5 siaN5-goa7 e5 kau-ia2, tui3 siaN5-kha si3-ui5 niu5-chhut chit8-chheng tiu2.  5). Li2 ti7 siaN5-goa7 niu5 i, tang--si3 nng7-chheng tiu2, lam5--si3 nng7-chheng tiu2, sai-si3 nng7-chheng tiu2, pak--si3 nng7-chheng tiu2, siaN5 ti7 tiong-ng; che si7 beh hou7 in choe3 siaN5 e5 kau-ia2.  6). Lin2 sou2 hou7 Li7-bi7 lang5 hiah e5 siaN5, ki5-tiong tioh8 lak8 e5 to5-siam2 e5 siaN5; lin2 tioh8 siat-lip8 i, hou7 thai5-si2 lang5-e5 thang to5-chau2 ti7-hia; chiah-e5 i2-goa7, tioh8 koh hou7 in si3-chap8-ji7 e5 siaN5.  7). Lin2 tioh8 hou7 Li7-bi7 lang5 e5 siaN5, kiong7 si3-chap8-poeh; siaN5 kap kau-ia2, long2 tioh8 hou7 in.  8). Lun7-kau3 lin2 tui3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 san2-giap8-tiong, sou2 hou7 Li7-bi7 lang5 e5 siaN5, tui3 giap8 choe7-e5, chhu2 khah-choe7 siaN5, tui3 giap8 chio2-e5, chhu2 chio2; kok chiau3 sou2 seng5-chiap e5 giap8 poah-chhut siaN5 hou7 Li7-bi7 lang5.
	9). Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 Mou5-se kong2,  10). Li2 tioh8 hoan-hu3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5, ka7 in kong2, Lin2 ke3 Iok-tan3 ho5, jip8 Ka-lam5 toe7,  11). chiu7 tioh8 poah-chhut kui2 e5 siaN5, hou7 lin2 choe3 to5-siam2 e5 siaN5, hou7 chho3-gou7 thai5-si2 lang5 e5 hiong-sin thang to5-chau2 ti7-hia.  12). Chiah e5 siaN5 thang hou7 lin2 siam2-pi7 hit e5 po3-siu5 e5 lang5, hou7 hiong-sin bo5 ti3-kau3 si2; theng3-hau7 i khia7 ti7 hoe7-chiong3 e5 bin7-cheng5 siu7 sim2-phoaN3.  13). Lin2 sou2 poah--chhut-lai5 e5 siaN5, tioh8 choe3 lin2 lak8 e5 to5-siam2 e5 siaN5.  14). Ti7 Iok-tan3 ho5-goa7 tioh8 poah-chhut saN e5 siaN5, ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7 ia7 tioh8 poah-chhut saN e5 siaN5, choe3 to5-siam2 e5 siaN5.  15). Chi2 lak8 e5 siaN5 tioh8 hou7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5, kap in tiong-kan e5 chhut-goa7 lang5, kap kia3-kha-e5, choe3 to5-siam2 e5 lou7-eng7; hou7 chho3-gou7 thai5-lang5-e5 thang chau2-khi3 hia.  16). Siat-su2 lang5 eng7 thih-khi3 phah lang5, ti3-kau3 si2, i chiu7-si7 hiong-hoan7, hiong-hoan7 tek-khak tioh8 hou7 i si2.  17). I e5 chhiu2 na7 eng7 oe7 hou7 lang5 si2 e5 chioh8 tim3 lang5, ti3-kau3 lang5 si2, i chiu7-si7 hiong-hoan7, hiong-hoan7 tek-khak tioh8 si2.  18). I e5 chhiu2 na7 eng7 oe7 hou7 lang5 si2 e5 chha5 phah lang5, ti3-kau3 lang5 si2, i chiu7-si7 hiong-hoan7, hiong-hoan7 tek-khak tioh8 si2.  19). Po3 jin5-beng7--e5, pun2-sin tioh8 thai5-si2 hit e5 hiong-hoan7; chit8-e7 tu2-tioh8--i chiu7 tioh8 thai5 i.  20). Lang5 na7 oan3-hun7 hit-lang5 lai5 ka7 i chhia-to2, a2-si7 bih-teh eng7-mih8 tim3 i, ti3-kau3 si2;  21). khiam2-chhai2 in-ui7 hiap8-hun7 eng7 chhiu2 phah lang5 ti3-kau3 si2, chiu7 hit e5 phah-lang5-e5 tek-khak tioh8 si2, in-ui7 i chin-chiaN3 si7 hiong-hoan7, po3 jin5-beng7-e5 tu2-tioh8 hiong-hoan7, chiu7 thai5-si2 i.
	22). Siat-su2 lang5 bo5 hiap8-hun7, hut-jian5 chhia i, a2-si7 bo5 bih-teh, eng7 mih8 tim3 i;  23). a2-si7 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 si5, eng7 oe7-phah-si2 lang5 e5 chioh8-thau5 tim3-tioh8 i, lai5 ti3-kau3 si2, kap i pun2 bo5 oan-siu5, ia7 bo5 i3-su3 beh hai7 i,  24). hoe7-chiong3 chiu7 tioh8 chiau3 hiah e5 hoat-tou7, ti7 phah-si2-lang5-e5 kap po3 jin5-beng7--e5 e5 tiong-kan sim2-phoaN3 i.  25). Hoe7-chiong3 tioh8 kiu3 hit e5 chho3-gou7 thai5-lang5-e5 thoat-li7 po3 jin5-beng7--e5 e5 chhiu2; hoe7-chiong3 ia7 tioh8 hou7 i to3-tng2 i sou2 chau2-jip8 to5-siam2 e5 siaN5, i tioh8 tiam3 ti7 hi2 lai7-bin7, theng3-hau7 kau3 boah seng3-iu5 e5 che3-si-thau5 si2.  26). Chong2-si7 chho3-gou7 thai5-si2-lang5--e5, bo5-lun7 chaiN2-iuN7, na7 chhut-khi3 i sou2 chau2-jip8 to5-siam2 e5 siaN5 e5 keng2-goa7,  27). po3-jin5-beng7--e5 na7 ti7 to5-siam2 e5 siaN5 e5 keng2-goa7 tu2-tioh8 i, lai5 thai5-si2 hit e5 hiong-hoan7, po3-jin5-beng7--e5 chiu7 bo5 thai5-si2 lang5 e5 choe7.  28). In-ui7 i eng-kai tioh8 tiam3 i to5-siam2 e5 siaN5, theng3-hau7 che3-si-thau5 si2; che3-si-thau5 si2 liau2-au7, chho3-gou7 thai5-lang5-e5 chiah thang to3-khi3 i san2-giap8 e5 toe7.
	29). Che ti7 lin2 it-chhe3 khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7 beh choe3 lin2 tak8 se3-tai7 e5 hoat-lut8.  30). KiN3-na7 thai5-si2 lang5, hit e5 hiong-hoan7 tioh8 chiau3 kui2-na7 e5 kan-cheng3 e5 lang5 e5 oe7 lai5 hou7 i si2; na7 chi2-u7 chit8-lang5 choe3 kan-cheng3, chiu7 m7-thang hou7 lang5 si2.  31). Thai5-si2-lang5 hoan7-tioh8 si2-choe7 e5, lin2 m7-thang siu siok8-hoe5 siN3-mia7 e5 ke3-chiN5; tek-khak tioh8 hou7 i si2.  32). Hit e5 chau2 kau3 to5-siam2 e5 siaN5 e5 lang5, lin2 m7-thang ka7 i theh8 siok8-hoe5 e5 ke3, hou7 i ti7 che3-si be7 si2 e5 tai7-seng, koh lai5 tiam3 pun2-toe7.  33). An2-ni, lin2 chiu7 bo5 phah la5-sam5 lin2 sou2 khia7-khi2 e5 toe7; in-ui7 huih si7 phah la5-sam5 toe7 e5; na7 u7 huih lau5 ti7 toe7--nih, siat-su2 m7-si7 lau5 hit e5 thai5-lang5-e5 e5 huih, hit e5 toe7 chiu7 boe7 tit-tioh8 chheng-khi3.  34). Lin2 m7-thang phah la5-sam5 lin2 sou2 tiam3 e5 toe7, chiu7-si7 Goa2 tiam3 ti7 hit tiong-kan e5 toe7; in-ui7 Goa2 Ia5-ho5-hoa tiam3 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 tiong-kan.

[36]	Siok8 Iok-sek e5 kiaN2-sun chiah e5 ke, Ma2-na2-se e5 sun, Ma2-kiat e5 kiaN2 Ki-liat8 e5 kiaN2-sun hiah e5 chok8-tiuN2 lai5 kau3 Mou5-se kap I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chiah e5 chok8-tiuN2 chiah e5 siu2-leng2 e5 bin7-cheng5, kong2,  2). Ia5-ho5-hoa bat beng7-leng7 goa2 e5 chu2 liam-khau pun-toe7 hou7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 choe3-giap8, goa2 e5 chu2 ia7 siu7-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 beng7-leng7, chiong goan2 e5 hiaN-ti7 Se-lo5-hui-hap e5 san2-giap8 pun hou7 i hiah e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2.  3). In na7 ke3 I2-sek-liat8 pat8 chi-phai3 e5 lang5, in e5 san2-giap8 chiu7 tui3 goan2 chou2-kong sou2 lau5 e5 san2-giap8 poah-ke3-khi3, ke-thiN ti7 in sou2 beh siok8 e5 chi-phai3 e5 san2-giap8; an2-ni chiu7 tui3 goan2 liam-khau sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 giap8 poah-ke3-khi3.  4). Kau3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 hi-lian5, in e5 san2-giap8 chiu7 ke-thiN ti7 in sou2 beh siok8 e5 chi-phai3 e5 san2-giap8; an2-ni, in e5 san2-giap8 chiu7-si7 tui3 goan2 chou2-kong chi-phai3 e5 san2-giap8 poah-ke3-khi3.  5). Mou5-se chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7, beng7-leng7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kong2, Iok-sek kiaN2-sun e5 chi-phai3 sou2-kong2-e5 si7 tioh8.  6). Lun7-kau3 Se-lo5-hui-hap chiah e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni beng7-leng7, kong2, In thang ke3 in kah-i3 e5 lang5, tok8-tok8 tioh8 ke3 hou7 in lau7-pe7 tang5-chong chi-phai3 e5 lang5.  7). An2-ni, I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 san2-giap8 chiu7 bo5 tui3 chit chi-phai3 kui kau3 hit chi-phai3; in-ui7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tioh8 tak8-e5 chip-siu2 in chou2-kong chi-phai3 e5 san2-giap8.  8). KiN3-na7 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 chi-phai3 tiong tit-tioh8 san2-giap8 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, tioh8 choe3 i e5 lau7-pe7 tang5-chong chi-phai3 e5 lang5 e5 bou2, thang hou7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 chi-phai3 tak8-e5 chip-siu2 in e5 chou2-kong e5 san2-giap8.  9). An2-ni, in e5 san2-giap8 chiu7 bo5 tui3 chit chi-phai3 kui kau3 hit chi-phai3; in-ui7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 chi-phai3, beh tak8-e5 chip-siu2 in e5 san2-giap8.  10). Ia5-ho5-hoa an2-ni hoan-hu3 Mou5-se, Se-lo5-hui-hap e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 chiu7 an2-ni kiaN5.  11). In-ui7 Se-lo5-hui-hap e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, Ma2-lah8, Tek-sat, Hat-lah8, Bit8-ka, Na2-a, long2 ke3 in e5 chek-peh e5 kiaN2.  12). In ke3 ti7 Iok-sek e5 kiaN2, Ma2-na2-se kiaN2-sun hiah e5 ke; chiu7 in e5 san2-giap8 iu5-goan5 lau5 ti7 in lau7-pe7 e5 ke e5 chi-phai3.
	13). Chiah-e5 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 Mou5-ap piN5-iuN5, Iok-tan3 ho5-piN, Ia5-li7-ko tui3-bin7, thok Mou5-se sou2 hoan-hu3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 beng7-leng7, hoat-tou7.
